### [1] [Exposing impostor Majorana zero modes through atomic-scale shot-noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26002)
*A. Maiti,G. D. Gu,F. Massee*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文利用原子尺度散粒噪声谱（shot-noise spectroscopy）区分超导体Fe(Se,Te)中缺陷束缚的零偏压峰（zero-bias peak）是马约拉纳零模（Majorana zero mode）还是平庸束缚态（trivial bound states），实验证明散粒噪声可以揭示隐藏在隧穿电导中的粒子-空穴特征，从而排除虚假的马约拉纳信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在p波超导体中观测到的零偏压电导峰通常被视为马约拉纳零模的关键证据，但平庸束缚态也能产生类似特征，导致传统电导谱（conductance spectroscopy）作为诊断工具的可靠性受限。该问题长期存在，亟需一种能够区分真实与虚假马约拉纳信号的新方法。

Method: 采用原子尺度散粒噪声谱（atomic-scale shot-noise spectroscopy），对广泛研究的超导体Fe(Se,Te)中多个缺陷束缚的零偏压态进行详细分析。该方法超越常规电导测量，通过测量散粒噪声（shot noise）来揭示隧穿电导中隐藏的个体粒子与空穴特征（particle- and hole character）。

Result: 在Fe(Se,Te)中，差分电导（differential conductance）表现出看似“稳健”（robust）的零偏压峰，但散粒噪声测量一致地揭示了隧穿电导中隐藏的粒子-空穴特征指纹，明确暴露了该零偏压峰的平庸本质（trivial nature）。

Conclusion: 散粒噪声谱被确立为一种决定性诊断工具（decisive diagnostic），可用于在原子尺度实验中排除虚假的马约拉纳信号（false Majorana signatures）。

Abstract: A robust zero-bias conductance peak in putative $p$-wave superconductors is often regarded as the primary signature of a Majorana zero mode. Yet similar features can also arise from trivial bound states. This ambiguity has limited the reliability of conventional spectroscopy as a diagnostic tool, raising a long-standing problem of how to detect such impostors. Here, we address this issue with an alternative approach, atomic-scale shot-noise spectroscopy, that goes beyond conductance measurements. Through a detailed investigation of multiple defect-bound zero-bias states in the widely studied superconductor Fe(Se,Te), we observe that differential conductance can exhibit an apparently `robust' zero-bias peak. However, shot-noise measurements consistently reveal the fingerprint of the individual particle- and hole character hidden in the tunnelling conductance, unambiguously exposing the trivial nature of the zero-bias peak. Our results establish shot-noise spectroscopy as a decisive diagnostic for ruling out false Majorana signatures in atomic-scale experiments.

</details>


### [2] [From Wavefunction Collapse to Superconductivity: Evolution of the Electronic State in Compressed GaNb4Se8](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26203)
*Yuejian Wang,Zhongyan Wu,K C Bhupendra,Dongzhou Zhang,Lin Wang,Sanjay V. Khare,Lilian Prodan,Vladimir Tsurkan*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究通过压力依赖的输运测量，揭示了簇状Mott绝缘体GaNb4Se8中从局域化到巡游电子态的演化过程：低压力下为Efros-Shklovskii变程跳跃（受Coulomb能隙控制），约5 GPa开始向金属输运转变，约20 GPa发生晶体结构相变，显示出电子退局域化与结构对称性变化之间的解耦；高压下从关联金属态中出现超导电性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解关联簇状固体（correlated cluster solids）中电子输运从局域化（localized）到巡游（itinerant）行为的演化，是凝聚态物理学中的一个重要挑战。本研究旨在通过压力调控，探索簇状Mott绝缘体（cluster Mott insulator）GaNb4Se8的电子态转变机制。

Method: 对GaNb4Se8施加高压，测量其压力依赖的输运性质（pressure-dependent transport properties），分析电阻率随压力的变化行为以及晶体结构的变化。

Result: 低压力下电阻率符合Efros-Shklovskii变程跳跃（Efros-Shklovskii variable-range hopping），局域化长度x~6.1 Å，表明Coulomb能隙控制的载流子局域化。约5 GPa开始向金属输运交叉；而立方相到单斜C2相的晶体学转变发生在约20 GPa，表明电子退局域化与结构对称性变化解耦。高压下关联金属态中出现超导电性（superconductivity），相干长度xi(0)~80-90 Å。

Conclusion: GaNb4Se8被确立为一个研究基于簇的固体（cluster-based solids）中关联控制的输运演化的平台。电子退局域化与结构相变在压力尺度上的分离，揭示了关联效应在金属-绝缘体转变中的主导作用。

Abstract: Understanding how electronic transport evolves from localized to itinerant regimes in correlated cluster solids remains an important challenge in condensed-matter physics. Here we investigate the pressure-dependent transport properties of the lacunar spinel GaNb4Se8, a cluster Mott insulator at ambient conditions. At low pressures, the resistivity follows Efros-Shklovskii variable-range hopping, indicating Coulomb-gap-controlled carrier localization (x ~ 6.1 Angstrom). A crossover toward metallic transport begins near ~ 5 GPa, whereas a crystallographic transition from the cubic phase to a monoclinic C2 phase occurs at significantly higher pressure (~ 20 GPa), establishing a hierarchy characterized by the decoupling of electronic delocalization from structural symmetry change. At higher pressures, superconductivity (xi(0) ~ 80-90 Angstrom) emerges from the correlated metallic regime. These results identify GaNb4Se8 as a platform for studying correlation-controlled transport evolution in cluster-based solids.

</details>


### [3] [Programmable superconducting diode from nematic domain control in FeS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26631)
*R. D. H. Hinlopen,C. Putzke,L. Holeschovsky,R. Nicholls,F. Ronning,E. D. Bauer,N. E. Hussey,P. J. W. Moll*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究展示了一种可编程超导二极管（superconducting diode），其功能由关联电子畴（correlated electronic domains）而非样品几何结构编码。利用向列超导体FeSe，实现了高达约75%的大规模本征超导二极管效应（SDE），并通过微秒级强电流脉冲调控向列畴（nematic domain）图案，从而控制SDE的极性与强度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统超导二极管的反演不对称性（inversion asymmetry）依赖于样品几何或非中心对称晶体，导致其为静态电路元件。本研究旨在实现一种可编程超导二极管，其功能可通过关联电子态中畴图案的编程来动态调控。

Method: 采用向列超导体FeSe作为平台，利用涡旋（vortices）与向列孪晶界（nematic twin boundaries）的相互作用产生大本征SDE。通过强度超过10^7 K/s的微秒级电流脉冲猝灭向列序（quench the nematic order），以修改畴图案，从而控制SDE的极性与强度。

Result: 在FeSe中报告了效率高达约75%的大规模本征SDE，表明畴壁构型（domain wall configuration）编码了器件的SDE。通过微秒级强电流脉冲成功修改了向列畴图案，实现了对SDE极性与强度的控制。

Conclusion: 这些结果建立了一种新范式，即超导电路元件可通过向关联电子态中印刻图案（patterns imprinted into correlated electronic states）进行编程，为可重构超导电子学（reconfigurable superconducting electronics）提供了可能。

Abstract: The superconducting diode effect (SDE) allows polarity-dependent critical currents when time-reversal and current-inverting spatial symmetries are broken. Superconducting diodes show promise for applications, but inversion asymmetry is usually encoded in sample geometry or non-centrosymmetric crystals, rendering them static circuit elements. Here we demonstrate a programmable superconducting diode whose functionality is encoded in correlated electronic domains. We use the nematic superconductor FeSe as a platform and report a large intrinsic SDE with efficiencies up to $η\sim 75\%$ due to vortices interacting with nematic twin boundaries. The domain wall configuration thus encodes the SDE of the device. Through intense microsecond current pulses to quench the nematic order at rates exceeding $10^7$~K/s, we modify the domain pattern and control the polarity and strength of the SDE. These results establish a new paradigm in which superconducting circuit elements can be programmed through patterns imprinted into correlated electronic states.

</details>


### [4] [Negative nonlocal and local voltages (resistances) in a quasi-one-dimensional superconducting aluminum structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26814)
*V. I. Kuznetsov,O. V. Trofimov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 通过实验测量铝超导准一维结构中的非局域负直流电压，并结合平衡/非平衡超导涨落的理论模型，揭示了由准粒子流通过正常-超导界面产生的负电压现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究铝超导准一维结构在接近临界温度的磁场下的非局域电子输运（nonlocal electron transport）行为，特别是负非局域（负局域）直流电压的产生机制。

Method: 测量了由窄线和宽线构成的正常-超导（normal-superconducting）结构中的负非局域直流电压；对比实验与理论计算的温度及磁场依赖关系，分别考虑了平衡和非平衡超导涨落（superconducting fluctuations）。

Result: 实验与理论均观察到负电压峰值，且该电压的温度和磁场依赖关系可由考虑了超导涨落的模型描述。

Conclusion: 负电压源于准粒子流（quasiparticle current）穿过正常-超导界面，超导涨落（包括平衡与非平衡情形）对解释该输运现象至关重要。

Abstract: To study a nonlocal electron transport in an aluminum superconducting quasi-one-dimensional structure, we measured negative nonlocal (local) direct current voltages in the structure in a magnetic field near the critical temperature. The structure is a normal-superconducting at $T_{cn}<T<T_{cw}$ ($T_{cn}$ and $T_{cw}$ are the critical temperatures for narrow and wide wires, respectively, making up this structure). Negative voltage arises due to a quasiparticle current flowing through the N-S interface. We plotted the experimental and theoretical temperature and magnetic-field dependences of current, resistance and voltage corresponding to the peak of negative voltage, taking into account either equilibrium or nonequilibrium superconducting fluctuations.

</details>


### [5] [Engineering superconductivity on the surface of Weyl semimetals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26859)
*Riccardo Vocaturo,Mattia Trama*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出利用Weyl半金属表面Fermi弧的拓扑保护性质，通过沉积附加层诱导表面范霍夫奇点（van Hove singularities）来显著提升超导临界温度，并以PtBi₂为具体材料示例展示了实验可行的二维高温超导工程路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Weyl半金属中发现表面超导现象的十年后，理论和实验工作指向其可能实现相对高温的表面超导，但如何系统性地提高临界温度仍待解决。

Method: 以真实材料PtBi₂为驱动示例，通过在Weyl表面沉积合适的附加层来诱导表面范霍夫奇点，并分析化学势位于奇点附近时对临界温度的增强作用。

Result: 表面范霍夫奇点可被成功诱导，当化学势处于其附近时，超导临界温度显著提升；拓扑保护机制可用于操控表面电子态以实现高温超导。

Conclusion: 拓扑保护可被利用来调控表面电子态，从而开辟实验可行的路径来工程化高温二维超导及其他奇异相。

Abstract: Ten years after the experimental discovery of Weyl semimetals, theoretical and experimental work has pointed to the possibility of realizing surface-only superconductivity at relatively high temperatures in these materials. A consensus is developing that this unusual form of superconductivity is mediated by surface electronic states unique to Weyl semimetals, known as Fermi arcs. In this work, we show that the topological protection of these exotic states can be exploited to engineer high critical temperatures. Motivated by a real-material example (PtBi$_2$), we demonstrate that surface van Hove singularities can be induced by depositing a suitable additional layer on top of the Weyl surface. We also investigate the role of these singularities in raising the critical temperature, showing that it is significantly enhanced when the chemical potential lies in their vicinity. More generally, our results demonstrate how topological protection can be exploited to manipulate surface electronic states, thereby opening experimentally accessible routes toward engineering high-temperature two-dimensional superconductivity and other exotic phases.

</details>


### [6] [Non-local Tunneling Spectroscopy of Inelastic Quasiparticle Relaxation in Superconducting 1-D Wires](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26862)
*Kevin M. Ryan,Detlef Beckmann,Venkat Chandrasekhar*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文利用三端铜和铝的NIS器件，通过双偏压方案研究超导体中准粒子的非局域输运与能量失衡效应，观测到与破缺配对相关的非局域电导特征，并结合准经典模拟提取了能量依赖的非弹性散射时间，同时展示了超电流引起的动力学效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非局域电导实验能够提供超导体中准粒子输运和弛豫的光谱信息，但此前在超导相干长度尺度上对准粒子能量失衡（quasiparticle energy imbalance）及其对配对势（pair potential）影响的实验研究尚不充分。

Method: 采用介观三端Cu和Al的NIS（normal-insulator-superconductor）器件；利用双偏压方案（dual-bias scheme），使探测器偏压分别设置在超导能隙之上和之下，通过对称性分析从自洽配对势中提取准粒子能量失衡效应；并结合包含非弹性效应的准经典模拟（quasiclassical simulations）进行对比。

Result: 观测到因破缺配对（pair-breaking）导致的非局域电导特征，该特征对偏压极性呈反对称（anti-symmetric），且在能量约3Δ的单电子隧穿过程中出现尖锐的起始信号；通过模拟获得了能量依赖的非弹性散射时间（inelastic scattering time）估计值；同时展示了由大超电流引起的动力学效应，该效应可在粒子-空穴对称性与超电流方向下进行分解。

Conclusion: 双偏压方案结合准经典模拟能有效提取超导体中准粒子的能量失衡与非弹性散射信息，该方法可进一步推广以研究超电流等动力学效应，具备进一步发展的潜力。

Abstract: Non-local conductance experiments using tunnel junctions can provide valuable spectroscopic information on both the transport and relaxation of quasiparticles in superconductors, as these techniques directly probe the quasiparticle charge and energy imbalance even at mK temperatures. In this work, we employ mesoscopic three terminal Cu and Al NIS devices to study non-local quasiparticle transport over length-scales on the order of the superconducting coherence length in this regime. Via a dual-bias scheme, which utilizes detector biases both above and below the superconducting gap, we are able to extract the effect of quasiparticle energy imbalance via its impact on the self consistent pair potential by symmetry considerations. We observe non-local conductance features due to pair-breaking which are anti-symmetric with respect to the polarity of the voltage bias, with a sharp onset during single electron tunneling at energies around $3Δ$. We compare these findings with quasiclassical simulations including inelastic effects to obtain estimates of the energy dependent inelastic scattering time. In addition, we demonstrate kinetic effects due to a large applied supercurrent which can also be captured in this formalism and decomposed with respect to the particle-hole symmetry and supercurrent direction, and discuss further opportunities for the advancement of this method.

</details>

### [7] [Rare but Resilient: Dispersal diversity buffers species vulnerability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26589)
*Davide Bernardi,Giorgio Nicoletti,Prajwal Padmanabha,Samir Suweis,Sandro Azaele,Simon A. Levin,Andrea Rinaldo,Amos Maritan*

Main category: q-bio.PE

TL;DR: 本文基于复杂系统的统计物理（statistical physics of complex systems）提出一个通用框架，将影响物种存活的关键过程整合为一个可测量的指标——竞争平衡（competitive balance）。该指标通过纳入扩散策略多样性和种间互作结构来量化物种脆弱性，且可从空间丰度数据推断，避免了对物种性状或扩散参数的估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 预测生态群落中物种的持久性（species persistence）是理论与实证生态学的基础性挑战。现有方法（mechanistic models）参数难以从数据中估计，而统计工具（statistical tools）的上下文特定参数（context-specific parameters）可解释性较差。

Method: 基于复杂系统的统计物理（statistical physics of complex systems）构建一般性框架，将控制物种生存的关键过程整合为单一可测量指标——竞争平衡（competitive balance）。该指标在物种丰度之外，纳入扩散策略多样性（diversity of dispersal strategies）和群落内部种间互作结构（structure of interspecific interactions）。关键突破在于该指标可从空间丰度数据（spatial abundance data）推断，无需估计物种性状（species traits）或扩散参数（dispersal parameters）。

Result: 结果表明，在给定丰度下，扩散策略的更大异质性（greater heterogeneity in dispersal strategies）会降低物种的脆弱性。通过热带和温带森林数据验证了该框架的有效性。

Conclusion: 该框架可推广至多种不同类型的生态系统，为评估物种在特定上下文中的脆弱性（context-dependent species vulnerability）提供了一个系统性且可解释的工具，充分考虑了物种与整个群落的交互作用。

Abstract: Predicting species persistence within ecological communities is a fundamental challenge for both empirical and theoretical ecology. Existing methods span from mechanistic models, whose parameters are difficult to estimate from data, to statistical tools whose context-specific parameters are less interpretable. Here, we present a general framework, grounded in the statistical physics of complex systems, that integrates the key processes governing species survival into a single measurable quantity: the competitive balance. This metric quantifies a focal species' vulnerability beyond its abundance by incorporating the diversity of dispersal strategies and the structure of interspecific interactions within the community. Crucially, it can be inferred from spatial abundance data, thus circumventing the need to estimate species traits or dispersal parameters. Our results reveal that greater heterogeneity in dispersal strategies reduces vulnerability for a given abundance. Although we validate the framework using tropical and temperate forest data, it can be applied to a range of different ecosystems, providing a systemic and interpretable tool for assessing a context-dependent species vulnerability that accounts for its interactions with the entire community.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.dis-nn'></div>

# cond-mat.dis-nn [[Back]](#toc)

### [8] [Effective length scales, dispersion relations, and discrete densities of states for Laplacian eigenvectors on complex networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26599)
*Per Arne Rikvold*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种从图拉普拉斯矩阵（graph Laplacian matrix）的特征向量中提取有效长度尺度（effective length scale）的方法，用于构建随机网络上的扩散或振荡过程的色散关系（dispersion relations）。该方法源自凝聚态物理（condensed-matter physics）中通过体积与界面面积之比估算无序材料关联长度（correlation length）的技术，并将其重新解释为图中两倍总边数与连接不同符号顶点的边数之比。作者将该方法以教学性细节描述后，应用于九种不同的自然与人工网络图，识别出分布型和局域型特征向量，并以图表和表格形式呈现了色散关系、态密度（density of states）及主要数值结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在随机网络（random networks）上研究扩散或振荡过程时，需要为图拉普拉斯矩阵的特征向量获取有效的长度尺度，因为该矩阵的特征值代表逆时间尺度（inverse time scales）。此前缺少一种系统的方法将这些特征向量映射为空间上的关联长度，从而构建对应的色散关系。

Method: 借鉴了Debye等人在无序材料中估算关联长度的经典方法（体积与界面面积之比），将其移植到图论框架下：将目标量定义为两倍总边数除以特定特征向量上符号不同的顶点之间相连的边数。该方法在文中以教学性方式详细阐述了所需的数学概念和计算步骤，并应用于九种不同的图结构。

Result: 识别出了分布型（delocalized）和局域型（localized）两类特征向量。结果以图形形式展示了示例特征向量、色散关系和离散态密度（discrete densities of states），并以表格汇总了主要数值结果。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法能够有效地为各种自然与人工网络的特征向量赋予长度尺度，从而构建色散关系，可用于刻画随机网络上的扩散与振荡动力学。

Abstract: To construct dispersion relations for diffusion or oscillation processes on random networks, it is necessary to obtain effective length scales for the eigenvectors of a graph Laplacian matrix, whose eigenvalues represent inverse time scales. For this purpose, we adapt a method originally introduced in condensed-matter physics to estimate correlation lengths for disordered materials as the ratio of volume to interface area [P. Debye, H.R. Anderson and H. Brumberger, J. Appl. Phys. 28, 679 (1957)]. In a graph setting of vertices connected by edges, we interpret this as the ratio of twice the total number of edges to the number of edges connecting vertices bearing values of different sign on the particular eigenvector. After describing the method and the necessary concepts in pedagogical detail, we apply it to nine different graphs representing natural and artificial networks, including two tree graphs without and with random shortcuts, the nervous system of a roundworm, a food web, a social network of dolphins, an electrical power grid, and a model porous material. The results identify both distributed and localized eigenvectors. They are given in graphical format showing example eigenvectors, dispersion relations, and discrete densities of states, as well as tables summarizing the main numerical results.

</details>

# math.PR [[Back]](#toc)

### [9] [Spectrum of Random Matrices with Exploding Moments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26499)
*Indrajit Jana,Sunita Rani*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文研究了当矩阵元素矩随矩阵规模增长（即爆炸矩，exploding moments）时，椭圆（elliptic）、中心对称（centrosymmetric）、循环（circulant）和互相关分块（inter-correlated block）等几类矩阵模型线性特征值统计量的中心极限定理（central limit theorem, CLT），并利用渐近Wick公式（asymptotic Wick formula）建立了这些CLT。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关于随机矩阵线性特征值统计量中心极限定理的研究通常假设矩阵元素矩有界或固定；本文旨在将CLT推广到元素矩随矩阵规模增长（即“爆炸矩”）的更一般情形，并涵盖多种具有特殊结构的矩阵模型。

Method: 采用渐近Wick公式（asymptotic Wick formula）作为主要技术工具，对椭圆矩阵、中心对称矩阵、循环矩阵以及互相关分块矩阵等不同类型矩阵模型的线性特征值统计量建立CLT。

Result: 针对椭圆、中心对称、循环和互相关分块等四类矩阵模型，在爆炸矩条件下，分别证明了线性特征值统计量服从中心极限定理。

Conclusion: 在元素矩可随矩阵规模增长的条件下，多种结构随机矩阵的线性特征值统计量仍满足中心极限定理，且渐近Wick公式是处理此类问题的有效统一框架。

Abstract: We study the central limit theorem (CLT) for linear eigenvalue statistics of several types of matrix models, whose entries are having exploding moments, i.e., moments of the entries are increasing with the size of the matrix. In particular, we study elliptic, centrosymmetric, circulant, and inter-correlated block matrices. The CLTs are established using asymptotic Wick formula.

</details>

### [10] [Domain-induced control of latent heat in freestanding BaTiO$_3$ membranes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26089)
*Tapas Bar,David Pesquera,Arnau Villalobos-Martin,Cristian Rodriguez-Tinoco,Umair Saeed,Kumara Cordero-Edwards,Jessica Padilla,Jose Manuel Caicedo Roque,Jose Santiso,Pol Lloveras,Leo Boron,Igor Lukyanchuk,Gustau Catalan,Javier Rodriguez-Viejo*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过去除衬底约束的自支撑BaTiO₃薄膜实验，发现畴形态（domain morphology）而非厚度或边界条件决定了铁电相变阶数：大畴区域呈现一级相变特征和潜热，而密集180°畴区域则表现为连续相变，Ginzburg-Landau分析表明畴尺寸减小会降低自由能势垒，从而使名义上的一级不稳定性变得平滑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释薄铁电BaTiO₃薄膜中持续相变（continuous transition）与块体一级相变（first-order transition）行为差异的微观机制，澄清该差异究竟源于外延应变（epitaxial strain）、维度效应（dimensionality）还是畴形态。

Method: 采用准绝热纳米量热法（quasi-adiabatic nanocalorimetry）测量无衬底夹持与热沉效应的自支撑BaTiO₃薄膜；利用X射线衍射确认四方-立方结构转变；通过压电力显微镜（piezoresponse force microscopy）关联畴尺寸演变；结合Ginzburg-Landau分析进行理论解释。

Result: 厚膜中形成大单畴区域，相变时表现出明显的潜热（latent heat）；薄膜中形成密集180°畴模式，在相同四方-立方结构变化下呈现连续相变。畴尺寸减小导致自由能势垒降低，使一级不稳定性变得平滑。

Conclusion: 畴形态是氧化物薄膜中铁电相变阶数的关键决定因素；通过畴工程（domain engineering）可实现增强热效应（caloric effects）的设计指导。

Abstract: Thin ferroelectric BaTiO$_3$ films often exhibit continuous transitions instead of the first-order behavior of bulk crystals, a discrepancy usually attributed to epitaxial strain or dimensionality. Using quasi-adiabatic nanocalorimetry on freestanding BaTiO$_3$ membranes-free of clamping and substrate heat sinking-we show that domain morphology, not thickness or boundary conditions, controls the transition order. Thick membranes with large, monodomain-like regions display clear latent heat, whereas thinner membranes with dense 180$^{\circ}$ domain patterns show a continuous transition despite undergoing the same tetragonal-cubic structural change confirmed by x-ray diffraction. Piezoresponse force microscopy links this behavior to domain-size evolution, and a Ginzburg-Landau analysis demonstrates how reduced domain size lowers the free-energy barrier, rounding a nominally first-order instability. These results identify domain morphology as the key determinant of ferroelectric transition order in oxide membranes and establish design guidelines for enhancing caloric effects through domain engineering.

</details>


### [11] [Hidden Crossover and Relaxor-Like Response from Emerging Polar Skyrmion Correlations in Ferroelectric Superlattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26100)
*Zhiyang Wang,Fei Yang,Long-Qing Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过相场模拟，本研究发现铁电超晶格中的极性斯格明子（polar skyrmions）在低温下经历一个隐藏的热交叉（thermal crossover），从无关联的层分辨态演变为层间关联的集体态，并在不伴随对称性破缺的情况下产生显著的介电峰，揭示了拓扑缺陷关联（topological defect correlations）作为热力学异常组织原理的新机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为极性斯格明子是弱耦合的、局限在单层中的纳米拓扑构型，其角色次于对称性破缺序参量。本文意在揭示这类拓扑缺陷在深处于铁电相内部时是否存在未被认识到的热力学行为和组织原理。

Method: 采用大规模相场模拟（phase-field simulations）对铁电超晶格系统进行研究，分析温度变化下极性斯格明子构型的关联演化以及介电响应的变化。

Result: 发现了隐藏的热交叉：极性斯格明子从无关联的层分辨态转变为层间关联态；该交叉不伴随额外的对称性破缺或新的序参量，但产生了明显的介电峰（dielectric susceptibility peak）；该峰在交流驱动下随频率移动，表现出类似弛豫铁电体（relaxor ferroelectrics）的行为，尽管系统中不存在淬灭无序（quenched disorder）或极性纳米区（polar nanoregions）。

Conclusion: 确立了非无序路径产生弛豫型介电响应（relaxor-like dielectric response）的可能性，指出拓扑缺陷关联可作为热力学异常的组织原理（organizing principle），提供了一种区别于传统对称性破缺临界行为（critical behavior）的新机制。

Abstract: Polar skyrmions in ferroelectric superlattices are nanoscale topological polarization textures typically regarded as weakly coupled objects confined to individual layers, with a role secondary to that of the underlying symmetry-breaking order parameter. Here using large-scale phase-field simulations of ferroelectric superlattices, we uncover a hidden thermal crossover deep inside the ferroelectric phase, where polar skyrmions evolve from an uncorrelated, layer-resolved state into an interlayer-correlated ensemble. This crossover occurs without additional symmetry breaking or a new order parameter, but produces a pronounced broad peak in the dielectric susceptibility. The anomaly originates from the competition between correlation-enhanced response, associated with the growth of interlayer skyrmion correlations, and polarization-induced stiffness, which suppresses dielectric fluctuations at low temperature. Under AC driving, the peak shifts with frequency, resembling relaxor ferroelectrics despite the absence of quenched disorder or polar nanoregions. Our results establish a disorder-free route to relaxor-like dielectric response and identify topological defect correlations as an organizing principle for thermodynamic anomalies, providing a mechanism distinct from conventional critical behavior associated with symmetry breaking and divergent order-parameter fluctuations.

</details>


### [12] [Implementation of the hybrid exchange-correlation functionals in the SIESTA code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26108)
*Yann Pouillon,Bill Clintone Oyomo,James Sifuna,María Camarasa-Gómez,Xinming Qin,Carlos Beltrán,Fernando Gómez-Ortiz,Honghui Shang,Javier Junquera*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文在SIESTA代码中实现了杂化交换关联泛函（hybrid XC functionals）的高效精确版本，利用高斯型轨道（GTOs）拟合局域数值原子轨道（NAOs）以解析计算四中心电子排斥积分（ERIs），结合多重筛选技术和动态并行方案，实现了对半导体、绝缘体和二维材料等大体系的高精度能带预测，HSE06泛函结果与G0W0及实验数据高度一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统密度泛函理论（DFT）中的半局域泛函（如PBE）在预测带隙时存在系统性低估问题，而杂化泛函虽能显著改善精度，但在基于严格局域数值原子轨道（NAOs）的SIESTA代码中缺乏高效实现，难以应用于大规模扩展体系。

Method: 采用高斯型轨道（GTOs）对NAOs进行拟合表示，借助LIBINT库解析计算四中心电子排斥积分（ERIs）；将杂化泛函框架无缝集成至SIESTA的实空间网格和稀疏矩阵基础设施中，并结合多种积分截断筛选技术控制计算复杂度；引入杂化泛函力的全解析公式及动态并行分布策略。

Result: 在半导体、绝缘体和二维材料等基准测试集上，HSE06杂化泛函显著改善了带隙预测精度，结果与G0W0及实验数据高度一致；详细分析了高斯函数数量、基组范围和积分截断阈值对精度与效率的权衡关系。

Conclusion: 杂化泛函计算在SIESTA中对于大型扩展体系已成为可行方案，实现了大规模高精确度的电子结构和结构性质的第一性原理预测。

Abstract: We present an efficient and accurate implementation of hybrid exchange-correlation (XC) functionals in the SIESTA code, enabling large-scale simulations based on Hartree-Fock-type exact exchange combined with strictly localized numerical atomic orbitals (NAOs). Our approach exploits a fitted representation of the NAOs in terms of Gaussian-type orbitals (GTOs), which allows for the analytical evaluation of four-center electron repulsion integrals (ERIs) via the LIBINT library. This framework is seamlessly integrated with SIESTA's real-space grid and sparse-matrix infrastructure, and is combined with multiple screening techniques to control the computational complexity. We also introduce a fully analytical formulation of hybrid-functional forces and a dynamic parallel distribution scheme that ensures excellent scalability. We validate our implementation through benchmark calculations on a broad set of systems (including semiconductors, insulators, and two-dimensional materials) and demonstrate that the HSE06 functional significantly improves the prediction of band gaps compared to PBE, in close agreement with G0W0 and experimental data. We analyze in detail the trade-offs between accuracy and computational efficiency as a function of the number of Gaussians, basis set range, and integral screening thresholds. Our results confirm that hybrid functional calculations in SIESTA are now feasible for large extended systems, making accurate first-principles predictions of electronic and structural properties accessible at scale.

</details>


### [13] [First-Principles Study of Structural, Electronic, Thermal, and Optical Properties of Quasi-2D C2 N2 O Using GGA and HSE06](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26149)
*Hemn. G. H,Nzar. R. Abdullah,Vidar Gudmundsson*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过密度泛函理论（DFT）和从头算分子动力学（AIMD）系统分析了准二维C2N2O结构的结构稳定性、电子性质、光学性质及热学性质。C2N2O是一种中等间接带隙半导体，具有显著的光学各向异性、可见-紫外波段吸收能力、极低的晶格热导率（约0.017 W/m·K），以及接近杜隆-珀蒂（Dulong-Petit）极限的热容，表明其在纳米光电子和热控器件方面具有应用潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索准二维材料C2N2O在结构、稳定性、电子、光学和热学方面的综合性能，评估其在纳米尺度光电子学及热控应用中的可行性。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）和从头算分子动力学（ab initio molecular dynamics, AIMD）方法，对C2N2O的几何结构、电子结构、光学响应及热学性质进行第一性原理计算。

Result: C2N2O结构在热力学和能量上稳定，但动力学稳定性较弱；为中等间接带隙半导体，带隙值为2.3 eV（GGA）和3.9 eV（HSE06），带隙源于N、C、O原子的p轨道杂化。光学性质方面，材料在可见光和紫外区有显著吸收，面内与面外极化方向呈现明显各向异性，等离激元共振（plasmon resonance）位于约3.8 eV。热学方面，300 K时热容约382 J/mol·K，接近并略高于杜隆-珀蒂极限（Dulong-Petit limit）；晶格热导率极低，约0.017 W/m·K，主要由高声子散射率（约3.2 1/ps）导致。

Conclusion: 准二维C2N2O结构在保持结构稳定性的同时，展现出可调控的电子、光学和热学性质，是纳米光电子器件和热控应用的潜在候选材料。

Abstract: DFT and AIMD are used to investigate the structural, stability, electronic, thermal, and optical properties of the quasi-2D C2N2O structure. The structure exhibits thermal and energy stability, signifying robustness under ambient conditions, however less dynamical stability is observed. The electronic structure investigation reveals that C2N2O displays semiconducting properties with a moderate indirect band gap resulting from the hybridisation of p-orbitals of N, C, and O atoms, with band gap values of 2.3 eV (GGA) and 3.9 eV (HSE06). The optical properties, including the dielectric function, optical conductivity, and refractive index, are thoroughly analyzed to clarify the electronic transitions. The material exhibits considerable optical absorption in the visible and ultraviolet spectrum, with notable anisotropy between in-plane and out-of-plane polarizations. Furthermore, plasmon resonance occurs at around 3.8 eV, relating to the collective oscillations of charge carriers. The thermal properties indicate a heat capacity of around 382 J/mol.K at 300 K, which is close to and slightly above the standard Dulong-Petit limit for this structure, indicating near-complete excitation of lattice vibrational modes at room temperature. The lattice thermal conductivity is extremely low, reaching approximately 0.017 W/m.K at 300 K, primarily attributed to significant phonon scattering, evidenced by a scattering rate of roughly 3.2 1/ps in the phonon frequency ranges. The findings demonstrate that the C2N2O structure maintains structural stability while allowing for tunable electronic, optical, and thermal properties, making it a promising candidate for nanoscale optoelectronic and thermal control applications.

</details>


### [14] [Achieving Large Uniaxial and Homogeneous Strain in Two-Dimensional Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26164)
*Yangchen He,Jessica Kienbaum,Wuzhang Fang,Hongrui Ma,Ying Wang,Ping Yuan,Daniel A. Rhodes*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种高良率的样品制备与器件应变平台，突破现有二维材料应变调控在可逆性、低温传递和应变幅度上的限制。该平台可实现最高至材料本征断裂应变（约4%–5.5%）的可逆均匀单轴应变调控，并能设计跨度数十微米的线性应变梯度（最高0.06%/μm）。以CrSBr及三种过渡金属二硫属化物（transition metal dichalcogenides）相（2H-MoTe₂、1T′ -MoTe₂、T_d-WTe₂）验证其通用性，在T_d-WTe₂中观测到A₁³模创纪录的约5.5%应变连续红移以及2%应变起A₁³与A₁²模的清晰分岔。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 应变工程（strain engineering）是调控二维材料电子、磁性与拓扑性质的有力手段，尤其>3%高应变下预测了大量相变与物态转变；然而现有方法多限于1.5%以下应变，且在循环应变可重复性与低温应变传递方面存在显著不足，亟需开发能实现高应变、可逆、均匀且可控梯度应变的实验平台。

Method: 作者提出一种高良率样品制备与器件应变平台，通过特殊设计实现样品与基底间的有效耦合与应力传递；该平台支持均匀单轴应变与线性应变梯度的可逆调控，并适用于多种二维材料体系。

Result: 以CrSBr作为模型体系实现了最高约4%的均匀单轴应变（无显著滑移）与0.06%/μm的线性应变梯度；该方法在2H-MoTe₂、1T′ -MoTe₂和T_d-WTe₂三种过渡金属二硫属化物（transition metal dichalcogenides）相中均验证有效。在T_d-WTe₂中，理论计算支持的拉曼A₁³模连续红移达到创纪录的约5.5%应变，且自2%应变起A₁³与A₁²模发生清晰分岔。

Conclusion: 该应变平台克服了高应变下的可逆性、低温兼容性与梯度设计等关键瓶颈，为系统研究挠曲电（flexoelectric）与挠曲磁（flexomagnetic）效应提供了新途径，并展示了在多种二维材料体系中的广泛适用性。

Abstract: Strain engineering is a powerful tool for tuning the electronic, magnetic, and topological properties of two-dimensional (2D) materials and thin films - particularly at high values of strain (>3%) where many electronic, magnetic, and structural transitions have been predicted. However, most approaches to tuning strain in 2D materials are limited below 1.5%, with poor repeatability when cycling strain and low strain transfer when cooling to cryogenic temperatures. Here, we report a high-yield sample preparation and device strain platform that overcomes these limitations, enabling precise, reversible strain tuning up to the intrinsic strain-to-failure of the materials tested herein. In addition, we show that this platform can be used to controllably design uniform linear strain gradients across of 10's of $μ$m, providing a novel route to systematically investigate flexoelectric and flexomagnetic phenomena. Using CrSBr as a model system, we demonstrate uniform uniaxial strain, up to ~4%, with negligible slippage and linear strain gradients of up to 0.06%/$μ$m. We further show that our strain approach is applicable to a broad class of 2D materials, validating its performance for three different phases of transition metal dichalcogenides: 2H-MoTe$_2$, 1T$^\prime$-MoTe$_2$ and T$_\mathrm{d}$-WTe$_2$. In T$_\mathrm{d}$-WTe$_2$, verified by theoretical calculations, we show a continuous redshift of the A$_1^3$ mode, up to a record-breaking ~5.5% strain, with a clear separation of the A$_1^3$ and A$_1^2$ modes starting at 2% strain.

</details>


### [15] [Negative magnetoresistance in strained $α$-Sn and $α$-SnGe films in an in-plane magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26168)
*Sunny Phan,Andrei Kogan,Jesse Thompson,Trent Johnson,Alexander Khaetskii,Arnold Kiefer*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过研究应变异质外延薄膜中狄拉克半金属态（Dirac semimetal）纯α-Sn与三维拓扑绝缘体态（3D topological insulator）合金α-SnGe的磁输运性质，发现两者均表现出与手征反常（chiral anomaly）预期不一致的负磁电阻（negative magnetoresistance, MR）行为，因此提出其他机制可能主导α-Sn体系中负MR的产生，并讨论了样品设计和材料质量等因素对实验结果不一致性的潜在影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验手征反常（chiral anomaly）是否为应变异质外延α-Sn薄膜中负磁电阻（negative MR）现象的物理根源。

Method: 实验研究了处于狄拉克半金属态（Dirac semimetal）的纯α-Sn与处于三维拓扑绝缘体态（3D topological insulator）的合金α-SnGe在应变异质外延薄膜中的磁输运（magnetotransport）行为。

Result: 两种态均观测到负磁电阻（negative MR），且无论电流方向与面内磁场（in-plane magnetic field）平行还是垂直，该现象均存在；但负MR对磁场强度的依赖关系不同。

Conclusion: 观测结果与手征反常（chiral anomaly）的预言不一致，暗示狄拉克/外尔半金属（Dirac/Weyl semimetal）相α-Sn中的负MR可能源自其他物理机制；样品设计和材料质量等因素可能造成已有文献中关于应变α-Sn薄膜负MR观测结果的不一致。

Abstract: To test the hypothesis that the chiral anomaly is responsible for negative magnetoresitance (MR) in \atn{}, we have studied magnetotransport in strained, epitaxial films of pure \aSn{} and the alloy \aSnGe{} that are in the Dirac semimetal and 3D topological insulator state, respectively. We have observed for both states a negative MR with current either parallel or transverse to the in-plane magnetic field, but with a different dependence of MR on $\vec{B}$ strength. Our results are inconsistent with the chiral anomaly and suggest that other mechanisms may be responsible for negative MR in the Dirac/Weyl semimetal phase of \aSn{}. We also discuss several factors in sample design and material quality that may be contributing to the incongruous observations of MR reported in studies of strained \atn{} films.

</details>


### [16] [All-organic self-separating three-dimensionally nanoarchitected electrochemical energy storage devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26222)

TL;DR: 该工作实现了一种全有机、三维纳米结构（3D nanoarchitected）的“自分离”锂离子电化学储能（EES）器件，以固态全电池形式循环运行。器件由碳阳极与导电活性阴极组成，通过电化学处理生成固体电解质界面（SEI）作为隔膜，是首个全有机材料衍生的3D纳米结构EES器件及“自分离”电池制造设计。

Method: 利用超高分子量嵌段共聚物（block copolymer, BCP）引导酚醛树脂结构定向，制备具有共连续孔网络（co-continuous pore network）的单体碳阳极；通过电聚合（electropolymerization）将单相导电氧化还原活性材料PAQEDOT填充至孔隙中作为阴极；通过在外置锂存在下进行电化学循环处理，生成固体电解质界面（solid electrolyte interphase, SEI）作为隔膜并实现电极锂化。

Abstract: This work realizes a three-dimensionally (3D) nanoarchitected, all organic, "self-separating" lithium-ion electrochemical energy storage (EES) device that is cycled as a solid-state full cell. Electropolymerization of a single-phase conductive and redox-active material, poly((2,3-dihydrothieno[3,4-b][1,4]dioxin-2-yl)methyl 9,10-dioxo-9,10-dihydroanthracene-2-carboxylate) (PAQEDOT), into the pore space provides the cathode of the cell. The device is electronically contacted to the relevant electrode network enabled by the co-continuous nature of each electrode. Electrochemical processing via cycling against external lithium in an electrolyte generates a solid electrolyte interphase (SEI) as a separator and lithiates the cell electrodes, after which the EES device is cycled in the solid state. While the full cell does not demonstrate high cyclability, the best full cell demonstrates a discharge capacity of 267 milliamp hours per gram (mAh/g). This work marks, to the best of knowledge of the authors, the first example of an all-organic materials derived 3D nanoarchitected EES device, as well as the first design of "self-separating" cell fabrication. Furthermore, generalization of the design to another co-continuous carbon form factor is demonstrated.

### [17] [Coexistence of d-Wave Altermagnetism and Topological States in Janus FeSeX (X = S, Te) Monolayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26239)
*Alvaro Gonzalez-Garcia,William Lopez-Perez,Paola Pacheco,Luz Ramirez-Montes,Rafael Gonzalez-Hernandez*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算，揭示了Janus FeSeX (X = S, Te)单层中d波交替磁性（d-wave altermagnetism）与拓扑行为（topological behavior）的共存现象。化学不对称性破缺面外镜面对称和反演对称，产生各向异性交换相互作用和动量依赖的自旋劈裂；引入自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）后，费米能级处出现有限拓扑带隙，伴随量子化的自旋霍尔电导平台和非平庸拓扑不变量（自旋陈数=1, Z₂=1）。这些发现确立了FeSeS和FeSeTe作为实现拓扑交替磁性和自旋-轨道驱动电荷-自旋转换的二维平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维材料中非常规磁性（unconventional magnetism）与能带拓扑（band topology）之间的相互作用已成为凝聚态物理的重要主题。探索同时具备交替磁性和拓扑性质的材料，对于低耗散自旋电子学器件的开发具有重要意义。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）对Janus FeSeX (X = S, Te)单层进行电子结构分析；通过声子色散分析（phonon dispersion analyses）验证动力学稳定性；利用应变依赖计算（strain-dependent calculations）研究双轴应变对交替磁交换劈裂（altermagnetic exchange splitting）的调控；在引入自旋-轨道耦合后计算拓扑带隙、自旋霍尔电导和拓扑不变量。

Result: Janus结构化学不对称性导致面外镜面对称和反演对称破缺，在无自旋-轨道耦合时即产生各向异性交换相互作用和动量依赖的自旋劈裂（交替磁性的标志特征）。两种化合物均具有动力学稳定性；交替磁交换劈裂大小（Δ_s）可通过双轴应变有效调控。考虑自旋-轨道耦合后，费米能级处出现有限拓扑带隙，并观察到量子化的自旋霍尔电导平台以及非平庸拓扑不变量（自旋陈数=1, Z₂=1）。

Conclusion: FeSeS和FeSeTe单层被确立为有望实现拓扑交替磁性（topological altermagnetism）和自旋-轨道驱动电荷-自旋转换的二维平台，为低耗散自旋电子学器件开辟了新途径。

Abstract: The interplay between unconventional magnetism and band topology in two-dimensional materials has emerged as an important theme in condensed matter physics. Here, we present first-principles calculations that reveal the coexistence of d-wave altermagnetism and topological behavior in Janus FeSeX (X = S, Te) monolayers. The chemical asymmetry of the Janus structure breaks both out-of-plane mirror and inversion symmetries, leading to anisotropic exchange interactions and momentum-dependent spin splittings even in the absence of spin-orbit coupling, the defining signature of altermagnetism. Phonon dispersion analyses confirm the dynamical stability of both compounds, while strain-dependent calculations demonstrate that the magnitude of the altermagnetic exchange splitting ($Δ_s$) can be efficiently tuned by biaxial strain. When spin-orbit coupling is included, a finite topological band gap emerges at the Fermi level, accompanied by quantized spin Hall conductivity plateaus and nontrivial topological invariants (spin Chern number = 1, Z2=1). These findings establish FeSeS and FeSeTe as promising two-dimensional platforms for realizing topological altermagnetism and spin--orbit--driven charge--spin conversion, thus opening new avenues for low-dissipation spintronic devices.

### [18] [Influence of strain on the anomalous Hall and Nernst effects in Fe thin films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26257)
*Ao Nakagawa,Ryo Toyama,Keisuke Masuda,Weinan Zhou,Hirofumi Suto,Kodchakorn Simalaotao,Yoshio Miura,Yuya Sakuraba,Tetsunori Koda*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过调控单元素铁（Fe）外延薄膜中的晶格应变，系统分析了反常霍尔效应（AHE）和反常能斯特效应（ANE）的应变依赖性。结果表明，反常霍尔电导率（AHC）主要由本征贡献（贝里曲率）决定，与理论计算吻合；而反常能斯特电导率（ANC）则显著偏离理论值，受外在贡献强烈影响，揭示了两者物理起源的本质差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶格应变是调控反常霍尔效应（AHE）和反常能斯特效应（ANE）的有效手段，但多组分材料中由于杂质和无序等外在贡献的复杂性，难以将应变效应从贝里曲率（Berry curvature）调制中分离出来，且难以与第一性原理计算直接对比。因此，需要选择结构简单的单元素体系来厘清应变对这两种横向输运现象的内在影响机制。

Method: 选择铁（Fe）这一典型单元素铁磁体作为研究对象，通过改变衬底和沉积条件，在外延薄膜中调控应变的符号和大小；利用标度律分析（scaling law analysis）区分本征和外在贡献，并将实验结果与基于贝里曲率修正的理论计算进行对比。

Result: 反常霍尔电导率（AHC）随四角畸变比（c/a）呈现清晰的依赖性，与基于贝里曲率（Berry curvature）修正的理论计算结果高度一致；反常能斯特电导率（ANC）则显著偏离理论预测值，且随c/a的变化趋势与AHC截然不同。

Conclusion: 在铁（Fe）薄膜中，反常霍尔电导率（AHC）主要由本征机制（intrinsic mechanism）主导，而反常能斯特电导率（ANC）则受到外在贡献（extrinsic contribution）的强烈影响，表明这两者具有不同的物理起源。

Abstract: The anomalous Hall effect (AHE) and anomalous Nernst effect (ANE) are the transverse transport phenomena in magnetic materials, which reflect the Berry curvature arising from the electronic structure near the Fermi level. Lattice strain provides a direct means to tune these effects by modifying the electronic structure; however, disentangling the strain-induced effect through the Berry curvature modulations in multicomponent materials is challenging due to complexities arising from extrinsic contributions by impurities and disorder, as well as difficulties in simple direct comparison with first-principles calculations. In this study, we focus on Fe, a prototypical single element ferromagnet with a well-established electronic structure, and tune the sign and magnitude of the strain in epitaxial thin films of by varying the substrates and deposition conditions to investigate the strain effect on the AHE and ANE. Scaling law analysis revealed that the intrinsic anomalous Hall conductivity (AHC) exhibits a clear tetragonal distortion (c/a) dependence, in good agreement with theoretical calculations based on Berry curvature modification. In contrast, the anomalous Nernst conductivity (ANC) shows a pronounced deviation from the theoretical values and markedly different c/a dependence. These results demonstrate a crucial difference in the physical origin between the AHC and the ANC in the Fe films; the AHC is predominantly governed by intrinsic mechanisms, whereas the ANC is strongly influenced by the extrinsic contribution.

### [19] [Accelerated Prediction of Surface Stability and Particle Morphology in Ionic Crystals via Electrostatic Screening](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26264)
*Sourav Baiju,Payam Kaghazchi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 提出一种基于静电分析（electrostatic analysis）的快速可扩展方法，用于预测离子材料（ionic materials）的表面稳定性与平衡晶体形貌（equilibrium crystal morphology）。该方法通过构建化学计量比表面端元（stoichiometric slab terminations）并评估其静电能量，绕过昂贵的密度泛函理论（Density Functional Theory, DFT）计算，实现高通量（high-throughput）表面构型筛选，并在多种材料体系中得到验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于DFT的表面稳定性预测方法计算成本高昂，难以扩展到大体系（large systems）和高指数表面（high-index surfaces），限制了材料高通量筛选与加速发现。因此需要一种快速且可扩展的替代方案。

Method: 方法包括：构建化学计量比表面端元并计算其静电能量；通过表面偶极矩（surface dipole moment）计算识别极性表面（polar surfaces），并利用基于静电学的副本交换蒙特卡洛模拟（replica-exchange Monte Carlo simulations）实现表面重构稳定化；将表面偶极矩作为区分不同材料类别行为的有效描述符（effective descriptor）。

Result: 在简单与复杂三维材料以及二维层状氧化物（2D layered oxides）上的验证表明，预测的主导晶面（dominant facets）与DFT及实验观测结果一致。静电相互作用（electrostatic interactions）能够捕捉多种材料体系中相对表面稳定性（relative surface stability）的主要趋势。框架还揭示了一些高指数表面在平衡形貌中不可忽略的作用。

Conclusion: 静电学方法为表面稳定性与颗粒形貌（particle morphology）的高通量预测提供了快速可靠的途径，有助于加速材料发现，并为复杂能源材料（energy materials）中更精细的计算提供稳健的起点。

Abstract: This work presents a fast and scalable approach for predicting surface stability and equilibrium crystal morphology in ionic materials using electrostatic analysis. The method constructs stoichiometric slab terminations and evaluates their electrostatic energies, enabling high-throughput screening of surface configurations at a fraction of the cost of conventional approaches. Polar surfaces are identified through surface dipole moment calculations and stabilized via electrostatics-based reconstruction using replica-exchange Monte Carlo simulations. The surface dipole moment further emerges as an effective descriptor to distinguish the behavior of different classes of materials. By bypassing expensive Density Functional Theory (DFT) calculations, the approach extends naturally to large systems and high-index surfaces that are typically inaccessible to DFT. Electrostatic interactions are shown to capture the dominant trends in relative surface stability across diverse material systems. The method is validated on simple and complex 3D materials as well as 2D layered oxides, where the predicted dominant facets are consistent with reported density functional theory and experimental observations. Importantly, the framework also reveals cases where high-index surfaces play a non-negligible role in the equilibrium morphology. These results establish electrostatics as a fast and reliable route for high-throughput prediction of surface stability and particle morphology, opening a pathway for accelerated materials discovery and providing a robust starting point for more detailed calculations in complex energy materials.

Method: 采用Song等人开发的具有可迁移性的机器学习势，对二元Al-Ti液态合金进行分子动力学模拟，涵盖不同温度与组分条件，并与实验数据对比以验证势函数的可靠性。

Abstract: We investigate the structural and dynamical properties of binary aluminum-titanium liquid metallic alloys, as a function of temperature and composition. Although this potential was initially trained on solid properties, we find good agreement between the experimental data and the simulation results for the liquid state. The excess volume and compositional changes of the structure are captured well by the machine-learned potential. ### [21] [Polaron Conductivity in $α$-Fe2O3 Quenched by Adsorbed NO2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26372)
*Tushar K. Ghosh,Elvar Ö. Jónsson,Stephan Steinhauer,Panagiotis Grammatikopoulos,Hannes Jónsson*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过DFT+U和弹性带（nudged elastic band）计算，揭示了α-Fe2O3(0001)表面极化子（polaron）的形成、迁移及NO₂吸附对其的淬灭机制，为氧化铁基气体传感器的电阻响应提供了微观解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极化子介导的电荷传输在α-Fe2O3的气敏性能中至关重要，但表面吸附物与极化子之间的原子尺度相互作用尚未被充分理解。

Method: 采用含Hubbard-U校正的密度泛函理论（DFT+U）结合弹性带（nEB）计算方法，研究Fe端接α-Fe2O3(0001)表面的极化子形成、迁移及淬灭行为。

Result: 体相α-Fe2O3中小极化子跳跃的活化能为0.12 eV，与实验高度吻合；极化子从体相迁移至表面能量降低0.12 eV，表明载流子优先定域在气-固界面；NO₂吸附诱导0.72 e-从氧化物转移到分子，消除了局域化的Fe²⁺极化子态，抑制了极化子导电性。

Conclusion: 研究直接解释了赤铁矿传感器在氧化性气体中电阻升高的微观机制，并建立了表面吸附通过控制极化子数量来调制α-Fe2O3电荷传输的框架，为改进氧化铁气体传感器提供了设计原理。

Abstract: Polaron-mediated charge transport in α-Fe2O3 plays a central role in its performance as a gas-sensing material, yet the atomistic interaction between surface adsorbates and polarons remains insufficiently understood. Here, density functional theory with Hubbard-U correction (DFT+U) combined with nudged elastic band calculations is used to investigate polaron formation, migration, and quenching at the Fe-terminated α-Fe2O3 (0001) surface. The calculated activation energy for small-polaron hopping in bulk α-Fe2O3 is found to be 0.12 eV, in excellent agreement with experimental measurements, confirming the validity of the computational approach. Slab calculations show that migration of the polaron from bulk to the surface lowers the energy by 0.12 eV, indicating preferential localization of charge carriers at the gas-solid interface. Adsorption of NO2 induces substantial electron transfer (0.72 e-) from the oxide to the molecule, eliminating the localized Fe2+ polaron state and thereby suppressing polaronic conductivity. These results provide a direct microscopic explanation for the resistance increase of hematite-based sensors upon exposure to oxidizing gases. More broadly, the study establishes how surface adsorption can modulate charge transport α-Fe2O3 through control of polaron populations, offering design principles for improved iron oxide gas sensors.

### [22] [A Theoretical Investigation of the Thermal and Photochemical Mechanisms of Ethylbenzene Dehydrogenation on Rutile TiO$_{2}$(110)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26428)
*Nico Yannik Merkt*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本硕士论文利用DFT-PBE-D3与多参考方法（SA-CASSCF）研究了金红石TiO₂(110)表面乙苯脱氢制苯乙烯的热与光化学路径，发现表面化学计量比和光子能量通过质子耦合电子转移（PCET）或氢原子转移（HAT）机制调控反应效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工业苯乙烯生产能耗巨大，而半导体光催化可在温和条件下提供替代方案。本工作旨在从原子层面阐明乙苯在金红石TiO₂(110)表面热脱氢与光催化脱氢的反应机制，并解释文献中观测到的波长依赖现象及表面氧化对产率的影响。

Method: 采用双方法量子化学计算：使用密度泛函理论（DFT-PBE-D3）进行几何优化，使用高水平多参考方法（态平均-完全活性空间自洽场，SA-CASSCF）准确描述激发态和自由基中间体的电子结构复杂性。

Result: 在化学计量比表面上，热与光化学路径均以质子耦合电子转移（PCET）为主导；343 nm辐照导致快速弛豫至基态并遭遇高动力学势垒，而257 nm激发使体系维持在S1/T2高激发态以绕过基态决速步骤。表面氧化使机制转变为直接的氢原子转移（HAT），预吸附的氧自由基（OTi）充当“氢清除剂”，显著提高苯乙烯产率。

Conclusion: 多参考方法对于复杂表面反应的准确描述不可或缺；表面化学计量比和光子能量共同决定了光催化效率，为设计高效光催化脱氢体系提供了基础理解。

Abstract: This master's thesis investigates the thermal and photochemical dehydrogenation of ethylbenzene (EB) to styrene on the rutile TiO$_{2}$(110) surface. A dual-methodological quantum chemical approach is used for this investigation. While industrial styrene production is energy-intensive, photocatalysis on semiconductor materials offers a promising alternative under significantly milder conditions. To elucidate the underlying mechanisms, this study employs density functional theory (DFT-PBE-D3) for geometry optimization and high-level multi-reference methods (SA-CASSCF) to accurately describe the electronic complexity of excited states and radical intermediates.
  The investigation reveals that, on the stoichiometric surface, both thermal and photochemical pathways are dominated by proton-coupled electron transfer (PCET). The wavelength dependence observed in the literature is explained by how the system navigates electronic manifolds. 343 nm irradiation leads to rapid relaxation into the ground state, where high kinetic barriers persist. In contrast, 257 nm excitation enables the system to persist in higher excited states (S1/T2). This allows the reaction to bypass the rate-determining ground-state barrier.
  Furthermore, the study demonstrates that surface oxidation causes a fundamental mechanistic shift. On oxidized surfaces, pre-adsorbed oxygen radicals (O$_{Ti}$) enable direct hydrogen atom transfer (HAT), which is more efficient than PCET on reduced surfaces. This "hydrogen scavenger" effect explains the significant increase in styrene yield. This work underscores the necessity of multi-reference treatments for complex surface reactions and provides a fundamental understanding of how surface stoichiometry and photon energy govern photocatalytic efficiency.

</details>


### [23] [Geometry-Based Neural-Network Prediction of Electron Localization Function Topology in Dense Hydrogen](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26445)
*Xiaoyu Wang,Miriam Marqués,Sergio Gómez,Francesc Serratosa,Eva Zurek,Julia Contreras-García*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种机器学习框架，直接从原子几何结构预测稠密氢的电子局域化函数（ELF），无需显式电子结构计算。模型在稠密流体氢上训得高精度（R² > 0.99），并能稳健迁移至晶体氢构型，为高通量评估氢网络特性提供新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统电子结构计算（如密度泛函理论）成本高昂，难以用于高通量筛选或大规模模拟。本研究旨在绕过显式电子结构计算，通过机器学习直接从几何结构预测电子局域化函数（electron localization function, ELF），从而高效评估氢在极端条件下的键合与网络特性。

Method: 基于第一性原理（first-principles）数据训练机器学习模型，输入为纯稠密氢的原子几何结构，输出为ELF。模型覆盖多种压力范围下的稠密流体氢数据。采用实空间（real-space）与倒空间（reciprocal-space）联合分析残差，并通过迁移测试验证模型在晶体氢构型上的泛化能力。

Result: 模型在测试集上达到高精度（R² > 0.99），忠实还原ELF全局分布。残差主要由光滑的长波成分主导，其相关长度超过典型H—H键合尺度，且幅度随压力系统性地增大。模型从流体氢迁移至晶体氢时仍能保持ELF拓扑特征（如临界点和氢网络连接性）。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了一条可行的几何驱动高通量评估路径，可在流体和晶体氢中高效表征氢网络特性，无需昂贵电子结构计算。

Abstract: We develop a machine-learning framework to predict the electron localization function (ELF) of pure, dense hydrogen directly from atomic geometry, bypassing explicit electronic-structure calculations. Trained on first-principles data spanning multiple pressure regimes in dense fluid hydrogen, the model achieves high accuracy ($R^2 > 0.99$) and faithfully reproduces the global distribution of the ELF. A combined real- and reciprocal-space analysis reveals that the residual error is dominated by smooth, long-wavelength components with correlation lengths exceeding typical H--H bonding scales, and that the magnitude of these components increases systematically with pressure. Despite being trained exclusively on dense fluid hydrogen networks, the model transfers robustly to crystalline hydrogen configurations, preserving key features of ELF topology, including critical points and hydrogen-network connectivity. Taken together, these results suggest a viable route toward geometry-based, high-throughput evaluation of hydrogen-networking characteristics in both fluid and crystalline hydrogen.

### [26] [Unraveling the symmetry of Al5C3N](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26560)
*Vitalii Shtender,Chin Shen Ong,Pedro Berastegui,Olivier Donzel-Gargand,Johan Cedervall,Charles Hervoches,Premek Beran,Olle Eriksson,Ulf Jansson*

TL;DR: 本文通过单晶X射线衍射、粉末中子衍射联合精修、DFT计算和STEM分析，推翻了Al5C3N最初报道的非中心对称空间群P63mc结构，证实其实际晶体结构应为中心对称的P63/mmc空间群，并给出了新的堆叠序列 -Al2C-Al(C/N)-Al2(C/N)2-。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用多种合成路线以最大化目标相的产率和质量；应用单晶X射线衍射、粉末中子衍射联合精修、密度泛函理论（DFT）计算以及扫描透射电子显微镜（STEM）分析等多种技术手段对Al5C3N的晶体结构进行综合表征。

Abstract: The high-temperature ceramic compound Al5C3N with promising application usage belongs to the scarcely studied Al-C-N system. It was originally reported as an ordered compound in the non-centrosymmetric space group P63mc and described as a nanolaminate with an -Al2C-AlN-Al2C2- stacking sequence. The recently reported structural disorder in the related compound Al4SiC4 led us to question this proposed structure for Al5C3N and investigate the possibility of a disordered structure in the centrosymmetric space group P63/mmc. In the present work, we employed different synthesis routes to maximize the yield and quality of the desired phase, and applied a variety of techniques to probe the Al5C3N crystal structure. Our single-crystal X-ray diffraction analysis clearly indicates that the non-centrosymmetric space group P63mc must be rejected. From a joint refinement of single-crystal X-ray and powder neutron diffraction data, the occupancies of C and N were refined at two sites in P63/mmc resulting in the stacking sequence -Al2C-Al(C/N)-Al2(C/N)2-. Furthermore, DFT calculations show that a centrosymmetric disordered structure described in a supercell has the lowest energy, 0.2 eV per formula unit, relative to the previously reported P63mc structure. The calculated band structure shows both direct and indirect band gaps which lead to implications for the physical properties. Finally, STEM analysis provides additional evidence that the crystal structure of Al5C3N is better described in the centrosymmetric space group P63/mmc.

### [28] [Third-order intrinsic anomalous Hall effect as a transport fingerprint of altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26665)
*Longjun Xiang,Hao Jin,Jian Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文基于自旋群对称性分析证明，当考虑自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）时，交错磁体（altermagnets）可普遍存在三阶本征反常霍尔效应（third-order intrinsic anomalous Hall effect, third-order IAHE），并揭示了其二阶贝里曲率（second-order Berry curvature）及贝里曲率四极矩（Berry curvature quadrupole）的量子几何起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 背景是：本征反常霍尔效应（intrinsic anomalous Hall effect, IAHE）的线性和二阶响应可分别区分铁磁体和PT对称反铁磁体，而最近发现交错磁体存在三阶非本征反常霍尔效应。本文旨在探索是否存在对应的三阶本征反常霍尔效应，并验证其能否作为交错磁有序的输运诊断手段。

Method: 基于自旋群对称性分析（spin-group symmetry analysis），检查了交错磁体相关的十个自旋劳厄群（spin Laue groups）在三阶IAHE上的对称性约束；将对称性分析与由二阶贝里曲率诱导的反常速度（anomalous velocity）相结合，研究Lieb晶格交错磁体和实验已实现的V₂Se₂O中的共振行为。

Result: 在考虑SOC的情况下，三阶IAHE在交错磁体的十个自旋劳厄群中普遍允许存在；在Lieb晶格交错磁体和V₂Se₂O中，在交错磁体能带交叉（altermagnetic band crossings）附近观测到共振三阶IAHE；识别出由有限SOC激活的二阶贝里曲率所编码的贝里曲率四极矩（Berry curvature quadrupole）是这一共振的微观量子几何起源。

Conclusion: 三阶本征反常霍尔效应可作为交错磁体的本征量子几何输运指纹（intrinsic quantum geometric transport fingerprint），并将IAHE的层级体系（hierarchy of IAHE）拓展至共线量子磁体（collinear quantum magnets）领域。

Abstract: The intrinsic anomalous Hall effect (IAHE) provides a powerful transport fingerprint of quantum magnets, with its linear and second-order responses distinguishing ferromagnets and $\mathcal{P}\mathcal{T}$-symmetric antiferromagnets, respectively. Altermagnets, as an emergent class of quantum magnets, have recently been shown to host a third-order extrinsic anomalous Hall effect, raising a question of whether an \textit{intrinsic} counterpart can serve as a diagnostic of altermagnetic order. Based on spin-group symmetry analysis, we demonstrate that the third-order IAHE is generically allowed in the ten spin Laue groups relevant to altermagnets when spin-orbit coupling (SOC) is taken into account. By combining these symmetry constraints with the anomalous velocity induced by the second-order Berry curvature, we uncover a resonant third-order IAHE arising near the altermagnetic band crossings at generic momenta in both the Lieb-lattice altermagnet and the experimentally realized altermagnet V$_2$Se$_2$O. Notably, we identify the Berry curvature quadrupole, encoded in the second-order Berry curvature and activated by finite SOC, as the microscopic quantum geometric origin of this resonance. Our results establish the third-order IAHE as an intrinsic quantum geometric transport fingerprint of altermagnets and extend the hierarchy of IAHE across collinear quantum magnets.

### [29] [Emergent surface resonance from charge density wave symmetry breaking in TiSe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26685)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Here, we show that charge density wave (CDW) symmetry breaking can yield a surface states in 1T-TiSe2. Micro angle resolved photoemission spectroscopy resolves a sharp, two dimensional surface resonant state (SRS) that emerges within the CDW reconstructed low energy spectrum. The SRS exhibits notable temperature dependence and its spectral weight collapses around 160 K, while CDW transition temperature TCDW is commonly reported as 202 K. Slab DFT+U calculations reproduce a surface localized resonance when CDW folding brings valence and conduction states into near degeneracy, suggesting a correlation tuned, surface selective origin. These results point to a form of correlation-tuned surface resonance in a layered CDW compound and suggest a framework for engineering low dimensional quantum states in van der Waals materials via symmetry breaking and electronic structure tuning.

### [30] [Predicting massive helium-3 release from metal tritides using simple mechanical modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26697)
*Berengere Evin,Dorian Gaboriau,Mathieu Segard,Sylvain Challet,Arnaud Fabre,Stephanie Thiebaut*

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于位错阻塞（dislocation blocking）机制的简单有效模型，用以解释金属氚化物（metal tritides）在氚老化（tritium aging）过程中长期滞留氦-3后突然大量释放的现象。该机制结合力学与微观结构方法，计算结果与老化后的钯氚化物（palladium tritide）实验数据吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金属氚化物在氚老化过程中，氦-3（helium-3）会先被滞留数年，随后突然大量释放，其背后的物理机制尚不明确。现有解释缺乏能够涵盖这种突变行为的统一模型。

Method: 提出位错阻塞（dislocation blocking）假设作为核心机制，并采用力学（mechanical）与微观结构（microstructural）相结合的方法对现象进行建模。

Result: 基于该机制的计算结果与老化的钯氚化物（aged palladium tritide）的所有老化数据吻合。

Conclusion: 位错阻塞机制能够有效解释金属氚化物中氦-3的延迟释放行为，且模型具有较好的实验验证基础。

Abstract: This letter is presenting a simple but effective mechanism that explains why ,during tritium aging, metal tritides retain most helium-3 for years and then suddenly release massive amount. The mechanism is based on the hypothesis that dislocations blocking could explain the sudden change of behavior. The modeling of this phenomenon combine a mechanical and microstructural approach. The calculations made with this mechanism fit all the aging data acquired on aged palladium tritide

</details>


### [31] [A self-evolving agent for explainable diagnosis of DFT-experiment band-gap mismatch](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26703)
*Yue Li,Bijun Tang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出XDFT，一个闭环智能体，自动诊断标准密度泛函理论（DFT）预测与实验不符的电子基态；在124种材料的基准测试中，对90个错配案例中的70个（78%）成功识别出解析机制，性能远超随机基线（19%）和静态大语言模型排序（20%），并将已解决的案例归纳为一个三分元素分类法和一条四行静态规则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）对关联性和结构复杂的化合物的电子基态预测常出现错误，将实验报告的半导体误判为金属。这些错配通常源于计算中未纳入的特定非理想因素（如磁有序、电子关联、替代多晶型或缺陷），但大规模自动提取这些信号仍依赖手动操作。

Method: XDFT是一个闭环智能体，通过三个步骤自动诊断错配：从策划好的目录中抽取候选假设，执行相应的第一性原理（first-principles）测试，并根据每个判定结果更新关于假设有用性的全局贝叶斯后验（Bayesian posterior）。

Result: 在包含124种材料的验证基准上，XDFT成功解析了90个错配案例中的70个（78%），性能高出均匀随机基线（19%）和静态大语言模型排序（20%）一个数量级。内部后验与基准时间线上的实验经验性能保持一致；已解决案例可归纳为三分元素分类法（tri-partite element-class taxonomy）及一条四行静态规则。

Conclusion: XDFT的每个诊断材料都附带修正后的计算协议和机制归因；未能解决的案例则作为有证据支持的靶标用于实验重新检验。

Abstract: Standard density functional theory (DFT) routinely misclassifies the electronic ground state of correlated and structurally complex compounds, predicting metallic behaviour for materials that experiments report as semiconductors. Each such mismatch encodes a specific non-ideality -- magnetic ordering, electron correlation, an alternative polymorph, or a defect -- that the calculation excluded, but extracting that signal at scale has remained a manual exercise. Here we introduce XDFT, a closed-loop agent that diagnoses the mismatch automatically: it draws candidate hypotheses from a curated catalogue, executes the corresponding first-principles tests, and updates a global Bayesian posterior over hypothesis usefulness from each verdict. On a verified benchmark of 124 materials, XDFT identifies a resolving mechanism for 70 of 90 mismatch cases (78\%), an order of magnitude above a uniform-random baseline (19\%) and a static LLM ordering (20\%). The internal posterior aligns with empirical performance over the benchmark timeline, and resolved cases collapse into a tri-partite element-class taxonomy that we distil into a four-line static rule. Each diagnosed material is returned with a corrected protocol and a mechanistic attribution; failed cases are flagged as evidence-backed targets for experimental re-examination.

</details>


### [32] [Tracking visible pulsed laser annealing of Hf0.5Zr0.5O2 heterostructures with in situ transmission electron microscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26718)
*Aida Amini,Shruti Verma,Katharina Kohlmann,Sebastian Obernberger,Jean-Christof Lamanque,Andreas Rüdiger,Kenneth R. Beyerlein*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过可见纳秒激光退火（visible nanosecond laser annealing）技术，在模拟CMOS器件结构的Si3N4/TiN/Hf0.5Zr0.5O2薄膜异质结构中实现了铪锆氧化物（HZO）的铁电正交相结晶。利用局部原位透射电镜测量和有限元模拟，量化了HZO薄膜厚度、临界激光能量密度与铁电相分数之间的关系，发现激光脉冲能量存在尖锐阈值行为。最佳条件（8 nm HZO膜, 单脉冲177 mJ/cm²）可获得86%的铁电正交相，并揭示了氮化硅基底部分熔融对温度限制（1900 °C）的关键作用，支持了涉及四方相的动力学结晶路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激光退火（laser annealing）为后端工艺（back end of the line）制备基于HZO的铁电薄膜晶体管提供了一条有前景的路线。由于HZO带隙宽，已有研究多采用紫外或红外光结晶，但鲜有利用可见光且模拟实际CMOS器件结构的工作，因此本研究旨在探索可见光脉冲在典型器件异质结构中的结晶行为与机制。

Method: 采用可见纳秒激光脉冲辐照Si3N4/TiN/Hf0.5Zr0.5O2薄膜异质结构，利用TiN在可见光波段的吸收产生结晶所需热量；通过改进型透射电子显微镜进行局部原位测量，并结合有限元模拟（finite element simulation）揭示热传递动力学。

Result: HZO薄膜厚度、临界激光能量密度与铁电HZO相分数之间存在量化关系，激光脉冲能量呈现尖锐阈值行为；最佳条件为8 nm HZO薄膜经单脉冲177 mJ/cm²辐照，可获得86%的铁电正交相（ferroelectric orthorhombic phase）。有限元模拟表明氮化硅基底的部分熔融将温度限制在1900 °C，这一发现与脉冲能量阈值行为共同支持了涉及四方相（tetragonal phase）的动力学结晶路径。

Conclusion: 激光驱动的相工程（laser-driven phase engineering）能够实现铁电材料的可扩展设计（scalable design）并提升其在先进电子应用中的性能。研究结果揭示了可见纳秒激光退火中HZO结晶的关键物理机制，为后端兼容的铁电器件制备提供了重要指导。

Abstract: Laser annealing offers a promising route to back end of the line fabrication of ferroelectric thin film transistors based on hafnium-zirconium oxide (HZO). Due to the wide band gap of this material, previous reports have studied the crystallization of HZO using ultraviolet or infrared light. In contrast, we monitor its crystallization in a Si3N4/TiN/Hf0.5Zr0.5O2 thin film heterostructure upon irradiation with visible nanosecond laser pulses. This geometry mimics the structure of CMOS devices and harnesses the absorption of TiN in the visible regime to generate the heat necessary for the transformation. Through a series of local in situ measurements using a modified transmission electron microscope, we quantify the relationship between the HZO film thickness, critical laser energy density and the ferroelectric HZO phase fraction, finding a sharp threshold behavior in the laser pulse energy necessary to crystallize HZO. The optimal condition of irradiating an 8-nm HZO film with a single laser pulse with an energy density of 177 mJ/cm2 is found to produce 86% of the ferroelectric orthorhombic phase. Heat transfer dynamics within the heterostructure during laser annealing are revealed by finite element simulations, where the partial melting of the silicon nitride substrate is found to play an important role limiting the temperature to 1900 °C. This finding as well as the observed laser pulse energy threshold behavior support a kinetic crystallization pathway involving the tetragonal phase. More generally, these findings show how laser-driven phase engineering can lead to scalable design and enhanced performance of ferroelectric materials in advanced electronic applications.

### [33] [Resolving growth-induced off-stoichiometry in AgCrSe$_2$ single crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26887)
*Felix Eder,Zeno Maesen,Yurii Skourski,Enrico Giannini,Oksana Zaharko,Fabian O. von Rohr*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过元素分析、单晶X射线衍射和磁化测量，证实化学气相传输法生长的AgCrSe₂单晶普遍存在非化学计量比（Ag₁₋ₓCr(Se₂₋ᵧClᵧ)，x≈y≈0.08），并因此导致奈尔温度从58 K降至46 K；通过优化Ag/Se自助熔剂法，获得了恢复化学计量比和本征磁性质的大尺寸单晶，为重新评估该材料中异常输运现象的起源提供了可靠平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AgCrSe₂是一种层状三角晶格反铁磁体（layered delafossite-like antiferromagnet），高温下为超离子导体，低温下被报道存在反常霍尔行为（anomalous Hall behavior）和近藤物理（Kondo physics），但这些异常输运现象的报道几乎全部基于化学气相传输法（chemical vapor transport, CVT）生长的单晶，因此需要检验生长诱导的非化学计量比（off-stoichiometry）是否对这些现象产生了影响。

Method: 采用元素分析（elemental analysis）、单晶X射线衍射（single-crystal X-ray diffraction）和磁化测量（magnetization measurements）表征CVT法生长晶体的成分与磁性；同时优化Ag/Se自助熔剂法（self-flux growth method）制备大尺寸单晶，并与固相合成（solid-state synthesis）制备的化学计量比多晶样品进行对比。

Result: CVT法晶体普遍存在非化学计量比，成分为Ag₁₋ₓCr(Se₂₋ᵧClᵧ)（x≈y≈0.08），源于使用CrCl₃作为传输剂（transport agent）；该非化学计量比导致奈尔温度（Néel temperature）从58 K（化学计量比多晶样品）降至46 K。采用Ag/Se自助熔剂法生长的大尺寸单晶恢复了化学计量比多晶样品的磁转变温度和饱和场（saturation field）。

Conclusion: 自助熔剂法是获得高质量化学计量比AgCrSe₂单晶的有效途径，为重新评估已报道的反常输运现象是内禀性质（intrinsic）还是源于非化学计量比提供了可靠的材料平台。

Abstract: The layered delafossite-like antiferromagnet AgCrSe$_2$ is a superionic conductor at high temperatures and has been reported to exhibit anomalous Hall behavior and Kondo physics at low temperatures. These extraordinary transport properties have been established almost exclusively on single crystals grown by chemical vapor transport, raising questions about the role of growth-induced off-stoichiometry. Using elemental analysis, single-crystal X-ray diffraction, and magnetization measurements, we show that such crystals are indeed systematically off-stoichiometric, with a general composition of Ag$_{1-x}$Cr(Se$_{2-y}$Cl$_y$) ($x \approx y \approx 0.08$) arising from the use of CrCl$_3$ as a transport agent. This off-stoichiometry manifests in altered magnetic properties, most notably a suppressed Néel temperature of 46\,K compared to 58\,K in stoichiometric polycrystalline samples prepared by solid-state synthesis. By optimizing an Ag/Se self-flux growth method, we obtained large single crystals of AgCrSe$_2$ that recover the magnetic transition temperature and saturation field of stoichiometric powder samples. These results establish self-flux growth as a route to high-quality stoichiometric AgCrSe$_2$ single crystals and provide a reliable platform for reassessing whether the reported anomalous transport phenomena are intrinsic or arise from off-stoichiometry.

### [34] [Brane quantization and SYZ mirror symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26292)
*Kwokwai Chan,Naichung Conan Leung,Qin Li,Yat-Hin Suen,Yutung Yau*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文通过SYZ镜像对称（SYZ mirror symmetry）为共余切A-膜（coisotropic A-brane）建立了严格的数学框架，证明了其自同态代数与镜像B-侧自同态代数同构，并完整实现了Gukov–Witten的膜量子化（brane quantization）方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kapustin–Orlov引入的共余切A-膜虽在Fukaya范畴（Fukaya category）扩展和同调镜像对称（homological mirror symmetry）中具有重要理论意义，但其严格的范畴框架尚未建立。同时，Gukov–Witten的膜量子化方案预言了全纯形变量子化（holomorphic deformation quantization）与共余切A-膜自同态代数的关联，但缺乏严格的数学实现。

Method: 考虑具有SYZ纤维化（SYZ fibration）的全纯辛流形（holomorphic symplectic manifold），通过SYZ变换将半仿射、空间填充（space-filling）的共余切A-膜B_cc镜像构造为B-侧B-膜B̌_cc。通过构造一个特殊的非形式全纯形变量子化来数学定义自同态代数Hom_A(B_cc,B_cc)，并利用扭族Toeplitz构造（twisted family Toeplitz construction）将其映射到镜像B-侧，证明自同态代数之间的同构。

Result: 建立了Hom_A(B_cc,B_cc) ≅ Hom_B(B̌_cc,B̌_cc)的自同态代数同构；以环面纤维作为Lagrangian A-膜B时，完全实现了Gukov–Witten的膜量子化方案，即Hom_A(B_cc,B_cc)在Hom_A(B,B_cc)上的自然作用与镜像B-侧的自然作用恰好对应。

Conclusion: 该工作为共余切A-膜提供了与Gukov–Witten膜量子化方案、SYZ镜像对称以及族Floer理论（family Floer theory）兼容的统一数学框架。

Abstract: Coisotropic A-branes were introduced by Kapustin--Orlov to enlarge the Fukaya category of a symplectic manifold in a way that aligns with predictions from homological mirror symmetry. From a mathematical perspective, however, the categorical framework governing such branes remains largely undeveloped. On the other hand, Gukov--Witten's brane quantization suggests that a holomorphic deformation quantization of a holomorphic symplectic manifold $X$ arises from the endomorphism algebra $Hom_A(B_{cc},B_{cc})$ of a canonical coisotropic A-brane $B_{cc}$, which naturally acts on the morphism space $Hom_A(B,B_{cc})$ with a Lagrangian A-brane $B$ that in turn gives precisely the geometric quantization of $B$.
  In this paper, we consider a holomorphic symplectic manifold $X$ which admits an SYZ fibration and apply SYZ mirror symmetry to study its brane quantization. Given any semi-affine, space-filling coisotropic A-brane $B_{cc}$ on $X$, we construct the mirror B-brane $\check{B}_{cc}$ on the mirror manifold $\check{X}$ by an SYZ transform. We then present a mathematical definition of the endomorphism algebra $Hom_A(B_{cc},B_{cc})$ by constructing a distinguished non-formal holomorphic deformation quantization of $X$. Using a twisted family Toeplitz construction, we transform $Hom_A(B_{cc},B_{cc})$ to the mirror B-side and prove that this induces an isomorphism $Hom_A(B_{cc},B_{cc})\cong Hom_B(\check{B}_{cc},\check{B}_{cc})$ between the endomorphism algebras. Furthermore, taking any torus fiber of $X$ as the Lagrangian A-brane $B$, we fully realize Gukov--Witten's proposal, namely, there is a natural action of $Hom_A(B_{cc},B_{cc})$ on $Hom_A(B,B_{cc})$ which is precisely mirror to the natural action on the mirror B-side. This provides a mathematical framework which is compatible with Gukov--Witten's brane quantization proposal, SYZ mirror symmetry as well as family Floer theory.

</details>

### [36] [Strong-field signatures of a regular black hole in an Einasto dark matter halo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25961)
*Mohsen Fathi,Faizuddin Ahmed*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了由Einasto暗物质（DM）分布支持的静态球对称规则黑洞的强场现象学，发现该类黑洞的光子层尺度、阴影直径和残余光学结构对暗物质晕参数最为敏感，而类时轨道观测量的简并性较强；EHT阴影尺度测量表明整个分支与Sgr A*在1σ置信水平内一致，而M87*略微排斥接近临界值的参数区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Einasto暗物质（DM）分布所形成的规则黑洞在强场区域的可观测现象，识别哪些观测量对暗物质晕参数最为敏感，从而为未来通过天文观测检验暗物质黑洞模型提供理论依据。

Method: 基于Einasto指数型暗物质密度轮廓构建静态球对称规则黑洞，引入单一无量纲晕参数a（限制在黑洞分支0<a≤a_crit≈0.388）；通过求解类时与零测地线（包括有效势、圆轨道、ISCO半径、轨道周期、近星点进动、光子球、阴影半径、有效光子力及代表性光子轨迹），并在静态发射体近似下构建像面强度分布和正面对薄盘图像。

Result: 强场敏感性呈现层次结构：类时可观测量在大部分黑洞分支上与Schwarzschild极限高度简并；光子球尺度、阴影直径及残余光学结构在接近临界黑洞区域时对Einasto晕的响应最为敏感；与EHT阴影尺度测量的对比显示，整个参数分支与Sgr A*在1σ置信水平内一致，而M87*略微排斥接近临界值的参数。

Conclusion: Einasto暗物质晕最有可能的观测信号并非来自普通的类时轨道量，而是来自近临界光子传播及其光学表现，这为未来利用甚长基线干涉（VLBI）观测检验暗物质黑洞模型指明了优先方向。

Abstract: We investigate the strong-field phenomenology of a static and spherically symmetric regular black hole supported by an Einasto dark matter (DM) distribution. For the exponential Einasto profile, the geometry is controlled by a single dimensionless halo parameter $a$, and we restrict the analysis to the black hole branch $0<a\leq a_{\rm crit}\simeq0.388$. We study both timelike and null geodesics, including the effective potential, circular orbits, ISCO radius, orbital period, periapsis advance, photon sphere, shadow radius, effective photon force, and representative photon trajectories. We also construct image-plane intensity profiles and face-on thin-disk images in a static-emitter approximation. The analysis reveals a hierarchy of strong-field sensitivity. Timelike observables remain largely degenerate with the Schwarzschild limit along most of the black hole branch, while the photon sphere scale, shadow diameter, and residual optical structures provide the most sensitive response to the Einasto halo near the critical black hole regime. A comparison with the EHT shadow-scale measurements shows that the full branch is consistent with Sgr A* at the $1σ$ level, whereas M87* mildly disfavors values very close to criticality. These results indicate that the most promising signatures of the Einasto halo are not expected from ordinary timelike orbital quantities, but from near-critical photon propagation and its imprint on the optical appearance.

### [37] [Parameter-estimation bias induced by transient orbital resonances in extreme-mass-ratio inspirals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26011)
*Edoardo Levati,Alejandro Cárdenas-Avendaño*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本工作利用Fisher矩阵方法研究了极端质量比旋近（extreme-mass-ratio inspiral, EMRI）中暂态轨道共振对参数估计的影响，发现忽略共振效应会导致信噪比显著损失和参数反演偏差，且共振对运动积分修正的符号和幅度必须精确建模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相对论性轨道具有多频特征，暂态轨道共振（transient orbital resonances）在EMRI中普遍存在，会改变轨道动力学并引起引力波相位偏移，可能影响EMRI源的探测和参数估计精度，因此需要量化共振造成的参数反演偏差。

Method: 采用Fisher矩阵方法，分析暂态轨道共振对EMRI参数估计引入的偏差；重点关注动力学上最重要的低阶共振3:2和2:1，以及高阶次主导共振3:1和4:3。

Result: 对大多数被考察轨道而言，忽略共振穿越（resonance crossing）效应会导致信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio）显著损失，并在参数反演中引入偏差；共振对运动积分（integrals of motion）修正的符号和幅度对结果起关键作用。

Conclusion: 未能精确建模暂态轨道共振会阻碍EMRI的探测和参数估计，从而限制其科学潜力；进一步证实了共振建模的重要性。

Abstract: Given the multi-frequency nature of relativistic orbits, transient orbital resonances are expected to be ubiquitous during an extreme-mass-ratio inspiral (EMRI). At a resonance, the orbital dynamics is modified in a nontrivial way, imprinting an overall dephasing in the emitted gravitational waves and potentially impacting both the detection and parameter estimation of these sources. In this work, using a Fisher-matrix approach, we investigate the bias induced by transient orbital resonances in EMRI parameter estimation. We focus on the most dynamically significant low-order resonances, 3 : 2 and 2 : 1, as well as on the high-order, subdominant resonances 3 : 1 and 4 : 3. We find that, for most of the orbits considered, neglecting the effect of a resonance crossing leads to significant losses in signal-to-noise ratio and induces bias in parameter recovery. Furthermore, both the sign and the amplitude of the resonance-induced modifications to the integrals of motion play a crucial role and must be modeled accurately. Our results provide further evidence that failing to model transient orbital resonances accurately can hinder EMRI detection and parameter estimation, thereby limiting their scientific potential.

</details>


### [38] [Inflationary Scenarios in $f(Q,φ)$ Gravity with Scalar Field Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26156)
*F. Mavoa,M. B. Barry,R. Ndioukane,M. G. Ganiou,F. K. Ahloui*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在修正的 $f(Q,φ)$ 引力框架下研究了暴胀场景，重点分析了标量场与非度规标量之间的非最小耦合参数 ξ 对暴胀可观测量（标量谱指数 $n_s$ 和张量-标量比 $r$）的影响。结果表明，De Sitter 暴胀仅在 $10^{-3} \lesssim ξ\lesssim 10^{-2}$ 的窄区间内与 Planck 数据兼容；而 Cosh 型暴胀模型在 $N=60$ 时预测 $n_s \approx 0.965-0.967$ 且 $r \approx 0.017-0.018$，与当前观测约束高度吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在修正 $f(Q,φ)$ 引力框架下，非最小耦合（nonminimal coupling）对暴胀动力学的具体影响尚未被系统研究。本文旨在探索耦合参数 ξ 如何改变暴胀可观测量，并判断哪些模型参数区间能与 Planck 等宇宙学观测数据兼容。

Method: 采用修正 $f(Q,φ)$ 引力理论，引入标量场与非度规标量之间的非最小耦合项；分别对 De Sitter 暴胀和 Cosh 型暴胀两种场景进行解析与数值分析，计算标量谱指数 $n_s$ 和张量-标量比 $r$ 随耦合参数 ξ 或 e-fold 数 $N$ 的变化。

Result: 对于 De Sitter 暴胀，$n_s$ 随 ξ 增加而增大，$r$ 则减小，与 Planck 数据兼容的耦合参数区间为 $10^{-3} \lesssim ξ\lesssim 10^{-2}$；超出此范围会预测过大的张量模式（tensor modes）或非物理的蓝倾斜谱（blue-tilted spectrum）。一致性约束给出上界 $ξ< κ/(2p)$，对于 $κ=1,\ p=60$ 即 $ξ<0.00833$，偏好区域约为 $ξ\sim\mathcal{O}(10^{-3})$。对于 Cosh 型暴胀，$r$ 随 $N$ 增加而减小，$n_s$ 增加；当 $N=60$ 时，预测 $n_s \approx 0.965-0.967,\ r \approx 0.017-0.018$，与观测高度一致。

Conclusion: 非最小耦合在塑造暴胀动力学（inflationary dynamics）中起着关键作用，只有特定的耦合参数范围才能确保模型与宇宙学观测相容。Cosh 型暴胀模型为描述暴胀提供了一致且稳健的理论框架。

Abstract: In this work, we investigated several inflationary scenarios within the framework of modified $f(Q,φ)$ gravity with a nonminimal coupling between the scalar field and the nonmetricity scalar. We focused on the impact of the coupling parameter $ξ$ on the inflationary observables, namely the scalar spectral index $n_s$ and the tensor-to-scalar ratio $r$. In the case of De Sitter inflation, we showed that the model can reproduce observationally viable predictions only within a restricted range of the coupling parameter. Specifically, we found that $n_s$ increases with $ξ$, while $r$ decreases, leading to a narrow allowed region $10^{-3} \lesssim ξ\lesssim 10^{-2}$ compatible with Planck data. Outside this range, the model either predicts excessively large tensor modes or an unphysical blue-tilted spectrum. We also derived theoretical constraints on $ξ$ from the consistency of the model, leading to an upper bound $ξ< \fracκ{2p}$. For $κ= 1$ and $p = 60$, this implies $ξ< 0.00833$, with a preferred region around $ξ\sim \mathcal{O}(10^{-3})$. Furthermore, we analyzed the Cosh-type inflationary model and showed that it provides a robust and consistent description of inflation. In this case, the tensor-to-scalar ratio decreases while the scalar spectral index increases with the number of e-folds $N$. For $N = 60$, the model predicts $n_s \approx 0.965 - 0.967, \qquad r \approx 0.017 - 0.018$, in excellent agreement with current observational constraints. Overall, our results highlight the crucial role of the nonminimal coupling in shaping the inflationary dynamics and ensuring compatibility with cosmological observations.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究高维正则黑洞（regular black hole）在准拓扑引力（quasi-topological gravity）中的电磁扰动吸收特性，特别关注高曲率修正和额外维度如何影响散射与吸收过程，从而为检验高阶引力理论提供可观测信号。

Method: 采用基于WKB近似的灰体因子计算方法，在四维膜（four-dimensional brane）上考察高维正则黑洞背景下的电磁微扰传播，分析吸收截面随频率、维度和曲率修正的变化。

Result: 正则性效应使吸收谱相对于奇异Tangherlini解（singular Tangherlini solution）发生系统性的偏移，并改变有效光子球半径；增加时空维度会抑制这些偏离，减少收敛所需的多极数（multipoles）。高频区域吸收截面趋近几何光学极限（geometric-optics limit），低频区域则因透射概率降低而显著抑制。

Conclusion: 正则性与高曲率效应的相互作用在吸收特征中留下独特印记，可作为探测底层引力理论的灵敏探针。

Abstract: We investigate the absorption cross sections of electromagnetic perturbations propagating on a four-dimensional brane in the background of higher-dimensional regular black holes arising in quasi-topological gravity. Employing a WKB-based approach for the computation of greybody factors, we analyze the impact of higher-curvature corrections and spacetime dimensionality on the scattering properties of the system. We show that regularity effects lead to systematic deviations from the singular Tangherlini solution, manifested in shifts of the absorption spectrum and modifications of the effective photon sphere radius. Increasing the number of spacetime dimensions suppresses these deviations, driving the system toward the classical limit and reducing the number of multipoles required for convergence. In the high-frequency regime, the absorption cross section approaches the geometric-optics limit, while at low frequencies it is strongly suppressed due to diminished transmission probabilities. Our results demonstrate that the interplay between regularity and higher-curvature effects leaves distinct imprints on the absorption characteristics, providing a sensitive probe of the underlying gravitational theory.

### [40] [Trapping, Irregular Waveforms, and Efficient Radiation in Ultra-relativistic Black Hole Encounters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26253)
*Hengrui Zhu,Frans Pretorius,James M. Stone*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过数值相对论模拟，发现超相对论黑洞相遇会进入广义相对论二体相互作用的新区间，其波形偏离了标准的后牛顿描写向准正则环降的平滑过渡，表现出延长的不规则发射和显著的水平吸收，且辐射引力波能量占比超过65%，远高于此前基于低加速数据的预估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示超相对论黑洞相遇中尚未被认知的二体相互作用新机制，挑战传统的后牛顿（post-Newtonian）描写与准正则环降（Kerr ringdown）平滑过渡的预期。

Method: 采用数值相对论（numerical relativity）方法，演化等质量、无自旋黑洞系统，初始质心洛伦兹因子（Lorentz factor）γ 最高约5.1，并在非零碰撞参数下分析波形与能量辐射。

Result: 在非零碰撞参数下，系统表现出延长且高度不规则的引力波发射以及显著的事件视界吸收，即使不发生并合；当γ≈5.1时，超过65%的初始ADM能量以引力波形式辐射，显著高于从低加速数据外推得到的预估。

Conclusion: 超相对论黑洞相遇引发的异常现象由瞬态零测地线束缚（transient null trapping）和辐射在双星相互作用区域内的重复透镜效应（repeated lensing）驱动，表明该过程进入了广义相对论二体相互作用的新区间。

Abstract: We demonstrate that ultra-relativistic black hole encounters reveal a new regime of the two-body interaction in general relativity. Evolving equal-mass, nonspinning black holes with initial center-of-mass Lorentz factors up to $γ\approx 5.1$ using numerical relativity, we find that the resulting waveforms defy the standard expectation of a post-Newtonian description followed by a smooth transition to a prompt Kerr ringdown. Instead, at nonzero impact parameter, the system can exhibit prolonged, highly irregular emission and significant horizon absorption, even without coalescence. We show these phenomena are driven by transient null trapping and repeated lensing of radiation in the binary interaction region. Furthermore, our simulations indicate that over $65\%$ of the initial ADM energy can be radiated as gravitational waves at $γ\approx 5.1$, which is substantially larger than previously estimated by extrapolating from lower boost data.
