### [41] [Quantum Probe to the Higher Dimensional Yang-Mills Singularity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26350)
*M. Mangut,O. Gurtug,M. Halilsoy*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文运用霍罗威茨-马罗夫（Horowitz-Marolf）判据研究爱因斯坦-杨-米尔斯（EYM）理论中裸曲率奇点的量子性质，发现仅EYM和爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-杨-米尔斯（EMYM）时空在量子力学上保持奇性；加入高斯-博内（Gauss-Bonnet, GB）高阶曲率修正后，在D=5维且特定质量参数m下奇点可被量子力学正则化，但在D≥6维时仅外部（次级）奇点可被修复，中心奇点仍保持量子奇异性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典广义相对论中裸奇点的存在引发了因果性和可预测性问题，而量子引力可能从根本上改变奇点的性质。该研究旨在通过量子场在奇点附近演化的行为，判断爱因斯坦-杨-米尔斯理论中的裸曲率奇点是否可被量子力学“治愈”。

Method: 采用霍罗威茨-马罗夫（Horowitz-Marolf）判据，通过分析量子标量场在奇点附近的时间演化来评估奇点的量子力学奇异性（quantum singularity）。研究对象包括纯杨-米尔斯（Yang-Mills）和爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-杨-米尔斯（Einstein-Maxwell-Yang-Mills, EMYM）解，并进一步引入高斯-博内（Gauss-Bonnet, GB）高阶曲率修正项。

Result: EYM和EMYM时空在量子力学上保持奇性。加入GB修正后，在D=5维时空下，对于与杨-米尔斯荷Q相关的特定质量参数m，奇点可以变得量子力学正则；而在D≥6维时空下，仅外部（次级）奇点在特定m值下可被修复，中心奇点（central singularity）仍保持量子奇异性。特别地，GB修正中平方根内部的正性要求可能产生次级奇点（secondary singularity），需仔细审查。

Conclusion: 高阶曲率修正（GB项）能够在一定程度上缓解EYM理论中裸奇点的量子奇异性，但这种缓解效果依赖于时空维度和质量参数：仅在D=5维下可完全正则化，在更高维下中心奇点仍无法被量子力学的演化所消除。

Abstract: We investigate the quantum nature of naked curvature singularities in Einstein-Yang-Mills (EYM) theory using the Horowitz-Marolf (HM) criterion, which assesses quantum singularities via the evolution of quantum scalar fields. Focusing on timelike singularities in spacetime dimension $ D \geq 5 $, we analyze both pure Yang-Mills and Einstein-Maxwell-Yang-Mills (EMYM) solutions. We then incorporate higher curvature corrections through Gauss-Bonnet (GB) terms. From positivity requirement the expression under square root that arises in GB may create a secondary singularity that shall be scrutinized carefully. Our analysis reveals that while EYM and EMYM spacetimes remain quantum mechanically singular, the inclusion of GB corrections can, in general, render the singularity quantum mechanically regular for specific values of the mass parameter $m$, which is related to the YM charge $Q$ in $ D = 5 $ space-time dimensions. Contrary, for space-time dimension $D \geq 6$, although the outer (secondary) singularity may be healed quantum mechanically for certain values of the mass parameter $m$, the central singularity remains quantum mechanically singular.

### [42] [Thermodynamic properties of the Kerr Black-hole in non-linear electrodynamics with cosmological constant](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26586)
*Vinayak S. Pawar,Siba Prasad Das*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究了在非线性电动力学（NLED）背景下，包含宇宙学常数（Λ）的缓慢旋转磁荷Kerr黑洞的热力学性质，包括温度（T）、角速度（Ω_h）和熵（S），并分析了视界结构及其依赖参数。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先计算非线性电磁磁荷密度ρ_{NLED}(r)以得到磁质量；随后在a-M平面上利用鲨鱼鳍图（sharkfin diagram）展示允许参数空间，并分析视界函数Δ(r)的零点，识别内（Cauchy）、外（Event）和宇宙（cosmological）视界；最后数值计算温度（T）、角速度（Ω_h）和熵（S）三个热力学参数。

Result: 质量剖面M(r)在r接近宇宙学尺度L（L²=±Λ/3）处达到平台（plateau），与磁荷q_m和非线性参数β的组合无关；视界结构依赖于旋转参数a、宇宙学尺度L及质量剖面M(r)；三维热力学参数在不同视界表面的数值被列表呈现。

Conclusion: 非线性电动力学（NLED）与宇宙学常数（Λ）会显著修正缓慢旋转Kerr黑洞的内部结构与热力学性质。

Abstract: We study thermodynamic properties, in particular the Temperature~(T), Angular velocity~($Ω_h$) and Entropy~(S) of the of magnetically charged slowly rotating (with rotation parameter $a \lsim 0.10$) Kerr black-hole(BH) with the inclusion of cosmological constant ($Λ$) in the background of nonlinear electrodynamics (NLED). At first we calculated the nonlinear electromagnetic magnetic charged density $ρ_{NLED}$$(r)$ which is needed to calculate the magnetic mass of the slowly rotating Kerr-BH. We showed the mass profile $M(r)$ of the BH for different combinations of magnetic charges~($q_m$) and non-linear parameter ($β$) presence in the Lagrangian density. We found that $M(r)$ attains a plateau for values of $r$ close to the the cosmological length~($L$), where $L^2$= $\pm \fracΛ{3}$, irrespective of the combinations of $q_m$ and $β$. The $\pm$ sign corresponds to the de-Sitter(dS) and Anti-de-Sitter(AdS) respectively. Afterwards we showed the allowed parameter spaces in $a$-$M$ plane using sharkfin diagram for different values of $L$ with positive values of the horizon function, $Δ(r)$, and explain the extremal criterion and asymptotic limit. We showed the values of $r$ where the horizon function of the quadratic polynomials becomes zero and called them as the inner(Cauchy), outer(Event) and large cosmological horizons with different values of $a$. We showed that the horizon structure depends on $a$, $L$ and the mass profile $M(r)$. Finally, we tabulated the numerical values of three thermodynamic parameter, i.e., $T$, $Ω_h$ and $S$ at those horizons surfaces. Our results demonstrate that NLED with cosmological constant significantly modifies both the internal structure and thermodynamic properties of Kerr-BH.

### [43] [Causal structure of black holes immersed in a Chaplygin-like dark fluid environment: Horizons and singularities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26681)

Abstract: In the present work, we study the causal structure of spherically symmetric black holes immersed in a Chaplygin-like dark fluid, emphasizing the impact of the fluid parameters on curvature and horizon formation. We show that the spacetime curvature is significantly stronger than in its similar counterpart, the Reissner-Nordstrom-de Sitter geometry with the same mass and charge, leading to modifications of the internal causal structure. For the presence of horizons the Chaplygin black hole possesses an upper bound $Q \approx 0.556219 M$, which is much smaller than that for Reissner-Nordstrom spacetime $Q_{\text{critical}} = M$ or of the Reissner-Nordstrom-de Sitter case $Q_{\text{critical}} = 3M/(2\sqrt{2})$, indicating that the black holes immersed in a Chaplygin-like dark fluid reach the extremal regime more easily. ### [44] [Finite-Window Centered Organization of Neighboring Poles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26725)
*Yuye Wu,Hong-Bo Jin*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文指出在开放波系统（open-wave systems）中，当两个相邻复频率共振极（resonance poles）近乎简并时，在有限观测窗口下信号表现为公共载波（carrier）叠加缓慢变化的干涉包络（interference envelope），而非两个独立阻尼正弦之和。作者证明这种“载波加一阶射流（carrier-plus-first-jet）”结构普遍源自近简并极点对，并建立了一个有限窗口下的双尺度层级（two-scale hierarchy），以 Kerr 准正则模（quasinormal modes）作为引力实例验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波振铃（ringdown）等开放波系统中常出现近简并共振极点（near-degenerate resonance poles），即两个相邻模式的复频率几乎相同。在有限观测窗口上，若将波形视为两个独立阻尼正弦之和，数值拟合会不稳定，需要更自然的分析框架来描述这种近简并情形。

Method: 数学上，精确极点合并导致双极点（double pole）和约当链（Jordan-chain）时间依赖（含 $t e^{-i\omega t}$ 因子）。本文将这一结构推广至近简并极点对，指出在有限窗口下无需真正的极点合并即可出现相同的“载波加一阶射流”形式；并提出以共享载波为中心的“中心化两极点块（centered two-pole block）”组织局部响应。

Result: 建立了一个有限窗口下的双尺度层级：$\kappa$ 控制何时必须引入载波的领头修正，$\eta^2$ 控制在引入该修正后的剩余误差。二维极点的数值实验验证了该标度行为，Kerr 时空的准正则模提供了引力波领域的代表性实现。

Conclusion: 近简并极点对的局部响应更自然地组织为以共享载波为中心的框架，而非两个独立极点之和。该中心化组织揭示了有限窗口下的双尺度层级结构，且 Kerr 准正则模证实该结构在引力波振铃分析中具有实际意义。

Abstract: Near-degenerate resonance poles arise widely in open-wave systems, including gravitational-wave ringdowns, when two neighboring modes have almost the same complex frequency. On a finite observation window, the physical waveform is then dominated by a common carrier with a slowly varying interference envelope, so that attempting to treat the signal as a sum of two independently resolved damped sinusoids can become unstable in practice. Mathematically, an exact coalescence of poles leads to a double pole and a Jordan-chain (associated-vector) time dependence with a $t\,e^{-iωt}$ factor; here we show that the same carrier-plus-first-jet structure emerges more generally from a near-degenerate neighboring-pole \emph{pair} on a finite window, without requiring a true pole merger. We show that the local response is more naturally organized as a centered two-pole block about the shared carrier and, in the time domain, as a carrier-plus-first-jet waveform. This centered organization leads to a finite-window two-scale hierarchy: $κ$ controls when the leading correction to the carrier must be included, while $η^2$ controls the remaining error once that correction is retained. Toy two-pole numerics verify this scaling, and Kerr quasinormal modes provide a representative gravitational realization of the same finite-window centered organization.

</details>


### [45] [Power-Law Approach of the Stress-Energy Tensor to the Unruh State after Gravitational Collapse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26840)
*Michael Wilson*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文建立了无质量最小耦合标量场在坍缩零壳时空及真空态中重整化应力-能量张量趋近Unruh态值的速率，给出了有限外部半径处的上界 $\sim t_s^{-3}$ 和无穷远未来零无穷处的幂律渐近行为 $\sim u_s^{-3}$，其指数由径向波动方程Wronskian的 $\omega^2\ln\omega$ 支点奇异性决定，并推测引力扰动（$\ell_{\min}=2$）对应 $t_s^{-7}$ 的幂律衰减。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确定无质量最小耦合标量场在坍缩零壳时空及真空态（in-vacuum state）中，其重整化应力-能量张量（renormalized stress–energy tensor）逼近Unruh态（Unruh state）相应值的速率，并验证数值模拟中发现的幂律衰减行为。

Method: 利用Cauchy面分解Hadamard差（Hadamard difference）以及推迟格林函数（retarded Green function）的支切割结构（branch-cut structure）推导有限外部半径处的上界；通过小频率下支切割留数（branch-cut residue）的显式计算和热谱（thermal spectrum）在大频率下的Planck抑制（Planck suppression），得到未来零无穷（future null infinity）处主导系数的非零性与确定符号。

Result: 有限外部半径处给出上界 $|\Delta\langle T_{\mu\nu}\rangle|\leq C(r)t_s^{-3}$；未来零无穷处给出渐近行为 $\Delta\langle T_{uu}\rangle\sim C_{uu}u_s^{-3}$，其中 $C_{uu}\neq0$ 且 $C_{uu}<0$。指数 $3$ 由径向波动方程 $\ell=0$ 模Wronskian的 $\omega^2\ln\omega$ 支点奇异性（branch-point singularity）决定，与Price律（Price's law）源于同一结构。

Conclusion: 确认了数值研究中的猜想——趋于Unruh态的过程为幂律衰减（power law）。推测引力扰动（自旋2，$\ell_{\min}=2$）对应 $t_s^{-7}$ 的幂律衰减，但其推广涉及规范问题（gauge issues），未在本文中处理。

Abstract: We establish the rate at which the renormalized stress--energy tensor of a massless minimally coupled scalar field in the in-vacuum state of a collapsing null-shell spacetime approaches the corresponding Unruh-state value. At finite exterior radius, we establish the upper bound \[ |Δ\langle T_{μν}\rangle|\leq C(r)\,t_s^{-3} \] from the Cauchy-surface decomposition of the Hadamard difference and the branch-cut structure of the retarded Green function. At future null infinity, we show that the leading coefficient in the late-time expansion \[ Δ\langle T_{uu}\rangle\sim C_{uu}\,u_s^{-3} \] is nonzero, by computing the branch-cut residue explicitly at small frequency and using the Planck suppression of the thermal spectrum at large frequency to show that the dominant contribution to $C_{uu}$ has a definite sign. The result gives \[ Δ\langle T_{uu}\rangle\big|_{\Iscr^+}(u_s) \sim C_{uu}\,u_s^{-3}, \qquad u_s\to\infty, \] with $C_{uu}\neq 0$. The exponent is determined by the $ω^2\lnω$ branch-point singularity in the Wronskian of the $\ell=0$ radial wave equation, the same structure responsible for Price's law. The sign $C_{uu}<0$ is supported by a physical argument and by the numerical mode data of Gholizadeh Siahmazgi, Anderson, and Fabbri. The result confirms their conjecture that the approach is a power law. We conjecture that the same mechanism gives an analogous $t_s^{-7}$ bound for gravitational perturbations ($\ell_{\min}=2$), though the extension to the spin-2 case involves gauge issues not addressed here.

</details>


### [46] [Quintessence-dominated cyclic universe with negative cosmological constant](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.13906)
*Nasr Ahmed,Kazuharu Bamba*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过两个简化的非奇异性循环宇宙模型，引入随时间变化的负宇宙学常数（cosmological constant），实现了正能量密度的物理可接受演化，展示了在精质场主导宇宙中压力符号翻转（不违反零能量条件），以及在物质反弹场景中幻象分界线穿越等现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索负宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）在解释晚期宇宙加速膨胀（late-time cosmic acceleration）中的非传统机制，并检验模型在正能量密度约束下的可行性。

Method: 构建两个简化的非奇异性循环宇宙模型（non-singular cyclic models），引入时变负宇宙学常数（time-varying negative cosmological constant），分别分析精质场主导宇宙中的压力符号翻转和物质反弹（matter-bounce）场景中的幻象分界线（phantom divide line）穿越。

Result: 正能量密度演化在负宇宙学常数下可实现，而正或零宇宙学常数导致负能量密度主导。第一个模型中宇宙压力在精质场主导下发生符号翻转，且不违反零能量条件（null energy condition）。第二个模型中反弹附近观测到幻象分界线穿越。两个模型中标量动能项和势能为正，但标量势与量子势之和为负。

Conclusion: 负时变宇宙学常数能够提供物理上可接受的循环宇宙演化路径，并产生与观测相符的加速膨胀特征，但负的总有效势提示可能需要进一步检验模型的稳定性或引入额外修正。

Abstract: We investigate two simplified non-singular cyclic models with a negative time-varying cosmological constant to represent the non-conventional mechanism of negative cosmological constant expected to address the late-time cosmic acceleration. We show that a physically acceptable evolution with positive energy density can be realized, while negative energy density dominates in case of a positive or zero cosmological constant. In the first model, we demonstrate a sign flipping of the cosmic pressure in a quintessence-dominated universe with no violation of the null energy condition. In the second model, we propose a matter-bounce scenario with showing the crossing of the phantom divide line in the vicinity of the bounce. We find that while we get positive kinetic term and scalar potential, the sum of scalar and quantum potentials is negative.

</details>

### [47] [Search for new physics in $B \to K ππγ$ with Belle II data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26315)
*Sahil Saha*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文通过振幅分析（amplitude analysis）区分 $B^0 \to K_S^0 π^+ π^- γ$ 衰变中经由 CP 本征态（CP eigenstate）与非 CP 本征态的卡子共振（kaonic resonance）贡献，从而将时间依赖的 CP 不对称性（time-dependent CP-asymmetry）测量转化为对超出标准模型新物理的约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: $B^0 \to K_S^0 π^+ π^- γ$ 衰变中的时间依赖 CP 不对称性测量对超出标准模型（Standard Model）的新物理贡献敏感。然而，要将该测量转化为对新物理的有效约束，必须区分终态中来自 CP 本征态卡子共振与非 CP 本征态的不同衰变模式。

Method: 对 $B \to K_{res} γ \to K π^+ π^- γ$ 衰变进行振幅分析（amplitude analysis），以识别并区分不同卡子共振（kaonic resonance）成分的 CP 性质，从而分离 CP 本征态与非 CP 本征态的贡献。

Result: 本文讨论了该振幅分析的具体方法，但摘要中未给出明确的数值结果或分析结论。

Conclusion: 通过振幅分析区分 CP 本征态与非 CP 本征态贡献，是连接 $B^0 \to K_S^0 π^+ π^- γ$ 时间依赖 CP 不对称性测量与超出标准模型新物理约束的关键步骤。

Abstract: The measurement of the time-dependent CP-asymmetry of $B^0 \to K_S^0 π^+ π^- γ$ decays is sensitive to contributions from physics beyond the Standard Model. To translate this measurement into a constraint on new physics, it is necessary to distinguish between decay modes that contribute to the final state via a kaonic resonance that is a CP eigenstate, and those that proceed through non-CP eigenstates. This requires an amplitude analysis of the $B \to K_{res} γ\to K π^+ π^- γ$ decay, that is discussed in this article.

</details>

Zhukov,J. Zhuo,D. Zuliani,G. Zunica*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 利用LHCb实验在质心能量为7、8和13 TeV、总积分亮度为9 fb$^{-1}$的质子-质子对撞数据，首次报道了$B^+\to\pi^+ e^+ e^-$衰变过程的证据，观测到显著性为3.2$\sigma$的信号超出，并测得分支比为$(2.4\,{}^{+0.9}_{-0.8} \,{}^{+0.4}_{-0.2}) \times 10^{-8}$，结果与标准模型（Standard Model）预期一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找罕见重味物理（heavy flavor physics）衰变过程$B^+\to\pi^+ e^+ e^-$的直接实验证据，检验标准模型（Standard Model）对该衰变分支比的预测。

Method: 基于LHCb实验收集的质子-质子对撞（proton-proton collision）数据，质心能量（centre-of-mass energy）为7、8和13 TeV，总积分亮度（integrated luminosity）为9 fb$^{-1}$。

Result: 观测到显著性（significance）为3.2$\sigma$的信号超出；测得分支比（branching fraction）为$(2.4\,{}^{+0.9}_{-0.8} \,{}^{+0.4}_{-0.2}) \times 10^{-8}$，其中第一组不确定度为统计不确定度（statistical uncertainty），第二组为系统不确定度（systematic uncertainty）。

Conclusion: 该结果为$B^+\to\pi^+ e^+ e^-$衰变的首个实验证据，测得的分支比与标准模型（Standard Model）预期一致。

Abstract: The first evidence for the decay $B^+\toπ^+ e^+ e^-$ is reported using proton-proton collision data recorded by the LHCb experiment at centre-of-mass energies of 7, 8 and 13 TeV, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 9 fb$^{-1}$. A signal excess with a significance of 3.2$σ$ is observed and the branching fraction is measured to be $\cal{BR}(B^+\toπ^+ e^+ e^-) = (2.4\,{}^{+0.9}_{-0.8} \,{}^{+0.4}_{-0.2}) \times 10^{-8}$, where the first set of uncertainties is statistical and the second is systematic. The result is consistent with the Standard Model expectation.

</details>


### [49] [Flavour changing charged current decays at LHCb](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26879)
*Davide Fazzini*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于LHCb实验，报告了三个与带电电流（charged-current）半轻子衰变相关的新结果：首次测量比值 $\mathcal{R}(D^{**})$、确定 $\Lambda\to p \mu^{-} \bar{\nu}_\mu$ 分支比，以及从 $B^0 \to D^{*-} \mu^{+} \nu_\mu$ 衰变中提取形状因子参数，用以检验标准模型（Standard Model, SM）中的轻子普适性并探索新物理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型（Standard Model, SM）预言轻子与电弱规范玻色子（electroweak gauge bosons）的耦合具有普适性（universality）。半轻子衰变（semileptonic decays）为检验该预言及探索可能的新物理（New Physics）效应提供了有力框架。

Method: 利用LHCb实验数据，针对三个具体衰变过程进行测量：基于 $B^{-} \to D^{**} \tau^{-} \bar{\nu}_\tau$ 衰变首次测量分支比之比 $\mathcal{R}(D^{**})$；确定 $\Lambda \to p \mu^{-} \bar{\nu}_\mu$ 的分支比（branching fraction）；从 $B^0 \to D^{*-} \mu^{+} \nu_\mu$ 衰变中提取形状因子（form-factor）参数。

Result: 获得三个结果：$\mathcal{R}(D^{**})$ 的首次测量值；$\Lambda \to p \mu^{-} \bar{\nu}_\mu$ 分支比的测定值；$B^0 \to D^{*-} \mu^{+} \nu_\mu$ 衰变中形状因子参数的提取值。

Conclusion: 这些结果有助于在带电电流（charged-current）半轻子衰变中检验标准模型的轻子普适性预言，并为新物理搜索提供实验约束。

Abstract: The Standard Model (SM) predicts the universality of lepton couplings with the electroweak gauge bosons. Semileptonic decays of $b$-hadrons provide a powerful framework for testing the SM and probing possible New Physics effects. In particular, the processes mediated by charged-current interactions benefit from a relatively large branching fractions and theoretically well-controlled hadronic matrix elements. This contribution presents three recent results from the LHCb experiment: the first measurement of the ratio of branching fractions $\mathcal{R}(D^{**})$ using $B^{-} \to D^{**0} τ^{-} \barν_τ$ decays, the determination of the branching fraction for $Λ\to p μ^{-} \barν_μ$ and the extraction of form-factor parameters from $B^0 \to D^{*-} μ^{+} ν_μ$ decays.

</details>

### [50] [Diffusion with conserved marginal distributions and information theory in fracton hydrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26093)
*Vaibhav Mohanty,Sunghan Ro*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有子系统对称性（subsystem symmetries）的扩散过程，发现其动力学由非线性流体力学方程（nonlinear hydrodynamic equations）支配，且初始边缘分布（marginal distributions）中的局域化特征在长时间下得以保持；仅在均匀背景的小涨落极限下出现线性行为。论文推导了任意维度下的确定性与随机性流体力学方程，给出了约束边缘分布下的最大熵平衡分布，并揭示了边缘守恒扩散与多极矩部分守恒（partial multipole-moment conservation）之间的流体力学联系，同时提供了信息论解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有实验在强倾斜光晶格（strongly tilted optical lattices）中实现了多极矩守恒扩散，并发现完整多极矩群（complete multipole-moment groups）的守恒会导致亚扩散（subdiffusive dynamics）行为，服从非线性扩散方程。这自然引发了一个问题：当守恒律仅施加于子系统（subsystem）层面时，流体力学方程是否也会呈现非线性。本文正是为回答这一问题而开展研究。

Method: 论文采用理论分析方法，从子系统对称性出发推导了任意维度下流体力学方程的确定性部分和涨落部分（fluctuating parts），并求解了在约束边缘分布下的最大熵平衡分布（maximum-entropy equilibrium distributions）。同时，通过边缘守恒扩散（marginal-conserving diffusion）与部分多极矩守恒之间的对应关系，建立了具体的流体力学实现框架。

Result: 研究发现，子系统对称性一般会导致非线性的流体力学方程，且初始边缘分布中的任何局域化特征都会由边缘守恒律在长时间下保留；线性行为仅作为均匀背景附近小涨落的一个极限情形出现。此外，总关联（total correlation）单调衰减，而成对互信息（pairwise mutual information）不一定单调衰减。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了子系统对称性下扩散过程的非线性流体力学本质，建立了边缘守恒扩散与多极矩部分守恒之间的桥梁，并提供了信息论视角下的理解，为相关实验和理论提供了统一框架。

Abstract: Diffusion with multipole-moment conservation gives rise to transport laws that generalize Fick's law and has attracted growing attention following experimental advances in strongly tilted optical lattices. It was recently shown that conserving complete multipole-moment groups leads to subdiffusive dynamics governed by a nonlinear diffusion equation, raising the question of whether hydrodynamic equations would also be nonlinear when the conservation law is imposed only at the subsystem level. Here we show that subsystem symmetries generically produce nonlinear hydrodynamic equations with shear-only transport, in which any localization present in the initial marginal distributions is preserved at long times by the conservation of those marginals. A linear regime emerges only as a limiting case for small fluctuations around a uniform background. We derive the deterministic and fluctuating parts of the hydrodynamic equations in arbitrary dimensions and obtain the corresponding maximum-entropy equilibrium distributions under constrained marginals. We also show that marginal-conserving diffusion provides a concrete hydrodynamic realization of partial multipole-moment conservation, and we offer an information-theoretic interpretation in which total correlation decays monotonically even when pairwise mutual information does not.

</details>


### [51] [Topological transitions in spin-ice induced by geometrical constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26125)
*R. A. Borzi,E. S. Loscar,S. A. Grigera*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究表明，在沿[111]和[110]方向施加磁场的近邻自旋冰模型中，通过限制样品的横向尺寸，原本在热力学极限下不存在的Kasteleyn相变会被离散的拓扑相变级联所替代，每个相变对应一条自旋弦（string）逐条进入系统，并在磁化、比热和磁化率上产生可观测的特征信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究样品几何形状（geometry）在稳定阻挫磁体（frustrated magnets）中拓扑相变（topological phase transitions）的作用，特别是针对那些在热力学极限下原本不存在Kasteleyn相变的场方向（[111]和[110]）。

Method: 采用蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）研究有限横向尺寸样品中的磁化、比热（specific heat）和磁化率（susceptibility）行为，并结合基于熵-能平衡的解析处理方法推导各拓扑扇区（topological sector）的临界场（critical fields）。

Result: 有限横向尺寸下，无散度约束（divergence-free constraint）量化了可穿越体系的弦激发数量，导致磁化出现离散跃迁级联；每个跃迁对应尖锐的磁化台阶以及比热和磁化率峰值，其振幅随系统长度线性增长；各向异性样品中这些跃迁保持清晰分辨，而各向同性极限下合并为平滑交叉。

Conclusion: 有限几何结构（finite geometry）可以通过约束横向维度稳定原本不存在的拓扑相变，这是一种阻挫磁体中稳定拓扑相变的非常规机制。

Abstract: We study the nearest-neighbor spin-ice model subjected to a magnetic field applied along the global [111] and [110] directions, focusing on the role of sample geometry in stabilizing topological phase transitions. While no Kasteleyn transition is expected for this field orientations in the thermodynamic limit, we show that constraining the transverse dimensions of the system qualitatively changes the behavior. For samples elongated along the field direction with finite transverse area, the divergence-free constraint quantizes the number of string excitations that can span the system. As a result, the magnetization evolves through a cascade of discrete transitions corresponding to the successive entry of individual strings. Using Monte Carlo simulations, we demonstrate that each transition is marked by sharp magnetization steps and peaks in the specific heat and susceptibility, whose amplitudes scale linearly with the system length. We complement the numerical results with an analytical treatment based on the entropy - energy balance on a system with reduced dimensionality, deriving the critical fields associated with each topological sector. In the isotropic limit these transitions merge into a smooth crossover, but for anisotropic samples they remain sharply resolved, illustrating an unconventional mechanism by which finite geometry stabilizes topological phase transitions in frustrated magnets.

</details>


### [52] [Complex first-passage transport in ring networks with long-range jumps and stochastic resetting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26215)
*Oscar Ivan Torres Mena,Francisco J Sevilla*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过解析和数值方法研究了具有确定性捷径的环状网络（ring networks）上的离散时间随机游走（discrete-time random walk）的输运性质，发现捷径长度与系统尺寸之间的公度关系（commensurability relations）导致平均首达时间（MFPT）出现非单调且自相似的分层结构，且随机重置（stochastic resetting）会放大这种振荡行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究通常认为在网络中添加捷径（shortcuts）可以单调地提升输运效率，但这一预期可能过于简化。本文旨在揭示捷径的空间组织方式——特别是捷径长度与系统尺寸之间的定量关系——如何非平庸地影响网络的输运性能。

Method: 研究对象为具有确定性捷径的环形网络：节点在一维周期链上连接至最近邻以及距离为固定值 r 的节点。利用转移矩阵（transition matrix）的谱性质（spectral properties）解析推导占有概率（occupation probabilities）和平均首达时间（MFPT）的显式表达式；同时结合数值模拟分析均方位移（mean squared displacement）和随机重置的影响。

Result: 远距离节点间的平均首达时间随捷径长度呈高度非单调变化，而非简单单调递减。超过某个阈值后，MFPT 景观形成由最大、最小值构成的分层结构，呈自相似模式，该模式与捷径长度和系统大小之间的公度关系相关。极值的标度行为（scaling behavior）显示出输运效率被显著增强或抑制的特定区域。随机重置进一步放大了 MFPT 的振荡结构，并导致高度非均匀的稳态分布。

Conclusion: 长程连接的空间组织方式（而非简单地增加捷径数量）对网络中的输运效率具有决定性影响。公度性效应和随机重置的相互作用为设计具有特定输运特性的网络提供了新的视角。

Abstract: The transport properties of discrete-time random walks on ring networks with deterministic shortcuts are investigated through analytical and numerical methods. The network consists of a periodic chain where each node is connected to its nearest neighbors and to nodes located at a fixed distance $r$. Using the spectral properties of the transition matrix, we derive explicit expressions for the occupation probabilities and mean first-passage times (MFPTs). Contrary to the common expectation that shortcuts monotonically enhance transport, we find that the MFPT between distant nodes develops a highly non-monotonic dependence on the shortcut length. Beyond a threshold value, the MFPT landscape exhibits a hierarchy of maxima and minima organized in a self-similar pattern associated with commensurability relations between the shortcut length and the system size. The scaling behavior of these extrema reveals regimes where transport efficiency is either strongly enhanced or suppressed. We further analyze the mean squared displacement and the influence of stochastic resetting, showing that resetting amplifies the oscillatory MFPT structure and induces strongly nonuniform stationary distributions. These results demonstrate that the spatial organization of long-range connections plays a crucial role in determining transport efficiency in networks.

</details>


### [53] [Largest eigenvalue and top eigenvector statistics of large Euclidean random matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26852)
*Pasquale Casaburi,Pierpaolo Vivo*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文针对二次核（quadratic kernel）的大维欧几里得随机矩阵（Euclidean random matrices），提出了一个基于复制方法（replica-based framework）的统一理论框架，推导出了最大特征值（largest eigenvalue）和顶端特征向量（top eigenvector）的自洽方程与解析表达式，并通过数值模拟验证了理论预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 欧几里得随机矩阵广泛出现于无序介质和原子系综中的合作现象等物理系统，但其矩阵元通过随机点几何结构存在强关联（strongly correlated），导致解析处理非常困难。尽管谱密度等全局谱性质已相对清晰，但极端特征值（extremal eigenvalues）及其对应特征向量由于在应用中的核心地位备受关注，然而目前理解仍然不足。

Method: 对于任意维度 $d \geq 1$ 中由共同分布独立抽取的向量，作者构建了一个统一的复制方法框架（replica-based framework），导出了一组仅涉及少量参数的自洽方程（self-consistent equations）。该框架利用底层分布的低阶矩（low-order moments）给出平均最大特征值的显式表达式，并在大N极限（large-$N$ limit）下解析刻画了顶端特征向量分量的分布。

Result: 研究发现顶端特征向量展现出非平凡的几何结构（non-trivial geometric structure），其分量集中在一个由控制最大特征值的相同参数所决定的超曲面（hypersurface）上。广泛的数值模拟结果证实了上述理论预测。

Conclusion: 该工作为获取欧几里得随机矩阵的极端谱性质（extremal spectral properties）提供了一个通用框架（general framework），有望推广至更广泛的随机矩阵系统。

Abstract: Euclidean random matrices arise in a wide range of physical systems where interactions are determined by spatial configurations, including disordered media and cooperative phenomena in atomic ensembles. Unlike classical random matrix ensembles, their entries are strongly correlated through the geometry of the underlying random points, making their analytical treatment challenging. While global spectral properties such as the spectral density are relatively well understood, much less is known about extremal eigenvalues and the associated eigenvectors, despite their central role in applications. Here we address the problem of characterising the largest eigenvalue and the corresponding top eigenvector of large Euclidean random matrices with a quadratic kernel. For vectors in any dimension $d \geq 1$ drawn independently from a common distribution, we show that both quantities can be computed within a unified replica-based framework, leading to a set of self-consistent equations involving a small number of parameters. This approach yields an explicit expression for the average largest eigenvalue, fully determined by low-order moments of the underlying distribution, and an analytical characterisation of the distribution of top eigenvector's components in the large-$N$ limit. We find that the top eigenvector exhibits a non-trivial geometric structure, with components concentrating on a hypersurface determined by the same parameters controlling the largest eigenvalue. We further perform extensive numerical simulations that confirm these predictions. More broadly, our work provides a general framework to access extremal spectral properties of Euclidean random matrices.

</details>


### [54] [Quo vadis, stochastic thermodynamics?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26601)
*Jan Korbel,Artemy Kolchinsky,Sarah A. M. Loos,Gonzalo Manzano,Rosalba Garcia-Millan,Olga Movilla Miangolarra,Édgar Roldán*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文综述了随机热力学（stochastic thermodynamics）领域的最新进展，重点介绍了该框架如何超越传统的非平衡物理边界，向包含记忆效应、隐藏自由度、相互作用与活性物质、最优输运几何理论等方向扩展，并探讨其在宏观复杂系统以及计算、生物、社会动力学等非物理语境中的挑战与应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机热力学在过去三十年中已建立起一套用于描述非平衡过程（non-equilibrium processes）的成熟框架，产生了涨落定理（fluctuation theorems）和多种普适界（universal bounds）等基础性结果。然而，这些成果主要局限于传统领域，对含有记忆、隐藏自由度、多体相互作用等更复杂的系统仍缺乏系统整合。因此，有必要对该领域的新近扩展进行梳理，并审视其在跨越物理边界后所面临的新挑战。

Method: 本文采用综述（Perspective）的形式，对随机热力学近年来的延伸方向进行系统归纳：涵盖带有记忆和隐藏自由度（hidden degrees of freedom）的系统研究、针对相互作用与活性物质（active matter）的微观方法、基于最优输运（optimal transport）的几何形式化，以及将这些思想应用于宏观与复杂系统时的桥接问题。此外，还回顾了在计算、生物学及社会动力学（social dynamics）等非物理领域的新兴应用。

Result: 综述指出，随机热力学的边界正在显著拓宽：它已能处理超出马尔可夫假设的系统，并借助几何与输运理论提供新的约束形式。同时，在宏观复杂系统中，统计不可逆性（statistical irreversibility）与热力学耗散（thermodynamic dissipation）之间的关联变得更加间接和模糊。在非物理场景中，该框架已被用于理解计算的热力学代价、生物系统的能量-信息关系以及社会系统中的集体动力学。

Conclusion: 随机热力学正在超越其传统的物理边界，催生一种解决复杂系统热力学问题的非正统框架（unorthodox framework）。这些进展不仅拓展了理论工具的适用范围，也为构建跨学科的热力学方法论提供了新的契机。

Abstract: Stochastic thermodynamics is a framework for describing non-equilibrium processes at the level of fluctuating trajectories, where the state of a system evolves as a stochastic time series, allowing thermodynamic quantities such as work, heat, and entropy production to be defined along individual realizations rather than at the ensemble level only. Over the past three decades, the field has yielded fundamental results, including fluctuation theorems and several universal bounds, such as thermodynamic uncertainty relations, speed limit theorems, and many others. Many of them have been tested on a range of experimental platforms. This Perspective reviews recent developments in stochastic thermodynamics that extend its scope beyond its traditional domains, including systems with memory and hidden degrees of freedom, microscopic approaches to interacting and active matter, and geometric formulations based on optimal transport. Next, the Perspective surveys the challenges that arise when applying these ideas to macroscopic and complex systems, where the link between statistical irreversibility and thermodynamic dissipation becomes less direct. Finally, emerging applications in non-physical contexts are highlighted, including computation, biological systems, and social dynamics. Transcending the traditional boundaries of physics, these developments catalyze an unorthodox framework to tackle the thermodynamics of complex systems.

</details>

### [55] [Violation of a Monty-Hall constraint on determinism using a single qutrit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25953)
*Jorge Meza-Domínguez*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 基于三能级系统（qutrit）和 Monty Hall 谜题启发式协议，提出一个简单不等式，用于区分确定性隐变量理论（无论局域与否）与标准量子力学。量子力学对该不等式的违反表明，即使不依赖局域性（locality）假设，决定论（determinism）与量子相干性（quantum coherence）在序列测量（sequential measurements）中也是不相容的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统贝尔不等式（Bell inequality）排除的是局域隐变量理论（local hidden-variable theories），而该工作希望在不引入局域性假设的条件下，仅通过决定论（determinism）这一前提，区分确定性隐变量理论与量子力学。

Method: 基于 Monty Hall 谜题设计一个序列测量协议：先执行一个“判官（descarte）”过程——即一种相干操作（coherent operation），随后进行一次投影测量（projective measurement）。利用三能级系统（qutrit）中的相干叠加态（coherent superposition）制备，对比确定性理论与量子力学对某一特定状态出现概率的预测。

Result: 在满足 Monty Hall 条件（判官过程从不消除真实态）的任意确定性理论中，判官后得到选定态的概率精确为 1/3；而量子力学由于制备了相干叠加态，预测该概率为 1/6。该不等式（1/3 vs. 1/6）被量子力学违反。

Conclusion: 该不等式证明了决定论（即便不涉及局域性假设）与量子相干性在序列测量中本质不相容。实验上可利用光子 qutrit 实现该协议。

Abstract: We present a simple inequality that distinguishes deterministic hidden-variable theories (local or nonlocal) from standard quantum mechanics, using a single three-level system. The protocol is inspired by the Monty Hall puzzle: a coherent "descarte" procedure followed by a projective measurement. In any deterministic theory that respects the Monty Hall condition (the descarte never eliminates the real state), the probability of obtaining a chosen state after the descarte is exactly $1/3$. In contrast, quantum mechanics predicts $1/6$, due to the preparation of coherent superpositions. The inequality is violated by quantum mechanics, demonstrating that determinism (even without locality assumptions) is incompatible with quantum coherence in sequential measurements. An experimental implementation with photonic qutrits is proposed.

</details>


### [56] [Algebraic quantum kinematics and SR-selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26267)
*Leonardo A. Pachon*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文作为六篇系列论文之首，发展了一个将非相对论量子力学与狭义相对论联系起来的算子代数（operator-algebraic）框架。其核心在于：经典傅里叶-麦克斯韦（Fourier-Maxwell）理论无需量子输入即可提供复希尔伯特空间支架，单次正则对易子（canonical commutator）及其标度ħ即可将其提升为单光子QED；常数c与ħ扮演不可互换的角色；将框架提升为Haag-Kastler网（Haag-Kastler net）在伽利略情形下存在结构障碍，此即SR-选择猜想（SR-selection conjecture），并通过三大证据（Hegerfeldt扩散、伽利略多粒子分辨缺失、Reeh-Schlieder失效）加以论证，其中第三条在系列第二篇中被确立为精确的不可能性定理（no-go theorem）。框架的模内容（Tomita-Takesaki、Bisognano-Wichmann、Unruh作为KMS、type-III₁普适性）被汇集为后续文章的代数基底。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 试图在一个统一的算子代数框架内，厘清非相对论量子力学与狭义相对论之间的结构关系，特别关注常数c与ħ在其中扮演的不可互换的角色，并阐明为何伽利略相对论情形下无法构造满足严格微因果性（microcausality）和正能谱（positive-energy spectrum）的Haag-Kastler网。

Method: 以自由QED的光子扇区（photon sector）为透明实现案例，从经典傅里叶-麦克斯韦（Fourier-Maxwell）理论中提取复希尔伯特空间结构（内积、辛形式、薛定谔型模方程、极化C²），再通过引入单个标度为ħ的正则对易子（canonical commutator）将其提升为单光子QED。随后将这一框架推广至Haag-Kastler网，检验其在伽利略情形下的结构可行性。

Result: 发现c与ħ在框架中扮演不可互换的角色：c内禀于每个傅里叶共轭空间（Fourier-conjugate space）内部，而ħ作用于空间之间，将运动相位速率（kinematic phase rates）转化为动力学可观测量（dynamical observables）。在伽利略情形下，将框架提升为符合更严格微因果性和正能谱条件的Haag-Kastler网存在结构性障碍，表现为三大证据：Hegerfeldt扩散、伽利略多粒子分辨缺失、以及Reeh-Schlieder定理在伽利略Haag-Kastler网上的失效。

Conclusion: 该算子代数框架成功从经典理论出发构造了单光子QED，并将光子不可分性、普朗克关系E=ħω和自旋谱±ħ作为定理导出。伽利略情形下构造满足严格条件的Haag-Kastler网被证明是不可能的（该结论在系列第二篇中作为精确的不可能性定理被确立）。该框架的模内容（Tomita-Takesaki、Bisognano-Wichmann、Unruh作为KMS态、type-III₁普适性）为后续关于弯曲背景、动力学度规和叉积扩张的第三至第六篇论文提供了代数基底。

Abstract: We develop, as the first of a six-paper series, an operator-algebraic framework relating non-relativistic quantum mechanics and special relativity. Three structural facts organize the framework. (i)~The photon sector of free QED is a transparent realization: classical Fourier--Maxwell theory supplies a complex Hilbert-space scaffold (inner product, symplectic form, Schrödinger-form mode equation, polarization $\mathbb{C}^2$) with no quantum input, and a single canonical commutator with scale $\hbar$ on the mode amplitudes promotes it to single-photon QED, with photon indivisibility, the Planck relation $E=\hbarω$, and the spin spectrum $\pm\hbar$ as theorems. (ii)~The constants $c$ and $\hbar$ play non-interchangeable roles: $c$ is intrinsic to each Fourier-conjugate space, while $\hbar$ acts \emph{between} them, converting kinematic phase rates into dynamical observables. (iii)~Lifting the framework to a Haag--Kastler net with sharper-than-equal-time microcausality and positive-energy spectrum is structurally obstructed in the Galilean case; we state this as the SR-selection conjecture and identify three strands of evidence (Hegerfeldt spreading; absence of a known Galilean multi-particle resolution; Reeh--Schlieder failure on Galilean Haag--Kastler nets), the third established as a precise no-go theorem in the second paper of the series. The framework's modular content (Tomita--Takesaki, Bisognano--Wichmann, Unruh as KMS, type-$\mathrm{III}_1$ universality) is collected as the algebraic substrate on which the curved-background, dynamical-metric, and crossed-product extensions of the third through sixth papers operate.

</details>


### [57] [Galilean Reeh--Schlieder Obstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26271)
*Leonardo A. Pachon*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，在经典伽利略 Haag–Kastler 公理（augmented by Bargmann mass superselection）框架下，Reeh–Schlieder 性质（Reeh–Schlieder property）不可能成立：不存在一个真空态（vacuum）对所有局域场代数（local field algebra）同时具有循环性（cyclic）和分离性（separating）。这一结果揭示了 Relativistic AQFT 与 Galilean AQFT 之间的结构性区别——前者将 Reeh–Schlieder 作为定理导出，后者则无法拥有该性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究伽利略代数量子场论（Galilean algebraic quantum field theory, Galilean AQFT）与相对论性代数量子场论（relativistic AQFT）之间的结构性差异；具体而言，检验伽利略 Haag–Kastler 公理体系是否能够兼容 Reeh–Schlieder 性质。

Method: 通过结合两个关键因素进行证明：伽利略薛定谔场（Galilean Schrödinger fields）湮灭 Fock 真空（Fock vacuum），以及 Bargmann 质量超选择规则（Bargmann mass superselection）禁止使用 Hermitian 组合规避（Hermitian-combination evasion）——后者正是保持相对论性公理一致性的手段。论证还扩展到 Fock 表示假设之外，借助时间零限制（time-zero restrictions）和场代数稳定公共稠密定义域（field-algebra-stable common dense domain）等条件。

Result: 任何携带确定 Bargmann 质量荷（definite Bargmann mass charges）且允许时间零限制的伽利略 Haag–Kastler 网（Galilean Haag–Kastler net）均与 Reeh–Schlieder 性质不相容。此外，有下界的质量谱（bounded-below mass spectrum）和处于谱最小值的真空（vacuum-at-spectral-minimum）——通常作为独立公理引入——被分别推导为正能量提升正定性（positive-energy boost positivity）和 Bose-CCR 代数下降（Bose-CCR algebraic descent）的结果。因此，Tomita–Takesaki 模流（Tomita–Takesaki modular flow）在伽利略局域场代数上不可用。

Conclusion: Reeh–Schlieder 性质被确认为区分相对论性与伽利略代数量子场论的结构性判据：relativistic AQFT 可以将该性质作为定理导出，而 Galilean AQFT 则无法具备该性质。

Abstract: We prove that the standard Galilean Haag--Kastler axioms, augmented by Bargmann mass superselection, are inconsistent with the Reeh--Schlieder property: no such net admits a vacuum that is cyclic and separating for every local field algebra. Two ingredients combine: Galilean Schrödinger fields annihilate the Fock vacuum, and Bargmann mass superselection forbids the Hermitian-combination evasion that keeps relativistic axioms consistent. The result extends beyond the Fock-representation hypothesis: any Galilean Haag--Kastler net whose canonical fields carry definite Bargmann mass charges and admit time-zero restrictions on a field-algebra-stable common dense domain is incompatible with Reeh--Schlieder. The bounded-below mass spectrum and the vacuum-at-spectral-minimum, usually imposed as separate axioms, are derived consequences -- of positive-energy boost positivity and a Bose-CCR algebraic descent, respectively. The Tomita--Takesaki modular flow is consequently unavailable on Galilean local field algebras. We identify the Reeh--Schlieder property as the precise structural ingredient distinguishing relativistic from Galilean algebraic quantum field theory: relativistic AQFT has it as a theorem, Galilean AQFT cannot.

</details>


### [58] [Newton-Cartan limit of Klein-Gordon AQFT and the collapse of Galilean modular structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26287)
*Leonardo A. Pachon*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文将代数量子场论（algebraic quantum field theory）中伽利略/相对论结构分界线——即满足Bargmann电荷假设的伽利略Haag-Kastler网（Galilean Haag-Kastler net）不存在Reeh-Schlieder性质与Tomita-Takesaki模流（modular flow）——通过牛顿-卡特极限（Newton-Cartan limit, c→∞）推广至弯曲背景。作者以自由Klein-Gordon场为例，证明在Minkowski时空和允许后牛顿展开（Post-Newtonian expansion）的静态全局双曲时空（static globally hyperbolic spacetimes）中，与位置无关的静态能量重标度（rest-energy rescaling）在极限下可产生满足相应平直或弯曲时空公理的伽利略Haag-Kastler网。Bargmann中心荷等于Klein-Gordon质量m；引力势V(x)进入极限薛定谔哈密顿量，但不影响被伽利略Reeh-Schlieder禁戒定理所阻碍的代数结构。该禁戒定理在Fock表示下可推广至弯曲时空修正设定，且极限网在局域代数（local algebras）上不承载模流。以Schwarzschild时空为工作示例：Killing视界收缩为一点，Hartle-Hawking热态不存在c→∞极限，Boulware真空极限为类氢引力基态。Reissner-Nordström度规作为一致性检验，表明后牛顿领头阶未能捕捉背景的电磁内容。牛顿常数G仅在哈密顿量层面进入当前背景度规框架，而动力学度规扩展需G发挥结构性作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将已有平直时空下伽利略与相对论代数量子场论的结构分界——即Galilean Haag-Kastler网因Bargmann超选择规则而缺失Reeh-Schlieder性质与模流——推广至弯曲时空背景，以理解非相对论极限下量子场论代数结构在弯曲时空中的行为。

Method: 采用牛顿-卡特极限（c→∞）将平直时空的伽利略结构分界结果推广至弯曲背景；以自由Klein-Gordon场为具体模型，在Minkowski时空和可进行后牛顿展开的静态全局双曲时空上，通过与位置无关的静态能量重标度构造极限伽利略Haag-Kastler网；以Schwarzschild和Reissner-Nordström度规为工作示例验证理论。

Result: 在弯曲时空的牛顿-卡特极限下，自由Klein-Gordon场产生满足推广公理的Galilean Haag-Kastler网；Bargmann中心荷等于Klein-Gordon质量m；引力势V(x)仅进入极限哈密顿量而不影响被禁戒的代数结构；Reeh-Schlieder禁戒定理与模流缺失在弯曲时空修正设定下依然成立；Schwarzschild时空的Killing视界退化为点，Hartle-Hawking态无极限，Boulware真空极限为类氢引力基态。

Conclusion: 伽利略/相对论代数结构分界线在牛顿-卡特极限下可自洽地推广至弯曲时空；牛顿常数G在当前背景度规框架中仅出现在哈密顿量层面，未来需在动力学度规理论中赋予其结构性作用。

Abstract: We extend the established Galilean/relativistic structural divider in algebraic quantum field theory, namely, the absence of Reeh-Schlieder and of Tomita-Takesaki modular flow on local algebras of any Galilean Haag-Kastler net satisfying a natural axiom set augmented by the Bargmann-charge hypotheses (G7$^*$)(a) and (G7$^*$)(d) to curved backgrounds via the Newton-Cartan ($c\to\infty$) limit. We show, for the free Klein-Gordon field on Minkowski and on static globally hyperbolic spacetimes admitting a Post-Newtonian expansion, that a position-independent rest-energy rescaling produces in the limit a Galilean Haag-Kastler net satisfying the axioms of Ref. [1] in flat-space form (Minkowski) or in a curved-space modification (Killing-flow invariance and uniqueness of the vacuum replacing full translation invariance) appropriate to the static case. The Bargmann central charge equals the Klein--Gordon mass~$m$; the gravitational potential $V(x)$ enters the limiting Schrödinger Hamiltonian but not the algebraic structure obstructed by the Galilean Reeh-Schlieder no-go theorem. The strengthened obstruction theorem of Ref. [1] extends to the modified curved-space setting on Fock representations, and the limiting net carries no modular flow on local algebras. Schwarzschild is treated as a worked example: the Killing horizon shrinks to a point, the Hartle-Hawking thermal state has no $c\to\infty$ limit, and the Boulware vacuum limits to the gravitational hydrogenic ground state. The Reissner-Nordström metric is included as a sanity check confirming that leading Post-Newtonian misses the electromagnetic content of the background. We discuss how Newton's constant~$G$ enters the present (background-metric) framework only at the level of the limiting Hamiltonian, and indicate where dynamical-metric extensions would require $G$ to play a structural role.

</details>


### [59] [Imaginarity-generating power of unitaries: A resource-theoretic approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26392)
*Akhil Kumar Awasthi,Mrinmoy Samanta,Sudipta Mondal,Ayan Patra,Aditi Sen De*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文引入“虚部生成能力（imaginarity-generating power, IGP）”概念，量化酉动力学（unitary dynamics）从实数量子态生成虚数性的能力，并在动力学资源理论框架下推导其精确表达式、平均行为、极值条件及高维典型行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虚数性（imaginarity）作为量子力学复结构衍生的基本资源，其动力学生成机制尚未被充分探索。

Method: 基于希尔伯特-施密特范数（Hilbert–Schmidt norm）定义虚数性度量，并在实幺正操作（real unital operations）下证明其单调性；推导纯度约束下IGP的精确表达式；分析均匀分布和希尔伯特-施密特分布下的平均行为；研究哈尔随机酉矩阵（Haar-random unitaries）下IGP的高维集中性质。

Result: 对于纯实输入态，IGP仅取决于酉变换（unitary）固有的、实验可访问的性质；IGP满足动力学资源理论中有效资源单调量的基本性质；确定了最大化IGP的酉变换及对应上界；高维哈尔随机酉变换的IGP高度集中于最大值附近，波动极小。

Conclusion: 典型高维量子动力学在生成虚数性方面极为高效，IGP为刻画量子动力学中的虚数性资源提供了理论工具。

Abstract: Imaginarity, stemming from the complex structure of quantum mechanics, has recently emerged as a fundamental resource, yet its dynamical generation remains largely unexplored. In this work, we introduce the notion of imaginarity-generating power (IGP) of unitary dynamics, which quantifies the ability of unitary operations to produce imaginarity from initially real quantum states. To quantify imaginarity, we employ a measure based on the Hilbert--Schmidt norm, which we show to be monotone under real unital operations. Within the framework of dynamical resource theories, we derive an exact expression for the purity-constrained IGP in arbitrary dimensions and show that, for pure real input states, it depends solely on intrinsic and experimentally accessible properties of the unitary. We further analyze its average behavior over ensembles of states with varying purity under both uniform and Hilbert--Schmidt distributions. We prove that it satisfies the essential properties of a valid resource monotone within the dynamical resource theory of imaginarity. We also characterize the unitaries that maximize the IGP and determine the corresponding bounds. Moreover, for Haar-random unitaries, we show that the IGP concentrates near its maximal value in high dimensions with small fluctuations, indicating that typical high-dimensional quantum dynamics are highly effective at generating imaginarity.

</details>


### [60] [The Fock-Darwin-Darboux system: eigenstates, information entropies and dispersion-like measures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26466)
*Ignacio Baena-Jimenez,Angel Ballesteros,Ivan Gutierrez-Sagredo*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了Fock-Darwin（FD）量子系统及其在Darboux III曲面上的推广——Fock-Darwin-Darboux（FDD）系统的信息论熵与色散度量，给出了Shannon、Rényi和Tsallis熵等指标的解析表达式或数值分析，并揭示了曲率参数与磁场之间的相互影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子系统中，信息论度量（如熵）能够揭示系统的内在复杂性与量子关联结构。FD系统是描述带电粒子在平面上的运动模型，其推广到负曲率Darboux III空间上的FDD系统则引入了非平凡几何效应。本文旨在系统研究这两类可精确求解的量子系统的信息论熵与色散度量，尤其是分析曲率与磁场对熵行为的共同影响。

Method: 利用FD与FDD系统的精确可解性，推导了Shannon熵、Rényi熵和Tsallis熵等度量在坐标空间与动量空间中的解析表达式。对于FDD系统，由于流形的非线性性质，动量空间波函数无法获取简单闭式，因而采用数值方法进行分析。通过对比不同熵度量的数值行为，考察曲率参数与磁场的协同效应。

Result: 对于FD系统，其信息论度量在形式上与谐振子相同，只需引入一个依赖于磁场的修正有效频率。对于FDD系统，曲率参数与磁场的相互影响显著，且Darboux III空间上的Landau系统不存在无限简并的朗道能级（Landau levels）。

Conclusion: FD系统的信息论熵可通过修改有效频率统一到谐振子框架下；FDD系统中曲率破坏了动量空间波函数的简单闭式结构，并消除了Landau系统的无限简并特性，揭示了非欧几何背景对量子系统信息度量的重要影响。

Abstract: The Fock-Darwin (FD) quantum system describes the motion on the plane of a charged particle under the action of an isotropic oscillator potential together with a perpendicular constant magnetic field. When the isotropic oscillator is suppressed, the FD system leads to the Landau Hamiltonian with infinitely degenerate Landau levels. The Fock-Darwin-Darboux (FDD) system is the generalisation of the FD system to a particle moving on the Darboux III space, which is a conformally flat surface with non-constant negative curvature. We present a systematic study of some information-theoretic entropy and dispersion-like measures for these quantum systems. Since both systems are exactly solvable, analytical expressions for Shannon, Rényi and Tsallis entropies, among others, can be obtained. We show that for the FD system, its information-theoretic measures are formally the same as the ones for the harmonic oscillator, provided a modified effective frequency depending on the magnetic field is introduced. In the FDD case, the nonlinear nature of the underlying manifold precludes the existence of a simple closed form for the wave-function on momentum space, which is numerically analysed. We compare the numerical behaviour of the different entropy measures and we analyse the interplay arising in the FDD system between the curvature parameter and the magnetic field. In particular, it is shown that the Landau system on the Darboux III space has no infinitely degenerate Landau levels.

Abstract: We consider a many-body Hilbert space with a fixed global charge and show that the typical entanglement entropy of a subsystem, at the leading and subleading order in the thermodynamic limit, can be expressed in terms of a single quantity which represents the local thermal entropy at fixed charge density. We find a general formula which applies both to abelian U(1) symmetry and non-abelian SU(2) symmetry, including the case of a local Hilbert space which transforms under a general reducible representation of the symmetry group. We illustrate the general formula with model systems and discuss the relevance of the results as a probe of quantum chaos for physical Hamiltonians.

Method: 利用球谐函数最高权分支（highest-weight branch）的赤道局域化，定义了一个自然几何刚性指标（geometric rigidity index），其精确有限量子数取值表现为Wallis部分乘积（Wallis partial product）。该机制在刚性转子（rigid rotor）和薄球壳表面扇区（surface sector of a thin spherical shell）两个系统中实现，二者通过径向冻结（radial freezing）约化为相同的角问题。

Conclusion: 量子力学中的Wallis型结构可以精确地表现为由简单几何可观测量编码的半经典局域化（semiclassical localization）的签名，从而建立了π的涌现与量子局域化之间的直接几何联系。

Abstract: We present a genuinely non-radial quantum-mechanical route by which $π$ emerges from equatorial localization on the sphere. The mechanism is realized in two settings: the standard rigid rotor and the surface sector of a thin spherical shell, where radial freezing reduces the dynamics to the same angular problem. In the large-quantum-number limit, the probability cloud collapses toward the equator, the rigidity index approaches its classical value, and the Wallis formula is recovered through the correspondence principle. The result shows that Wallis-type structures in quantum mechanics can arise as exact signatures of semiclassical localization encoded by a simple geometric observable.

Method: 采用绝热规范势的弗罗贝尼乌斯范数来捕捉本征谱（eigenspectrum）对无穷小绝热规范变形的敏感性，从而构建相图；通过代价函数最小化技术进行无偏有限尺寸标度分析（unbiased finite-size scaling analysis），检验临界无序强度对系统尺寸的稳定性；利用相邻能隙比和谱形因子确定陶勒斯时间（Thouless time）随无序强度的标度行为。

Conclusion: 该研究为理解准随机系统中遍历-多体局域化转变的普适临界特征提供了新的分析工具和定量结果，有助于深化对无序量子系统中临界转变的认知。

Abstract: Although random matrix theory provides a fundamental framework for characterizing quantum chaos, encompassing both ergodic and localized phases, a comprehensive understanding of the universal features governing the critical transition remains elusive in many disordered and quasi-random systems. In this study, we explore the ergodic-to-many-body localization transition in the generalized Aubry-André model with interacting spinless fermions. Using the concept of Frobenius norm of an adiabatic gauge potential, we construct a phase diagram that captures the sensitivity of the eigenspectrum to infinitesimal adiabatic gauge deformations. To examine the stability of the critical disordered strength with respect to system size, we perform an unbiased finite-size scaling analysis via cost-function minimization techniques.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用无序平均Keldysh作用量（disorder-averaged Keldysh action）的精确二次型结构，推导了Tomonaga-Luttinger液体的框架势闭式解，并以随机场XXZ自旋链作为微观实现进行验证。

Conclusion: 研究结果在整个无能隙相（gapless phase）上均得到验证，对模拟量子模拟平台（analog quantum simulation platforms）中的算法设计具有直接意义。

Abstract: Disordered one-dimensional interacting systems have long been characterized via conventional correlation functions. A complementary quantum-information perspective quantifies the randomness of the unitary ensemble dynamics generated by a quantum system through the frame potential, which serves as a practical diagnostic for quantum algorithmic performance. However, no analytical treatment has yet been achieved for experimentally accessible interacting one-dimensional systems. In this Letter, we derive a closed-form expression for the frame potential of a Tomonaga-Luttinger liquid with quenched Gaussian forward-scattering disorder. Exploiting the exactly quadratic structure of the disorder-averaged Keldysh action, we show that the frame potential decays as a power law at early times and saturates to a late-time plateau controlled by a single coupling parameter. Taking the random field XXZ spin chain as a specific microscopic realization, we show that the strongest randomness is achieved near the Heisenberg ferromagnetic point and can be exponentially enhanced through a multiple-quench protocol. Abstract: One of the main difficulties in preparing many-body ground states is achieving the target state through simple counterdiabatic controls. In this work, we apply the recently introduced minimal action shortcut to adiabaticity (MA-STA) to a Kitaev chain and propose a multi-step strategy to obtain the optimal control protocol to drive the system across its different phases. Our results show that high fidelities can be achieved through the adapted MA-STA at time scales much shorter than those of linear ramp protocols. Abstract: This article presents a brief account of Amir O. Caldeira's contributions to the theory of quantum Brownian motion. ### [68] [Reservoir-mediated spin entanglement in the mean-force Gibbs state](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26562)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解在无直接相互作用时，通过共同玻色子热库强耦合诱导的两量子比特平衡态纠缠行为，并弥补现有平均力吉布斯态理论缺乏解析刻画的问题。

Method: 推导两量子比特平均力吉布斯态的近似解析表达式（approximate analytic expressions），并在热平衡条件下分析由库介导的纠缠特性。

Result: 纠缠在低温下最强；纠缠随系统-库耦合强度（system-reservoir coupling strength）呈非单调（non-monotonic）变化；将库的谱密度从单模展宽至多模（broadening spectral density beyond a single mode）可增强量子比特纠缠。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了对热平衡下库介导两量子比特纠缠的全面理解，为数值方法提供了基准，并展示了强系统-库耦合（strong system-reservoir coupling）作为有用资源的潜力。

Abstract: Two qubits strongly coupled to a common bosonic reservoir can become entangled with each other, despite having no direct interaction. In equilibrium, such coupling-induced coherences can be described by the mean-force Gibbs state. Here we derive approximate, analytic expressions for the two-qubit mean-force Gibbs state, and use these to characterize equilibrium qubit-qubit entanglement mediated by a thermal reservoir. Entanglement, which is highest at lowest temperatures, is a non-monotonic function of the system-reservoir coupling strength. Moreover, we find that broadening the reservoir spectral density beyond a single mode, as is realistic for typical baths, can enhance the qubit entanglement. Our results provide a comprehensive understanding of reservoir-mediated two-qubit entanglement in thermal equilibrium and provide a benchmark to compare with numerical methods, as well as demonstrating the utility of strong system-reservoir coupling as a resource.

</details>


### [69] [A Gaussian asymmetry measure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26878)
*Riccardo Travaglino,Pasquale Calabrese*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对自由费米子系统中标准纠缠不对称性（entanglement asymmetry）测量导致的非高斯特性问题，提出了一种严格限制在高斯流形内的不对称性度量，并证明其可精确计算且能捕捉动力学标志性现象（如Mpemba效应、对称性恢复等）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准纠缠不对称性定义在自由费米子系统中会引入显著的非高斯特征（non-Gaussian features），导致分析受到限制。因此，需要一种能够保留在高斯流形（Gaussian manifold）内的不对称性测量方法，以克服上述分析局限。

Method: 引入一种严格限制在高斯流形内的不对称性度量，通过量化高斯态（Gaussian state）与对称高斯态流形之间的最小距离来定义该度量；利用关联矩阵技术（correlation matrix techniques）进行精确计算，并采用准粒子图像（quasiparticle picture）进行渐近描述。

Result: 该高斯不对称性度量能够捕捉纠缠不对称性的已知动力学特征，包括Mpemba效应、对称性恢复（symmetry restoration）及其缺失情况。该度量可通过关联矩阵技术精确计算，并能在准粒子图像下进行渐近分析。

Conclusion: 高斯结构使得新提出的不对称性度量具有可精确计算的优势，同时保留了标准不对称性的物理内涵；此外，研究还探讨了利用电荷涨落（charge fluctuations）表征高斯态不对称性的可能性。

Abstract: The study of Entanglement Asymmetry has emerged in recent years as a powerful tool to characterise the symmetry properties of quantum states in relation to a given charge operator through the lens of entanglement. While extremely powerful and general, the standard definition of asymmetry introduces significant non-Gaussian features in free-fermionic systems, leading to certain analytical limitations. In this work, we introduce an asymmetry measure that remains strictly within the Gaussian manifold and analyse its properties. In particular, we show that it quantifies the minimal distance between a Gaussian state and the manifold of symmetric Gaussian states. We further demonstrate that this measure captures the established dynamical signatures of entanglement asymmetry, such as the Mpemba effect, symmetry restoration, and the lack thereof. The Gaussian structure allows these novel asymmetry measures to be computed exactly using correlation matrix techniques, and to be described asymptotically through the quasiparticle picture. We also comment on the possibility of using charge fluctuations to characterise the asymmetry of a Gaussian state.

### [70] [Normalizing flows for density estimation in multi-detector gravitational-wave searches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26581)
*Sam Insley,Michael J. Williams,Rahul Dhurkunde,Ian Harry*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出用归一化流（normalizing flows）替代PyCBC引力波搜索管线中基于直方图的密度估计方法，将存储需求降低三个数量级以上，且在保持高灵敏度的同时（模拟信号恢复率下降不到0.05%），对特定探测器组合的信号恢复率提升最高达6.55%，为未来多探测器网络分析提供了可扩展框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PyCBC引力波搜索管线（pipeline）目前依赖基于蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte-Carlo simulation）的预计算分箱直方图来估计候选事件的统计显著性，但随着探测器网络规模扩大（四个及以上探测器），直方图的存储需求呈指数级增长，严重限制了管线的扩展能力。

Method: 采用归一化流（normalizing flows）——一种基于机器学习的密度估计方法，替代PyCBC中传统的分箱直方图密度估计器，用于计算候选事件的排序统计量（ranking statistic）中所包含的信号到达时间差、相位延迟和振幅比率的联合概率分布。

Result: 在Advanced LIGO和Virgo第三次观测运行（third observing run）数据上的实验表明：归一化流将存储需求降低了三个数量级以上；在固定虚警率（false-alarm rate）下，模拟信号的恢复率下降不到0.05%；同时，由于放宽了蒙特卡洛方法所需的若干简化假设，特定探测器组合的信号恢复率提升了最高达6.55%。

Conclusion: 归一化流为PyCBC管线提供了一种可扩展且灵活的概率密度估计框架，使其能够有效支持四个及以上探测器网络的分析，并有望在未来的观测运行中扩展至进动信号（precessing signal）或高阶模信号（higher-mode signal）的搜索。

Abstract: Identifying compact binary coalescences buried within the non-Gaussian and non-stationary data taken by gravitational-wave interferometers requires sophisticated search pipelines, such as the PyCBC analysis. A critical task for these pipelines is determining the statistical significance of candidate events by comparing a "ranking statistic" against a large background set. Currently, PyCBC's ranking statistic incorporates the joint probability of the relative arrival times, phase delays and amplitude ratios of the signals seen in different detectors. These parameters are tightly constrained for physical signals but are more broadly distributed for noise. PyCBC currently relies on precomputed binned histogram-based density estimators using Monte-Carlo simulations to obtain these probabilities. However, the storage requirements for these histograms scale prohibitively with the size of the detector network, preventing PyCBC from effectively analyzing four or more detectors. In this paper, we demonstrate that these histograms can be replaced with normalizing flows, a machine learning approach to density estimation. Applying this method to data from the third observing run of Advanced LIGO and Virgo, we demonstrate that normalizing flows reduce storage requirements by over three orders of magnitude. Furthermore, our approach maintains high sensitivity, with less than a 0.05% drop in the recovery of simulated signals at a fixed false-alarm rate. By relaxing several simplifying assumptions previously required by Monte-Carlo methods, we also achieved up to a 6.55% increase in recovered signals for specific detector combinations. These results suggest that normalizing flows provide a scalable, flexible framework for the PyCBC pipeline as it expands to include four or more detectors, or to extend to searches for precessing or higher-mode signals, in future observing runs.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: KM3NeT由两个探测器组成：ARCA（优化用于TeV-PeV中微子）和ORCA（用于GeV-TeV中微子），两者均对来自核坍缩超新星（core-collapse supernova）的MeV中微子敏感，提供宽视场和近乎连续的工作周期。框架执行低延迟事件重建与分类，跟踪多信使社区的外部警报，监测核坍缩超新星中微子爆发，并自主识别与分发宇宙中微子警报（cosmic neutrino alert）。

Conclusion: KM3NeT实时警报系统代表了向快速、协调的多信使观测迈出的重大一步。

Abstract: Multi-messenger astronomy requires real-time systems capable of rapidly responding to external alerts and sharing significant detections with partner observatories. KM3NeT, a deep-sea Cherenkov neutrino telescope in the Mediterranean Sea, is actively contributing to these efforts through a dedicated real-time analysis framework. It comprises two detectors - ARCA, optimised for TeV-PeV neutrinos, and ORCA, for GeV-TeV neutrinos - both also sensitive to MeV neutrinos from core-collapse supernovae, providing a wide field of view and an almost continuous duty cycle. The framework performs low-latency event reconstruction and classification, follows up external alerts from the multi-messenger community, monitors for core-collapse supernova neutrino bursts, and autonomously identifies and distribute cosmic neutrino alerts. Now in advanced commissioning, the KM3NeT real-time alert system represents a major step toward rapid, coordinated multi-messenger observations.

### [72] [Eccentricity as a signature of hierarchical subsolar-mass mergers in collapsar disks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26912)
*Jiaxi Wu,Elias R. Most,Nils L. Vu,Nils Deppe,Lawrence E. Kidder,Kyle C. Nelli,William Throwe*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文通过数值相对论模拟，研究了塌缩星吸积盘中碎裂产生的亚太阳质量并合事件所激发的引力波特征，并发现该层级并合过程可产生并保留显著轨道偏心率（e≃0.1直至并合），可作为该形成机制的强标志。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期电磁暂变源AT2025ulz被疑为亚阈值引力波事件S250818k的超新星千新星（superkilonova）对应体，激发了人们对塌缩星吸积盘碎裂（fragmentation）引发亚太阳质量并合（subsolar-mass merger）场景的关注。该场景预测了层级并合（hierarchical merger）与轨道偏心率（orbital eccentricity）的产生，但目前缺乏直接的引力波特征验证。

Method: 采用数值相对论模拟（numerical relativity simulations），将层级致密天体并合建模为与吸积盘几何一致的黑色洞（black hole）系统，模拟盘状几何中的多次俘获和并合动力学过程。

Result: 最终并合的初始偏心率可达e≃0.6量级；由于系统寿命短，在一般情况下，大部分偏心率可以保留至并合时刻，残余偏心率可达e≃0.1。

Conclusion: 未来在亚太阳质量引力波候选事件中探测到显著偏心率，将是层级形成机制（hierarchical formation scenario）的有力证据。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate gravitational-wave signatures of a proposed subsolar-mass merger scenario resulting from fragmentation inside a collapsar accretion disk. This scenario has gained recent interest with the electromagnetic transient AT2025ulz, a possible superkilonova counterpart candidate to the sub-threshold gravitational wave event S250818k. One prediction of fragmentation is the formation of multiple smaller neutron-star fragments, some of which might merge hierarchically. Such mergers are expected not only to produce individual electromagnetic counterparts, but also, because of their repeated capture and merger dynamics, to impart kicks to the system and thereby drive orbital eccentricity. By performing numerical relativity simulations of hierarchical compact object mergers modeled as black holes in a disk-like geometry consistent with this scenario, we demonstrate the build-up of potentially large eccentricity for the final merger, of order $e \simeq 0.6$ initially, and show that, because of the short lifetime of the system, a substantial part of this eccentricity , up to $e\simeq 0.1$, can survive until merger in the general case. As a result, future detections of eccentricities in potential subsolar-mass gravitational-wave candidate events would be a strong indicator for a hierarchical formation scenario.

### [73] [Geometric Constraints on the Pre-Recombination Expansion History from the Hubble Tension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25813)
*Davide Pedrotti*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文对宇宙复合前（pre-recombination）的背景膨胀历史进行了与模型无关的重构（model-independent reconstruction），发现仅通过早期宇宙的修正（purely early-time resolutions）即可在背景层面上缓解哈勃张力（Hubble tension），同时满足几何宇宙微波背景（CMB）约束。这类解决方案要求在物质-辐射等值期（matter-radiation equality）附近出现平滑过渡，表现为复合前膨胀率增强约15%。该结果为未来模型构建提供了蓝图和背景层面的检验基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 哈勃张力（Hubble tension）是当前宇宙学中本地测量与CMB推定的哈勃常数（$H_0$）之间的显著分歧。寻找不改变后期宇宙演化的纯早期解决方案对理解新物理至关重要。

Method: 采用与模型无关的重建方法（model-independent reconstruction），直接对复合前的背景膨胀历史进行反演，避免对具体早期新物理模型的先验假设。

Result: 存在一类纯早期解决方案，能够在背景层面满足CMB几何约束并缓解哈勃张力。这类解的特征是在物质-辐射等值期附近出现平滑过渡，复合前膨胀率相比标准宇宙学模型增强约15%。

Conclusion: 该结果为未来的哈勃张力模型构建提供了蓝图（blueprint）和背景层面的压力测试（stress-test）基准，指导模型必须实现复合前约15%的膨胀率增强这一特征。

Abstract: I perform a model-independent reconstruction of the background pre-recombination expansion history of the Universe. I find that purely early-time resolutions to the Hubble tension, satisfying the geometric CMB constraints, exist at the background level. This class of solutions requires a smooth transition around matter-radiation equality, characterized by a $\simeq 15\%$ expansion rate enhancement prior to recombination. This result serves as a blueprint for future model-building approaches, providing a background stress-test for Hubble tension proposals.

</details>


### [74] [Sensitivity of binary pulsar timing to spin-0 and spin-1 ultralight dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26092)
*Federico Huxhagen,Diana López Nacir*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文扩展了一种两步贝叶斯推断框架，用于探测二次标量耦合和自旋-1矢量超轻暗物质（ultralight dark matter, ULDM），并通过脉冲星计时分析获得了新的耦合参数约束，填补了其他实验无法触及的质量区间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超轻玻色子暗物质在星系尺度上可近似为相干经典振荡场，可能通过直接耦合扰动天体运动，从而在脉冲星计时信号中留下可探测的特征。现有方法在参数推断中存在人工高估灵敏度的问题，且对二次标量耦合和矢量暗物质的探测尚不充分。

Method: 基于两步贝叶斯推断框架，将轨道扰动参数作为 nuisance 参数显式边缘化，以避免直接拟合方法导致的灵敏度过估；该方法最初针对线性耦合标量 ULDM 设计，本文将其扩展至二次标量耦合和自旋-1 矢量 ULDM 的情形。

Result: 对于二次标量 ULDM，在 $2 \times 10^{-22}$ eV 至 $2 \times 10^{-21}$ eV 的质量区间内建立了新的耦合参数 $β$ 约束，并指出不同质量范围下灵敏度主要由轨道相位 $Ψ'$ 或投影半长轴 $x$ 主导。对于矢量 ULDM，即使在圆轨道中也存在共振特征，在 $10^{-23}$ eV 至 $10^{-18}$ eV 区间内获得了耦合参数 $g$ 的边界，结果与当前实验室及空间实验量级一致。

Conclusion: 本文所扩展的贝叶斯推断方法能够有效抑制参数退化带来的灵敏度虚高问题，为利用脉冲星计时探测标量和矢量超轻暗物质提供了稳健的约束手段，并填补了特定质量区间的探测空白。

Abstract: If dark matter consists of ultralight bosons, on galactic scales it can be effectively described as a coherent classical field experiencing oscillations. Such a field could perturb the dynamics of celestial bodies via a direct coupling to ordinary matter, introducing signatures detectable through high-precision pulsar timing analysis. In this work, we extend a two-step Bayesian inference framework, originally developed for linearly coupled scalar ultralight dark matter (ULDM), to probe a quadratic scalar coupling and spin-1 vector dark matter. By explicitly marginalising over nuisance orbital parameters, our approach provides robust sensitivity limits that avoid the artificial overestimation often associated with direct fitting techniques. For quadratic scalar ULDM, we establish new constraints on the coupling $β$ in the range between $2 \times 10^{-22}$ eV and $2 \times 10^{-21}$ eV inaccessible to other experiments, while identifying mass regimes where the sensitivity is dominated by the orbital phase $Ψ'$ or the projected semi-major axis $x$. For vector ULDM, we characterize resonant signatures present even in circular orbits and obtain bounds on the coupling $g$ within the $10^{-23}$ eV to $10^{-18}$ eV range, yielding results within the same orders of magnitude as current laboratory and space-based experiments.

</details>


### [75] [Blinded Mock Data Challenge: Is the Spectral Siren Technique Robust for Measuring the Hubble Constant?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26273)
*Christos Karathanasis,Suvodip Mukherjee,Lalit Pathak,Sergio Vallejo-Peña,Mohit Raj Sah,Benoît Revenu,Antonio Enea Romano,Juan Garcia-Bellido*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文通过盲测模拟数据挑战，系统展示了光谱汽笛（spectral siren）技术在利用双黑洞（BBH）引力波事件测量哈勃常数时，必须准确掌握BBH质量分布随宇宙红移的演化，尤其是金属丰度依赖性和时间延迟分布的影响，否则模型误配会导致哈勃常数和BBH种群参数的系统性偏差，无法解决哈勃张力（Hubble tension）问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波源提供了一种不依赖距离校准（luminosity distance calibration）的直接测量哈勃常数的独立途径，有望揭示源于低红移与高红移宇宙学探针之间约8%不一致的哈勃张力问题。然而该方法高度依赖于引力波源红移的独立推断可靠性，因此亟需评估相关技术在红移推断中的精度和准确性。

Method: 采用盲测模拟数据挑战（blinded mock data challenge）方法，系统检验了光谱汽笛技术在推断哈勃常数时对BBH质量分布宇宙学演化的依赖。重点分析了BBH质量分布中的金属丰度依赖性（metallicity dependence）及其与时间延迟分布（time-delay distribution）之间的相互作用对哈勃常数推断的影响。

Result: 要解决哈勃张力所需精度水平下可靠测量哈勃常数，必须在所有相关红移处独立推断BBH质量分布，且精度需低于统计不确定性。若真实模型与分析中采用的假设不匹配，将导致BBH总体参数和哈勃常数的最佳拟合值均出现系统性偏差。

Conclusion: 光谱汽笛技术对哈勃常数的鲁棒推断依赖于对BBH质量分布宇宙学红移演化的准确理解，尤其是金属丰度依赖性和时间延迟分布的关键作用。未来若要可靠解决哈勃张力问题，必须确保BBH质量分布模型在所有相关红移处的准确性与统计精度相匹配。

Abstract: The measurement of the Hubble constant from gravitational wave (GW) sources is one of the independent avenues to shed light on the Hubble tension, which is associated with about an $8\%$ mismatch in the value of the Hubble constant inferred from low-redshift and high-redshift cosmological probes. Such a key measurement is expected from GW sources as it is a direct measurement of the Hubble constant using the luminosity distance without the need for any luminosity distance calibration. However, such a measurement relies strongly on the reliability of the independent inference of the source redshift of the GW source. As a result, it becomes pertinent to gauge the accuracy and precision of techniques in understanding their reliability in inferring redshifts of GW sources. In this work, we show the requirement of the spectral siren technique in knowing the mass distribution of BBHs across cosmic redshifts in order to make a reliable inference of the Hubble constant. We show by a blinded mock data challenge analysis the criticality in capturing the underlying metallicity dependence of the BBH mass distribution and its interplay with time-delay distribution for a robust inference of the Hubble constant using the spectral siren technique. In order to have a reliable measurement of the Hubble constant at the level required to resolve the Hubble tension in the future, the mass distribution of the BBHs needs to be independently inferred at all relevant redshifts with an accuracy less than the statistical uncertainty. Otherwise, a mismatch of the true model and the underlying assumption made in the analysis can lead to a best-fit model for the wrong value of both BBH population parameters as well as the Hubble constant.

</details>


### [76] [Tidal Heating of Stellar Clusters in Fuzzy Dark Matter Halos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26393)
*Yiheng Liu,Xinyu Li*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文通过模拟恒星团在模糊暗物质（fuzzy dark matter, FDM）晕中的动力学演化，发现当德布罗意波长（de Broglie wavelength）远大于星团尺度时，潮汐加热（tidal heating）是主要机制，且孤子质量减小和潮汐剥离晕会抑制加热，从而指出利用星团加热约束FDM质量时必须仔细考虑FDM晕的结构和环境。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超微矮星系（ultra-faint dwarf galaxies）为波动暗物质（wave dark matter）模型提供了重要的检验平台。此前基于模拟的研究利用扩散近似推导出了模糊暗物质（fuzzy dark matter, FDM）粒子质量的下限，但该近似仅在德布罗意波长远小于星系半光半径时有效，需要探索更广泛的参数空间。

Method: 研究团队模拟了恒星团在FDM晕中的动力学演化过程，覆盖了广泛的FDM质量范围，重点分析了不同质量下的加热机制，并考察了孤子质量减小和潮汐剥离晕对加热过程的抑制作用。

Result: 当FDM质量足够低、德布罗意波长远大于星团尺度时，潮汐加热（tidal heating）成为主要加热机制；孤子质量减小和潮汐剥离晕可以抑制加热效应。

Conclusion: 利用星团加热来约束FDM质量时，必须仔细考虑FDM晕的内部结构及其所处的环境，否则可能得出不准确的约束条件。

Abstract: Ultra-faint dwarf galaxies serve as powerful testing grounds for wave dark matter models through dynamical stellar heating. Previous simulation-based work derived a lower bound on the fuzzy dark matter particle mass using a diffusion approximation valid only when the de Broglie wavelength is much smaller than the galaxy's half-light radius. We simulate the dynamical evolution of stellar clusters in FDM halos across a wide mass range and find that for sufficiently low masses, where the de Broglie wavelength is much larger than the cluster size, tidal heating is the main mechanism. We also find that a reduced soliton mass and tidally stripped halo can suppress the heating. We demonstrate that in order to constrain FDM mass from cluster heating, the structure and environment of the FDM halo must be carefully considered.

</details>


### [77] [Studying spherical collapse and its implications in the Eddington-inspired Born-Infeld gravity theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26433)
*A. M Velásquez-Toribio*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文在亚视界、无压、准静态条件下研究爱丁顿启发式玻恩-因费尔德（Eddington-inspired Born–Infeld, EiBI）引力中的球状塌缩，指出该理论中物质梯度修正项使理想的不连续顶帽（top-hat）构造失效，因此引入正则化轮廓与粗粒化方案，并通过对比两种匹配初始构型计算了线性塌缩阈值、反转过密度、反转半径和维里过密度等关键量，发现EiBI效应显著影响非线性过密度观测量，对塌缩阈值和维里过密度产生与耦合常数相关的系统性偏移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有EiBI引力的弱场极限在物质梯度修正下与标准顶帽球状塌缩模型不相容，导致后者在边界处出现奇异性，因此需要发展一种适用于EiBI引力框架的正则化球状塌缩分析方法，以准确评估该理论对结构形成的影响。

Method: 从非线性的连续性方程和欧拉方程出发，推导密度对比的演化方程；采用有效物理梯度闭合（effective physical-gradient closure）处理EiBI源项，并构建两种匹配初始构型——正则化的Tanh轮廓和基于峰值的轮廓（peak-based profile），二者共享相同的特征半径和累积质量代理。

Result: 与ΛCDM参考情形相比，EiBI修正降低了线性塌缩阈值δ_c，提高了反转过密度δ_t和维里过密度Δ_vir，并使反转半径R_t略有减小；这些偏差随无量纲耦合参数κ̂_BI增大而增强。非线性过密度观测量对EiBI修正响应最强烈，且对内部分布形状存在残余依赖性，而反转半径则相对不敏感。

Conclusion: 球状塌缩是探测EiBI引力物质梯度耦合的灵敏探针，该结果可推广应用于晕统计和非线性结构形成研究。

Abstract: We investigate spherical collapse in Eddington-inspired Born--Infeld (EiBI) gravity in the subhorizon, pressureless, and quasi-static regime, emphasizing the matter-gradient correction that appears in the weak-field limit of the theory. Starting from the nonlinear continuity and Euler equations, we derive the evolution equation for the density contrast and show that the EiBI contribution depends explicitly on spatial derivatives of the matter density. This feature makes the ideal discontinuous top-hat construction ill-defined, since gradient terms become singular at the boundary, and requires a regularized overdensity profile together with a coarse-graining prescription. We adopt an effective physical-gradient closure for the EiBI source term and compare two matched initial configurations: a regularized Tanh profile and a peak-based profile, calibrated to share the same characteristic radius and cumulative mass proxy. Within this framework, we compute the linear collapse threshold $δ_c(z_{\rm coll})$, the turnaround overdensity $δ_t(z_{\rm coll})$, the turnaround radius $R_t(z_{\rm coll})$, and the virial overdensity $Δ_{\rm vir}(z_{\rm coll})$. Relative to the $Λ$CDM reference case, the EiBI correction lowers $δ_c$, enhances both $δ_t$ and $Δ_{\rm vir}$, and produces a more modest reduction of $R_t$, with deviations increasing with the dimensionless coupling $\hatκ_{\rm BI}$ over the range considered. The nonlinear overdensity observables show the strongest response to the EiBI correction and retain a residual dependence on the internal shape of the matched profile, whereas the turnaround radius is comparatively less affected. These results identify spherical collapse as a sensitive probe of EiBI matter-gradient couplings and motivate applications to halo statistics and nonlinear structure formation.

</details>


### [78] [Transient Parity Violation during Inflation: Implications for PTA Gravitational Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26513)
*Gianmassimo Tasinato*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究暴胀期间瞬态宇称破缺（parity violation）相位的后果，通过时间局域的Chern-Simons耦合建模，放大原初引力波（primordial gravitational waves）在小尺度上的信号，产生鲁棒的谱形（有效斜率n_T ≃ 2）。该信号位于脉冲星计时阵列（pulsar timing array, PTA）的宇宙学幂律解释范围内，与超大质量黑洞双星预期不同，为区分天体物理与原初引力波背景（gravitational-wave background）提供了可预测的宇宙学模板，并与宇宙微波背景（cosmic microwave background, CMB）约束一致。信号还表现出大线性偏振和非平凡斯托克斯关联，对应接近最大相位相干的手征态（helicity state），其探测将为引力波背景的原初相干起源提供间接证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）探测到的引力波背景信号可能存在天体物理（如超大质量黑洞并合）与原初宇宙学两种起源，需建立可区分的理论模板。暴胀期间的瞬态宇称破缺（parity violation）机制可产生具有独特谱形和偏振特征的引力波信号，为区分这两种起源提供预测性框架。

Method: 采用一个时间局域的Chern-Simons型耦合（time-localized Chern-Simons-like coupling）来建模暴胀期间的瞬态宇称破缺（parity violation）相位，分析该耦合对原初引力波（primordial gravitational waves）在小尺度上的放大效应。

Result: 该机制产生具有鲁棒谱形的引力波信号，有效斜率n_T ≃ 2，且对微观细节不敏感。该信号位于PTA（pulsar timing array）宇宙学幂律解释范围内，与超大质量黑洞双星预期不同，并与CMB（cosmic microwave background）约束一致。信号还具有大线性偏振和非平凡斯托克斯关联，对应接近最大相位相干的手征态（helicity state）。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一个可预测的宇宙学模板，用于区分引力波背景的天体物理（astrophysical）与原初（primordial）起源。若探测到上述独特的偏振和相干特征，将为引力波背景的原初相干起源提供间接证据（circumstantial evidence）。

Abstract: We investigate the consequences of a transient phase of enhanced parity violation during inflation. Modeling this phase through a time-localized Chern--Simons-like coupling, we show that it amplifies primordial gravitational waves at small scales, producing a robust spectral shape with a blue growth of effective slope $n_T \simeq 2$, largely insensitive to microscopic details. This prediction lies in the range explored by recent pulsar timing array (PTA) analyses under cosmological power-law interpretations, while differing from the canonical supermassive black hole binary expectation. Our framework thus provides a predictive cosmological template to benchmark astrophysical versus primordial origins of the signal, consistent with cosmic microwave background bounds. The signal also exhibits large linear polarization and non-trivial Stokes correlations, corresponding to an almost maximally phase-coherent helicity state. Such features are difficult to realize in classical stochastic backgrounds, and their detection would provide circumstantial evidence for a primordial, coherently generated origin of the gravitational-wave background.

</details>


### [79] [The End of the First Act: Spectral Running, Interacting Dark Radiation, and the Hubble Tension in Light of ACT DR6 Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26541)
*Mathias Garny,Florian Niedermann,Martin S. Sloth*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究指出，ACT合作组织DR6数据发布的ΔNeff约束对暴胀功率谱假设高度敏感。通过引入自相互作用暗辐射和谱指数跑动参数（α_s, β_s），并结合多项宇宙学数据，得到了显著松弛的ΔNeff上限（<0.58/0.68），减弱了 Hubble 张力的显著性（降至2.2σ/低于2σ），并讨论了跑动参数在暴胀场景中的可能起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ACT合作组织在DR6数据中报告了ΔNeff的低约束值，并宣称确认了Hubble张力的存在；但该约束对暴胀初始功率谱的假设高度敏感，需要检验引入更复杂的暴胀参数（谱指数跑动）和暗辐射模型后的结果是否依然成立。

Method: 将标准ΛCDM模型扩展为包含自相互作用暗辐射（self-interacting dark radiation）以及谱指数n_s的跑动α_s和跑动的跑动β_s的模型；同时考虑暗辐射与暗物质初始耦合、在物质-辐射等值期附近发生暗辐射-物质退耦（DRMD）的变体。采用Planck、ACT DR6、DESI DR2及未标定的Pantheon+数据进行联合统计分析。

Result: 在包含α_s和β_s的扩展模型中，得到ΔNeff < 0.58（95%置信度），α_s>0和β_s>0分别有2.9σ和2.6σ的偏好，Hubble张力降至2.2σ。在DRMD情景下，ΔNeff进一步松弛至< 0.68（95%置信度），Hubble张力降至2σ以下。暗辐射主要受Planck和DESI所覆盖的尺度约束，更小尺度则携带暴胀动力学信息。

Conclusion: ACT合作对ΔNeff的严格约束依赖于对暴胀初始功率谱的简单假设；一旦考虑谱指数跑动和自相互作用暗辐射，约束显著松弛，Hubble张力的统计学显著性也大幅减弱。α_s和β_s可自然地出现在暴胀场景中，可能与第一幕暴胀（first act of inflation）的结束相关。

Abstract: We point out that constraints on $ΔN_\mathrm{eff}$ reported by the ACT collaboration in their DR6 data release are surprisingly sensitive to the assumptions made about the initial power spectrum from inflation. The ACT collaboration reports no evidence of new light degrees of freedom alongside a low value of the expansion rate, thus confirming the Hubble tension. However, as we show here, when considering self-interacting dark radiation and including running, $α_s$, and running of the running, $β_s$, of the spectral index $n_s$, the picture changes significantly. Confronting this extended model with Planck, ACT DR6, DESI DR2, and uncalibrated Pantheon+ data, we find the significantly relaxed bound $ΔN_\text{eff}< 0.58$ at 95$\%$ CL, together with a $2.9 σ$ ($2.6 σ$) preference for $α_s>0$ ($β_s>0$), while the Hubble tension is reduced to $2.2 σ$ with only three more parameters compared to $Λ$CDM. If the dark radiation fluid is initially coupled to dark matter, and undergoes dark radiation-matter decoupling (DRMD) around matter-radiation equality, predicting dark acoustic oscillations with drag horizon $r_{d,\mathrm{DAO}} \approx 60 \,\mathrm{Mpc}/h$, the bound is further relaxed to $ΔN_\text{eff}< 0.68$ at 95$\%$ CL, reducing the Hubble tension below $2σ$. We also discuss how $α_s$ and $β_s$ could naturally appear in inflationary scenarios, possibly connected to the end of a first act of inflation. In this case dark radiation is mostly probed by scales covered by Planck and DESI, while smaller scales carry information on inflationary dynamics.

</details>


### [80] [Nonlinear Relativistic Effects on Cosmological Redshift Drift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26690)
*Pierre Béchaz,Giuseppe Fanizza,Giovanni Marozzi,Matheus R. Medeiros Silva*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文首次在文献中利用完全规范不变（gauge-invariant）的方法，计算了宇宙学扰动理论（cosmological perturbation theory）中红移漂移（redshift drift）至二阶的相对论效应。研究发现红移空间畸变（redshift-space distortion）仅作为二阶效应出现，而不存在于线性扰动中；并进一步推导了亚哈勃尺度（sub-Hubble scales）上领头阶扰动贡献的双谱（bispectrum）解析表达式。数值结果表明，在低红移和大动量条件下，双谱中的非线性增强超过了平方功率谱（squared power spectrum）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 红移漂移是直接探测宇宙膨胀动力学的关键可观测量，但以往研究大多局限于线性扰动层面。本文旨在弥补这一空白，通过规范不变方法系统计算二阶相对论效应对红移漂移的贡献，并定量评估其对双谱的影响。

Method: 采用完全规范不变的形式体系，并引入一组光锥坐标（light-cone coordinates）来简化在非均匀且各向异性宇宙中光传播的描述。基于此，在宇宙学扰动理论框架下进行二阶展开，推导了双谱的解析表达式并给出数值评估。

Result: 红移空间畸变在线性扰动中不出现，仅在二阶效应中显现。在低红移和大动量区域，双谱中的非线性增强显著大于平方功率谱的非线性贡献。

Conclusion: 高阶相对论效应对红移漂移和双谱具有不可忽略的影响，尤其是在低红移和大尺度结构探测中必须加以考虑。这为未来精确宇宙学观测（如对暗能量和引力理论的检验）提供了重要的理论修正依据。

Abstract: Using a fully gauge-invariant approach, we compute for the first time in the literature relativistic effects on the redshift drift up to second order in cosmological perturbation theory. This is achieved by employing a set of light-cone coordinates that simplify the description of light propagation in an inhomogeneous and anisotropic universe. We show that redshift-space distortion occurs only as a second-order effect whereas, as known, it is not present among the linear perturbations. We then derive analytical expressions of the bispectrum for the leading-order perturbative contributions on sub-Hubble scales, providing some numerical evaluations. Our finding is that, at low redshift and for large momenta, the non-linearities in the bispectrum are enhanced more than the squared power spectrum.

</details>
