### [81] [Comparison of Silvaco and Synopsys TCAD Predictions Including the Perugia Radiation Damage Model in Silicon Pixel Detectors for the HL-LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26386)
*M. Bomben,T. Croci,K. Aouadj,A. Fondacci,F. Moscatelli,A. Morozzi,D. Passeri*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文比较了Silvaco与Synopsys TCAD两种器件模拟工具在HL-LHC高辐射环境下对硅像素探测器性能的预测，基于“佩鲁贾辐射损伤模型”（Perugia radiation damage model）的表面和体缺陷及陷阱设置，在两种温度和通量下对漏电流、耗尽电压、电场及陷阱统计的预测结果较为一致且令人满意。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: HL-LHC中硅像素探测器将承受比当前内层像素层高5–10倍的辐射注量（fluence），信号损失因辐射损伤成为追踪（tracking）和顶点重建（vertexing）性能的主要限制，漏电流（leakage current）和耗尽电压（depletion voltage）的升高严重制约运行条件，因此需要可靠的辐照后预测以估计运行电压值并检验追踪算法的鲁棒性（robustness）。

Method: 将“佩鲁贾辐射损伤模型”（Perugia radiation damage model）的表面和体缺陷及陷阱纳入后，分别使用Silvaco和Synopsys TCAD两种器件模拟（device simulation）工具进行预测，并在两个不同的参考温度（reference temperatures）和通量（fluences）条件下进行对比。

Result: 在漏电流、耗尽电压、电场（electric field）和陷阱统计（trap statistics）方面，两种TCAD工具在两个参考温度与通量条件下的预测结果均表现出良好的一致性，结果令人满意。

Conclusion: Silvaco与Synopsys TCAD结合佩鲁贾辐射损伤模型能够可靠地预测高辐射环境下硅像素探测器的关键电学性能，有助于为HL-LHC的探测器运行提供参数估计与算法验证基础。

Abstract: At the High Luminosity Large Hadron Collider (HL-LHC), silicon pixel detectors will be exposed to radiation fluences about 5 to 10 times larger than those experienced by the current innermost pixel layers up to today. Signal loss will be the main limitation to tracking and vertexing performance due to radiation damage in hybrid pixel detectors, with the increase in leakage current and depletion voltage posing severe constraints on operating conditions. It is important to have reliable predictions for all observables - such as charge collection performance, leakage current level and breakdown voltage - after irradiation, in order to estimate operational voltage values and to test the robustness of tracking algorithms. In this paper, the predictions of Silvaco and Synopsys TCAD device simulations are compared when the surface and bulk defects and traps of the ``Perugia radiation damage model'' are included. The results are quite promising regarding leakage current, depletion voltage, electric field and trap statistics, at two distinct reference temperatures and fluences.

### [82] [Towards a microscopic model for an electronic quantum charge liquid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25992)
*Jacob R. Taylor,Sankar Das Sarma,Seth Musser*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一条构建电子量子电荷液体（quantum charge liquid, QCL）的路径，从自旋less费米子于填充数ν=3/2出发，配对得到填充数ν=3/4的玻色子，进而研究正方晶格上的四聚体模型（tetramer model）作为玻色子QCL候选，发现其中一个态具有ℤ₄拓扑序（topological order）且为有能隙（gapped）的玻色子QCL。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子电荷液体（QCL）是一种在不破坏平移对称性的情况下由费米子组成的量子态，尤其是玻色子QCL的存在性尚不明确，本文旨在为构建这类态提供一条具体路径，并寻找其最小拓扑序的实现。

Method: 从自旋less费米子（spinless fermions）在填充数ν=3/2出发，通过配对得到玻色子（bosons）于填充数ν=3/4；将正方晶格上的四聚体模型（tetramer model）作为玻色子QCL的候选模型，并研究了四聚体波函数族（tetramer wavefunctions）的数值性质。

Result: 四聚体模型展现出局域ℤ₄对称性（local ℤ₄ symmetry）；数值研究显示，部分波函数因U(1)³对称性为无能隙（gapless），而至少另一个波函数可被明确证明为有能隙（gapped）。

Conclusion: 该有能隙态连同其ℤ₄对称性，表明它是具有最小ℤ₄拓扑序（minimal ℤ₄ topological order）的玻色子QCL；文章最后讨论了向其他晶格几何、电子QCL以及里德伯原子（Rydberg atoms）推广的可能性。

Abstract: We provide a route to constructing an electronic quantum charge liquid (QCL), a state made up of fermions at fractional filling of a lattice that does not break translation. Starting with spinless fermions at filling $ν=3/2$ we pair them to get bosons at filling $ν=3/4$ per unit cell. The tetramer model, a generalization of the dimer model, on the square lattice is evaluated as a candidate bosonic QCL at filling $ν= 3/4$. It is shown that these models exhibit a local $\mathbb{Z}_4$ symmetry. Upon numerical study of a family of tetramer wavefunctions it is found that while one is gapless due to $\mathrm{U}(1)^3$ symmetry at least one other can be definitively shown to be gapped. The gapped nature of this state, along with its $\mathbb{Z}_4$ symmetry, leads us to propose that it is an example of the elusive bosonic QCL displaying the minimal $\mathbb{Z}_4$ topological order. We conclude by discussing possible extensions to other lattice geometries, electronic QCLs, and to Rydberg atoms.

</details>


### [83] [QERNEL: a Scalable Large Electron Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26018)
*Khachatur Nazaryan,Liang Fu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出 QERNEL，一种基础的神经波函数（neural wavefunction），通过变分法求解参数化多电子哈密顿量族，在单一模型中捕获整个参数空间内的基态。该方法结合了 FiLM 条件化、专家混合（mixture of experts）与分组查询注意力（grouped-query attention），在低计算成本下显著提升表达能力。应用于半导体莫尔异质双层中多达150个电子的相互作用系统，QERNEL 成功捕获了量子液体与量子晶体状态，并发现了两者之间的尖锐相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法通常为每个哈密顿量参数单独求解基态，缺乏能在整个参数空间内高效泛化的统一模型。作者希望构建一个可统一解决参数化家族多电子哈密顿量基态问题的神经波函数，并为莫尔量子材料（moiré quantum materials）提供基础模型。

Method: QERNEL 采用基于 FiLM（Feature-wise Linear Modulation）的参数条件化机制，将专家混合层与分组查询注意力整合到波函数架构中，以低计算开销提升模型的表达能力。训练时使用所有参数化哈密顿量共享权重的单一模型进行变分蒙特卡罗（variational Monte Carlo）求解。

Result: 在半导体莫尔异质双层（semiconductor moiré heterobilayers）中，QERNEL 成功对最多含150个电子的相互作用系统进行训练。该模型能够捕获莫尔势阱深度调控下的量子液体（quantum liquid）与量子晶体（quantum crystal）两种基态，并准确识别出二者之间以相互作用能和电荷密度突变标志的尖锐相变（sharp phase transition）。

Conclusion: QERNEL 建立了莫尔量子材料的基础模型，其可扩展的架构为构建面向固体的通用大型电子模型（Large Electron Model）提供了可行方向。

Abstract: We introduce QERNEL, a foundational neural wavefunction that variationally solves families of parameterized many-electron Hamiltonians and captures their ground states throughout parameter space within a single model. QERNEL combines FiLM-based parameter conditioning with scale-efficient architectural elements -- mixture of experts and grouped-query attention, substantially improving expressivity at low computational cost. We apply QERNEL to interacting electrons in semiconductor moiré heterobilayers, training a single weight-shared model for systems of up to 150 electrons. By solving the many-electron Schrödinger equation conditioned on moiré potential depth, QERNEL captures both quantum liquid and crystal states and discovers the sharp phase transition between them, marked by abrupt changes in interaction energy and charge density. Our work establishes a foundation model for moiré quantum materials and a scalable architecture toward a Large Electron Model for solids.

Abstract: After growing successfully high quality VP$_2$ single crystals, we studied systematically their longitudinal $ρ_{xx}(T)$ and Hall resistivity $ρ_{yx}(T)$ at various magnetic fields, combining the electronic band and Fermi surface (FS) calculations. Band calculations reveal that VP$_2$ is a type-II nodal-line semimetal, evidenced by the Hall resistivity measurements. It is found that the magnetoresistance (MR) at higher magnetic fields exhibits a linear behavior and does not show any sign of saturation, reaching 170\% at 40 K up to 9 T, which is determined by the intrinsic electronic structure and dominated by the Lorenz force, demonstrated by the resistivity anisotropy measurements and the numerical simulations. ### [85] [Torsion Induced Asymmetric Luttinger Liquids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26617)
*Arseny Pantsialei,Nicholas Sedlmayr*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究了在宇称（parity）和时间反演（time reversal）对称性同时破缺但复合对称性保持完整的系统中，Luttinger液体的一般模型，发现自旋自由度通常会产生能隙（gapped），从而形成具有不对称速度的有效无自旋Luttinger液体，并在谱函数中表现出可观测的不对称特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前对Luttinger液体的研究多集中于无自旋最小模型，而实际系统中宇称和时间反演对称性可能同时破缺（如纳米线中的扭转（torsion）与塞曼场（Zeeman field）的组合），其物理效应尚不清晰。本文旨在建立一个更一般的自旋全模型，系统分析此类对称性破缺下的物理行为。

Method: 构建了具有所有可能的散射项和相互作用项的自旋全玻色化模型（bosonic model），分析对称性破缺导致的能带结构变化，并通过重整化方法研究自旋自由度的行为。

Result: 在一般条件下，自旋自由度会打开能隙，系统退化为具有不对称速度的有效无自旋Luttinger液体；这种速度不对称性可在谱函数（spectral function）中作为实验可观测特征体现。

Conclusion: 该工作将之前仅针对无自旋Luttinger液体最小模型的研究推广到更一般的情形，揭示了复合对称性保护下不对称速度的自旋隙化行为，并为实验探测此类不对称性提供了谱函数这一可观测途径。

Abstract: We consider a general model of a Luttinger liquid with broken parity and time reversal symmetry, but with their composite symmetry intact. Such a scenario can be due to a combination of torsion and a Zeeman field in nanowires, or a result of bringing different helical Luttinger liquids into proximity. The broken symmetries result in a band structure with no axis of symmetry, and therefore with asymmetric velocities between left and right moving contributions. By taking a general spin-full model with all possible scattering and interaction terms in the bosonic model we show that generically the spin degree of freedom becomes gapped out, resulting in an effective spinless Luttinger liquid with asymmetric velocities. Our work generalizes and extends previous studies which focused on a minimal model of a spinless Luttinger liquid. We further demonstrate that a possible experimental signature of the asymmetry of such asymmetric models can be seen in the spectral function.

### [86] [Electronic structure, quasiparticle renormalizations, and magnetic correlations in the alternating single-layer bilayer nickelate La$_5$Ni$_3$O$_{11}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26627)
*I. V. Leonov*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用 DFT+DMFT 方法研究新型层状镍氧化物 La₅Ni₃O₁₁（1212-LNO）的正常态电子结构与磁关联，揭示了单层与双层镍离子的轨道依赖强关联效应、轨道选择 Mott 绝缘态、以及压力下金属-绝缘体相变，并发现磁关联从单层主导到双层主导的交叉行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解新型交替单层-双层 Ruddlesden-Popper 镍氧化物 La₅Ni₃O₁₁（1212-LNO）的正常态电子结构（normal-state electronic structure）和磁关联（magnetic correlations），特别关注由于结构差异导致的轨道依赖关联效应。

Method: 采用 DFT+DMFT（密度泛函理论+动力学平均场理论）方法对 1212-LNO 体系进行第一性原理电子结构计算和磁关联分析。

Result: 双层镍离子的 e_g 电子态形成强重整化准粒子能带（重整化因子 m^*/m 约 3.5~4.2）；单层镍离子呈现轨道选择 Mott 绝缘态（orbital-selective Mott insulating state），其中 3z²-r² 轨道开能隙，x²-y² 轨道表现为非费米液体（non-Fermi-liquid）行为。磁关联分析显示双层 NiO₆ 板块形成自旋-电荷密度波条纹，主要不稳定性对应波矢 Q=(1/3,1/3)，竞争态为 (1/4,1/4) 双共线条纹。压力下发生轨道选择 Mott 绝缘体-金属相变，单层 e_g 态金属化并呈现坏金属行为。磁关联从 DFT 结果重构，存在单层到双层主导的交叉。

Conclusion: 1212-LNO 中单层与双层镍离子因约束效应（confinement）和轨道依赖关联（orbital-dependent correlations）呈现截然不同的电子态；磁关联与双层层状材料类似，但存在从单层到双层主导的交叉演化，压力可实现轨道选择绝缘体-金属相变。

Abstract: Using DFT+DMFT we study the normal-state electronic structure and magnetic correlations of the recently discovered alternating single-layer bilayer Raddlesden-Popper nickelate La$_5$Ni$_3$O$_{11}$ (1212-LNO). Our results exhibit qualitative differences for the structurally distinct single-layer and bilayer Ni ions, implying the importance of confinement and orbital-dependent correlations. The Ni $e_g$ electronic states originating from the bilayer Ni ions form strongly renormalized quasiparticle bands with a large enhancement factor $m^*/m \sim 3.5$ and 4.2 for the Ni $x^2-y^2$ and $3z^2-r^2$ orbitals, respectively. Moreover, the $e_g$ states of the single-layer Ni ions exhibit an orbital-selective Mott insulating state, with a narrow energy gap for the Ni $3z^2-r^2$ states and metallic, strongly incoherent (non-Fermi-liquid) Ni $x^2-y^2$ ones. Our analysis of magnetic correlations suggests the formation of intertwined spin and charge density wave stripes in the bilayer NiO$_6$ slab, in close similarity to the double-layer material. We refine two major instabilities, a leading one is associated with a wave vector ${\bf Q}=(\frac{1}{3},\frac{1}{3})$ (``up-down-0" spin pattern), competing with the bicollinear $(\frac{1}{4},\frac{1}{4})$ (``up-up-down-down") stripe state. The single-layer Ni $3d$ electrons exhibit instability towards the Néel-type magnetic state. Under pressure, 1212-LNO undergoes an orbital-selective Mott insulator-to-metal phase transition, associated with metallization of the single-layer Ni $e_g$ states. As a result, the single-layer Ni $e_g$ bands exhibit non-Fermi-liquid (bad metal) behavior with strongly incoherent spectral weights near $E_F$. We note that correlation effects result in a reconstruction of magnetic correlations as compared to that obtained within DFT. In fact, we observe a crossover from single-layer to double-layer dominated magnetic correlations.

Abstract: We report a comprehensive investigation of the anisotropic magnetism and magnetic field-induced transitions in single crystals of the orthorhombic system TbAlGe, a member of the topological RAlGe (R = rare-earth) family with the highest ordering temeprature in the RAlX (X = Si, Ge) series. ### [88] [Kondo transport in an anisotropic two-dimensional electron gas with quadratic momentum-dependent spin splitting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26767)
*M. R. Parymuda*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文发展了一套格林函数（Green's function）框架，研究具有二次自旋织构（quadratic spin texture）的各向异性二维电子气（two-dimensional electron gas）在 S=1/2 近藤杂质（Kondo impurity）存在下的输运性质。分析表明，纵向电阻率修正与二次自旋劈裂耦合系数 α 密切相关，并发现当 α 达到临界值 α_cr 时，近藤温度 T_K 相对于传统二维电子气下降约 37%，标志着近藤塌缩（Kondo collapse）的出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来具有自旋织构的二维电子气在自旋电子学（spintronics）与关联电子物理中受到关注，但其中近藤杂质效应如何受到二次自旋劈裂耦合的影响尚不明确。本文旨在填补这一空白，从微观理论层面揭示自旋织构与近藤散射（Kondo scattering）的耦合机制及其对输运行为的调控。

Method: 基于低能有效 k·p 模型描述各向异性二次自旋织构，建立格林函数框架以同时处理自旋织构与近藤散射；在 s-d 交换耦合（s-d exchange coupling）的三阶微扰下，计算纵向电阻率修正 Δρ^{xx}/ρ^{xx}_0 和 Δρ^{yy}/ρ^{yy}_0，并推导近藤温度 T_K 的表达式。

Result: 纵向电阻率修正随温度的变化呈现出典型的近藤行为，而其大小与二次自旋劈裂耦合系数 α 呈负相关；近藤温度 T_K 随 α 增加而强烈抑制；当 α 达到临界值 α_cr 时，T_K 相对于常规二维电子气降低了约 37%，表明系统进入近藤塌缩（Kondo collapse）区域。

Conclusion: 二次自旋织构的各向异性耦合可有效抑制近藤效应，甚至引发近藤塌缩，为通过能带工程（band engineering）手段调控关联电子态提供了新的理论途径。该框架可推广至其他具有自旋-轨道耦合的二维体系中的杂质输运问题。

Abstract: We investigate the transport properties of an anisotropic two-dimensional electron gas with a quadratic spin texture, described by a low-energy effective $ k\cdot p$ model, in the presence of $S=1/2$ Kondo impurities. We develop a Green's function framework that captures the interplay between the spin texture and the Kondo scattering for calculating transport properties in such systems. Using this framework, we evaluate the longitudinal resistivity corrections $Δρ^{xx}/ρ^{xx}_0$ and $Δρ^{yy}/ρ^{yy}_0$ to third order in the $s$-$d$ exchange coupling and analyze their temperature dependence. We further determine the Kondo temperature $T_K$ and show that it is strongly suppressed with increasing quadratic spin-splitting coupling $α$. In particular, we identify a critical coupling $α_{cr}$ marking the onset of a Kondo collapse, at which $T_K$ is reduced by approximately 37\% relative to that of the conventional two-dimensional electron gas.

### [89] [Finite-Temperature Ferromagnetic Correlations of the Kagome Lattice Hubbard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26827)
*Francisco Correia,Kyle Corbett,Ehsan Khatami*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用数值链接团簇展开（numerical linked-cluster expansion）和行列式量子蒙特卡洛（determinant quantum Monte Carlo）两种精确有限温方法，系统研究了Kagome晶格Fermi-Hubbard模型中铁磁关联的掺杂与相互作用依赖性，发现排斥相互作用在高电子密度下增强铁磁关联，并随相互作用强度增大将强铁磁区域延伸至半填充，与Mott绝缘区附近的永田铁磁性（Nagaoka ferromagnetism）平滑连接。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kagome晶格Fermi-Hubbard模型是强关联物理（strongly-correlated physics）中最具物理丰富性但也最具挑战性的模型之一，其几何阻挫（geometric frustration）和平带（flat energy band）特性在能带绝缘体极限附近有利于铁磁性，但对该模型铁磁关联的掺杂与相互作用依赖性的全面理解尚不充分。

Method: 本文采用两种精确的有限温（finite-temperature）方法：数值链接团簇展开（numerical linked-cluster expansion）和行列式量子蒙特卡洛（determinant quantum Monte Carlo），研究铁磁关联及其他热力学性质。

Result: 研究发现：(1) 排斥相互作用（repulsive interactions）在高电子密度下增强铁磁关联；(2) 增大相互作用强度可将强铁磁关联区域延伸至半填充（half filling），并与Mott绝缘区附近的永田铁磁性（Nagaoka ferromagnetism）平滑连接；(3) 利用电荷压缩率（charge compressibility）获得了半填充处金属-绝缘体转变（metal-insulator transition）的临界相互作用强度的准确估计。

Conclusion: 这些结果增进了对模型在半填充之外磁倾向（magnetic tendencies）的理解，为包括光晶格（optical lattices）中超冷原子（ultracold atoms）在内的进一步研究铺平了道路。

Abstract: The Kagome lattice Fermi-Hubbard model is one of the most physically rich, and at the same time most challenging, models to study in strongly-correlated physics. Among its special features are geometric frustration and a flat energy band that create conditions favorable to ferromagnetism near the band insulating limit. Here, we utilize two exact finite-temperature methods, the numerical linked-cluster expansion and the determinant quantum Monte Carlo, to study the extent as well as doping and interaction dependence of ferromagnetic correlations and other thermodynamic properties of the model. We find that repulsive interactions enhance ferromagnetic correlations at high electron densities and that increasing the interaction strength, extends the region with strong ferromagnetic correlations towards half filling, smoothly connecting it to Nagaoka ferromagnetism near the Mott insulating region. We also use the charge compressibility to obtain an accurate estimate for the critical interaction strength for the metal-insulator transition at half filling. These results improve our understanding of the magnetic tendencies of the model away from half filling and pave the way for further studies, including with ultracold atoms in optical lattices.

### [90] [Ballistic Exciton Flow Driven by Intertwined Exciton-Electron Orders in a Moiré Superlattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26871)
*Shibin Deng,Jonas M. Peterson,Jonas Reimann,Heonjoon Park,Ammon Fischer,Takashi Taniguchi,Kenji Watanabe,Xiaodong Xu,Dante M. Kennes,Libai Huang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过超快光致发光和反射显微镜实验，结合密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization group, DMRG）数值模拟，揭示了WSe₂/WS₂异质双层中莫尔超晶格（moiré superlattice）中激子（exciton）与电子晶格（correlated electron lattices）之间强排斥相互作用驱动集体弹道输运（collective ballistic exciton transport）的物理机制，并展示了系统从弹道膨胀到混合电子-激子Mott态（mixed electron-exciton Mott state）的动力学演化过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过渡金属硫族化物（transition-metal dichalcogenides, TMDs）莫尔超晶格为研究强相互作用的玻色-费米混合物（Bose-Fermi mixtures）提供了理想平台，其中玻色型激子与关联电子晶格共存。理解这类体系中激子-电子和激子-激子强排斥作用如何影响激子输运行为，是探索多体量子态动力学和量子相变的关键科学问题。

Method: 采用超快时间分辨和能量分辨的光致发光（photoluminescence, PL）与反射显微镜（reflectance microscopy）技术，测量WSe₂/WS₂异质双层中的激子动力学；利用密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization group, DMRG）求解一维玻色-费米哈伯德模型（Bose-Fermi Hubbard model），对实验结果进行定性重现和物理机制验证。

Result: 实验观察到激子弹道输运具有能量选择性：排斥相互作用将激子驱动到更高的莫尔激子带（moiré exciton band），增强的位点间跳跃（intersite hopping）导致快速空间扩展，激子均方位移（mean-squared displacement, MSD）呈现二次时间依赖关系（∝ t²）。该弹道膨胀在分数电子填充（fractional electron fillings）形成广义维格纳晶格（generalized Wigner-crystal, GWC）序时被显著增强；之后系统因俄歇复合（Auger recombination）和密度耗尽而过渡到混合电子-激子Mott态。DMRG模拟定性地重现了激子输运和时间依赖响应，并证实强交叉物种相互作用使电子晶格“穿透”激子Mott背景，加速其熔化并增强激子运动。

Conclusion: 研究确立了莫尔TMDs作为高度可调控平台用于实现强相互作用的玻色-费米混合物，展示了交织的玻色子和电子序的实时控制，并为激子绝缘体-流体相变（exciton insulator-fluid transition）提供了新路线。

Abstract: Moiré superlattices of transition-metal dichalcogenides (TMDs) host strongly interacting Bose-Fermi mixtures in which bosonic excitons coexist with correlated electron lattices. Using ultrafast, time- and energy-resolved photoluminescence (PL) and reflectance microscopy, we show that strong exciton-electron and exciton-exciton repulsion can enable collective ballistic exciton transport in a WSe$_2$/WS$_2$ heterobilayer. The ballistic transport is energy-selective: repulsive interactions drive excitons into a higher moiré exciton band, where enhanced intersite hopping enables rapid spatial expansion. Correspondingly, the exciton mean-squared displacement (MSD) exhibits a quadratic time dependence ($\propto t^2$). This ballistic expansion is enhanced at fractional electron fillings where the electrons form generalized Wigner-crystal (GWC) orders. Afterwards, the system transitions into a mixed electron-exciton Mott state as Auger recombination and density depletion conclude the ballistic expansion. A one-dimensional Bose-Fermi Hubbard model solved using density-matrix renormalization group (DMRG) qualitatively reproduces the measured exciton transport and time-dependent response. It further confirms that strong cross-species interactions allow the electron crystal to perforate the exciton Mott background, accelerating its melting and enhancing exciton motion. Our results establish moiré TMDs as highly tunable platforms for realizing strongly interacting Bose-Fermi mixtures, which we employ here to demonstrate real-time control of intertwined bosonic and electronic order and to establish a route to the exciton insulator-fluid transition.

</details>


### [91] [Schwinger-Boson Mean-Field Study of the Anisotropic Kagome Antiferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26907)
*Sankha Subhra Bakshi,Brandon B. Le,Seung-Hun Lee,Gia-Wei Chern*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用Schwinger玻色子平均场理论，研究了空间交换各向异性对自旋-1/2 kagome反铁磁体的影响，发现各向异性重构低能自旋子能带，导致自旋子能隙闭合和磁有序转变，并给出各向异性磁有序的微观图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解空间交换各向异性如何驱动kagome自旋液体向磁有序的转变，并为解释各向异性kagome材料（尤其是钛基自旋-1/2化合物）的实验现象提供理论框架。

Method: 采用Schwinger-boson mean-field theory（Schwinger玻色子平均场理论），引入反映晶格对称性降低的projective-symmetry-group ansätze（投影对称群拟设），聚焦于与常规q=0态和√3×√3态对应的0-flux和π-flux态。

Result: 各向异性主要重构低能自旋子（spinon）能带，导致最低自旋子支的强烈软化和双自旋子连续谱（two-spinon continuum）的下移。在足够大的各向异性参数δ下，自旋子能隙在拟设依赖的特定值处闭合，标志自旋子凝聚（spinon condensation）和磁有序不稳定性。从软化的Bogoliubov本征模重构了起始自旋织构（incipient spin textures），发现磁有序本质上是各向异性的：强耦合键上磁矩被抑制，弱连接位点上磁矩增强。

Conclusion: 交换各向异性驱动kagome自旋液体态向各向异性磁有序的转变，为理解各向异性kagome材料（特别是钛基自旋-1/2化合物）的实验观测提供了微观理论支持。

Abstract: We investigate the effect of spatial exchange anisotropy on the spin-$1/2$ kagome antiferromagnet using Schwinger-boson mean-field theory. The anisotropy is introduced by strengthening the Heisenberg exchange along one set of nearest-neighbor bonds relative to the other two, and is controlled by a parameter $δ$ that measures the deviation from the isotropic limit. Incorporating the reduced lattice symmetry, we construct the corresponding projective-symmetry-group ansätze and focus on representative $0$- and $π$-flux states connected to the conventional $q=0$ and $\sqrt{3}\times\sqrt{3}$ kagome states. We find that anisotropy predominantly reconstructs the low-energy spinon sector, leading to a strong softening of the lowest spinon branch and a downward shift of the two-spinon continuum. At sufficiently large $δ$, the spinon gap closes at ansatz-dependent values, signaling an instability toward spinon condensation and the onset of magnetic order. From the soft Bogoliubov eigenmodes, we reconstruct the associated incipient spin textures and show that the resulting magnetic orders are intrinsically anisotropic, with suppressed moments on strongly coupled bonds and enhanced moments on more weakly connected sites. These results provide a microscopic picture of how exchange anisotropy drives the transition from kagome spin-liquid states to magnetic order, and offer a framework for interpreting recent experiments on anisotropic kagome materials, particularly titanium-based spin-$1/2$ compounds.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一个集成工作流（integrated workflow），将版本控制（version control）、代码审查（code review）、自动化测试（automated testing）、结构化日志（structured logging）、元数据丰富的输出（metadata-rich output）和标准化后处理（standardized post-processing）相结合，以支持从软件开发到出版物的可追溯性（traceability）。

Result: 所提出的概念针对一个特定的仿真框架进行了演示，并表明该工作流广泛适用于计算物理学及其他数据密集型科学计算领域。

Conclusion: 该工作流为数值物理研究提供了可重复且符合FAIR原则的实践方案，能够跨领域推广至其他数据密集型的科学计算场景。

Abstract: Computational physics increasingly depends on large simulation datasets generated by software that remains under active development for many years. In such settings, reproducibility requires not only well documented data but also explicit links between code versions, simulation inputs, generated outputs, analysis steps, and published figures. Here, we present an integrated workflow for reproducible and FAIR-aligned simulation research in numerical physics. We describe how version control, code review, automated testing, structured logging, metadata-rich output, and standardized post-processing can be combined to support traceability from software development to publication. The presented concepts demonstrated for one particular simulation framework are broadly applicable to computational physics and other data-intensive areas of scientific computing.

### [93] [Resonance Statistics -Informed Fitting Applied to Automated Cross Section Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25947)
*William Fritsch,Noah Walton,Justin Loring,Jacob Forbes,Oleksii Zivenko,Aaron Clark,Elan Park-Bernstein,Vladimir Sobes*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文探讨了在共振评估中利用共振统计量（resonance statistics）来辅助自旋群（spin group）分配，并提出一种替代传统卡方统计量（chi-squared statistic）的拟合目标函数。基于共振统计量的方法被应用于N. Walton等人开发的自动共振拟合框架。新的共振统计量引导的自旋群混洗算法减少了基础拟合算法中存在的自旋群频率偏差。虽然共振统计量引导的优化对逐点截面（pointwise cross section）一致性改善甚微，但它显著增强了对维格纳能级间距统计量（Wigner level-spacing statistics）的符合度，并在模型不完善时稳定了拟合的共振密度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的共振拟合通常依赖卡方统计量作为目标函数，但这种方法在自旋群分配和共振统计一致性方面存在局限。本文旨在探索共振统计量在自动化共振拟合框架中的应用，以改善自旋群分配并提高拟合结果的统计合理性。

Method: 基于共振统计量（resonance statistics）开发了新的自旋群混洗算法（spin group shuffling algorithm），并设计了替代卡方统计量的拟合目标函数。这些方法被嵌入到N. Walton等人建立的自动共振拟合框架中，用以指导共振评价过程。

Result: 新的算法有效减少了基础拟合算法中的自旋群频率偏差（spin group frequency bias）。在逐点截面一致性上变化不显著，但拟合结果与维格纳能级间距统计量（Wigner level-spacing statistics）的符合度明显改善，且在模型存在不完善时共振密度（resonance density）的拟合稳定性得到提升。

Conclusion: 引入共振统计量信息可以提升自动共振拟合框架的统计一致性，尤其是在自旋群分配和共振密度稳定性方面。该工作为核数据评价中超越传统卡方统计量的拟合策略提供了可行路径。

Abstract: This work investigates the use of resonance statistics for resonance evaluation to inform spin group assignment and an alternative fitting objective function beyond the commonly used chi-squared statistic. Resonance statistics -informed methods are applied to the automated resonance fitting framework, developed by N. Walton et al. In this automated framework, the utility of resonance statistics is largely unexplored. The new resonance statistics -informed spin group shuffling algorithm reduces spin group frequency bias seen in the base fitting algorithm. Although resonance statistics -informed optimization produces negligible changes in pointwise cross section agreement, it significantly improves consistency with Wigner level-spacing statistics and stabilizes the fitted resonance density in the presence of model imperfections.

### [94] [Accelerating finite-element-based projector augmented-wave density functional theory calculations with scalable GPU-centric computational methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26037)
*Kartick Ramakrishnan,Phani Motamarri*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于有限元（finite-element）离散化和投影缀加波（projector augmented-wave, PAW）公式的GPU中心计算方法（PAW-FE），用于在百亿亿次（exascale）计算系统上实现大规模Kohn-Sham密度泛函理论（DFT）的精确高效计算。通过残差型切比雪夫滤波子空间迭代（R-ChFSI）、混合精度算术和近似逆PAW重叠矩阵等创新，该方法在NVIDIA GPU上相比平面波PAW方法实现了近8倍的加速，并展示了高达130,000电子系统的可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模Kohn-Sham密度泛函理论（DFT）计算对模拟复杂材料系统（如界面、缺陷、纳米团簇和扭曲二维异质结构）至关重要，但现有DFT实现在10^4–10^5电子尺度下难以同时达到化学精度（chemical accuracy）和实际可行的计算时间。

Method: 采用有限元（finite-element）离散化的投影缀加波（projector augmented-wave, PAW）公式（PAW-FE），在共线自旋形式（collinear spin formalism）中开发。利用多分辨率求积（multi-resolution quadrature）在粗网格上精确计算原子中心PAW积分。广义Hermite本征问题通过残差型切比雪夫滤波子空间迭代（R-ChFSI）求解，利用其对不精确矩阵-多向量积的容忍性，采用近似逆PAW重叠矩阵、混合精度算术（FP32/TF32）和低精度最近邻通信（BF16），并结合分块计算-通信重叠策略。

Result: 在Intel和AMD GPU架构上分别实现最高8倍和20倍的CPU-GPU加速；在NVIDIA GPU上，针对10,000电子系统，相比平面波PAW方法实现近8倍的时间加速，相比模守恒（norm-conserving）FE方法实现约6倍加速；展示了高达130,000电子系统的可扩展性。

Conclusion: PAW-FE被确立为一种面向百亿亿次（exascale）系统的、可达成化学精度第一性原理模拟的方法。

Abstract: Accurate large-scale Kohn-Sham density functional theory (DFT) calculations are essential for modeling complex material systems, including interfaces, defects, nanoclusters, and twisted two-dimensional heterostructures. Achieving chemical accuracy at scales of $10^4$-$10^5$ electrons with practical time-to-solution, however, remains challenging for existing DFT implementations. We present GPU-centric computational methods and algorithmic innovations within a finite-element (FE) discretized projector augmented-wave (PAW) formulation (PAW-FE) for accurate, efficient, and scalable electronic-structure calculations on modern exascale systems. The FE discretization, developed within a collinear spin formalism, accommodates generic boundary conditions and employs multi-resolution quadrature for accurate evaluation of atom-centered PAW integrals on coarse grids. The resulting generalized Hermitian eigenproblem is solved using residual-based Chebyshev filtered subspace iteration (R-ChFSI). Exploiting R-ChFSI's tolerance to inexact matrix-multivector products, we employ an approximate inverse PAW overlap matrix, mixed-precision arithmetic (FP32/TF32), and low-precision nearest-neighbor communication (BF16) during filtered subspace construction, along with block-wise computation-communication overlap to reduce cost while preserving robustness. These strategies yield up to $8\times$ and $20\times$ CPU-GPU speedups on Intel and AMD GPU architectures, respectively. Compared to plane-wave PAW methods, PAW-FE achieves close to 8$\times$ reduction in time-to-solution for 10,000-electron systems on NVIDIA GPUs, with larger gains at scale, and around 6$\times$ over norm-conserving FE approaches. We demonstrate scalability to 130,000-electron systems, establishing PAW-FE as an exascale-ready method for chemically accurate first-principles simulations.

</details>


### [95] [Mixture of Experts Framework in Machine Learning Interatomic Potentials for Atomistic Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26143)
*Gabriel de Miranda Nascimento,Marc L. Descoteaux,Laura Zichi,Chuin Wei Tan,William C. Witt,Nicola Molinari,Sriteja Mantha,Daniil Kitchaev,Mordechai Kornbluth,Karim Gadelrab,Charles Tuffile,Boris Kozinsky*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于E(3)-等变Allegro架构的多保真度“专家混合”（Mixture-of-Experts）框架，通过空间域分解和协同训练策略，在Pt+CO催化体系中实现了与全高保真模拟相当的预测精度，同时计算速度提升两倍以上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 第一性原理原子模拟对于理解复杂材料现象至关重要，但受限于计算成本。尽管机器学习原子间势（MLIP）在给定精度下大幅降低了成本，但其推理成本在模拟大系统或长时间尺度时仍是瓶颈。

Method: 基于E(3)-等变Allegro架构，将模拟域空间划分为化学复杂区域（如反应界面）和简单区域（如体相晶格），为不同区域分配不同容量的模型。通过协同训练策略，在损失函数中加入一致性约束（agreement constraints），对模型在共享体相环境中的逐原子能量和力差异施加惩罚，迫使独立模型学习一致的体相材料物理描述。

Result: 在真实的Pt+CO催化体系上验证该方法：协同训练的模型保持精确能量守恒；体相力学响应（如状态方程和体模量）一致；预测精度与全高保真模拟相当，计算速度提升两倍以上。

Conclusion: 所提出的多保真度专家混合框架通过空间域分解与协同训练，有效解决了界面力学不匹配问题，在保证精度前提下显著提升计算效率，适用于大系统或长时间尺度的原子模拟。

Abstract: First-principles atomistic simulations are essential for understanding complex material phenomena but are fundamentally limited by their computational cost. While Machine Learning Interatomic Potentials (MLIPs) have drastically improved cost for a given accuracy, their inference cost remains a bottleneck for massive systems or long timescales. To address this, we introduce a multifidelity "Mixture-of-Experts" framework based on the E(3)-equivariant Allegro architecture. Our method spatially partitions the simulation domain into a chemically complex region (e.g., reactive interfaces) and a simple region (e.g., bulk lattice), assigning models of varying capacity to each. Among the challenges in such static domain decomposition, the mechanical mismatch between models at the interface is particularly critical, as it can generate artificial stress fields and instability. We address this challenge with a co-training strategy in which the loss function includes agreement constraints -- penalties on per-atom energy and force discrepancies between models evaluated on shared bulk environments -- forcing the independent models to learn a consistent physical description of the bulk material. We validate this approach on a realistic Pt+CO catalytic system, demonstrating that the co-trained models maintain exact energy conservation, align their bulk mechanical response (e.g., equation of state and bulk modulus), and achieve predictive accuracy comparable to a full high-fidelity simulation at more than twice the computational speed.

### [96] [On matrix Lax representations for (1+1)-dimensional evolutionary differential-difference equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26870)

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文研究了微分-差分矩阵Lax表示（Lax对）、规范变换（gauge transformations）和离散Miura型变换（MTs）之间的理论关系，提出了简化MLR、利用MLR构造MT以及判定非虚假MLR的新方法，并将该一般理论应用于构造若干新的双分量可积方程。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Differential-difference matrix Lax representations (Lax pairs), gauge transformations, and discrete Miura-type transformations (MTs) belong to the main tools in the theory of (nonlinear) integrable differential-difference equations.
  For a given equation, two matrix Lax representations (MLRs) are said to be gauge equivalent if one of them can be obtained from the other by applying a matrix gauge transformation. Generalizing and extending several previous works on MLRs and MTs, we present new results on the following problems:
  - When and how can one simplify a given MLR by means of gauge transformations?
  - How can one use MLRs and gauge transformations for constructing MTs?
  - A MLR is called fake if it is gauge equivalent to a trivial MLR. How to determine whether a given MLR is not fake?
  We consider the general (1+1)-dimensional evolutionary differential-difference case when a MLR can depend on any shifts of dependent variables and can be non-autonomous. As applications and illustrations of the presented general theory, we construct several new two-component integrable equations (with new MLRs) connected by new MTs to known integrable equations from the papers [S. Konstantinou-Rizos, A.V. Mikhailov, P. Xenitidis, J. Math. Phys. 2015], [E. Mansfield, G. Mari Beffa, Jing Ping Wang, Found. Comput. Math. 2013]), including non-autonomous examples.

### [97] [On Quantum Obstructions in Type IIA Orientifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25988)
*Lukas Kaufmann,Timo Weigand,Max Wiesner*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究四维N=1超引力理论中经典无限距离极限（infinite distance limits）在量子修正下的消失效应。通过分析Type IIA定向形（orientifold）的Kähler模空间（Kähler moduli sector），并借助M理论到G₂流形的提升（uplift）及世界面理论（worldsheet theory）等方法，作者论证了量子层面上无限距离方向不再存在，且该结论适用于以往在Type IIB框架中未能检测到量子阻碍的极限情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子修正可能显著修改甚至消除四维最小N=1超引力理论中的经典无限距离极限。然而，这一效应在定向形模空间（orientifold moduli space）的Kähler模扇区中，特别是来自4d N=2矢量多重态扇区的部分，尚未得到系统研究。本研究旨在澄清这些无限距离方向在量子层面上是否仍然存在。

Method: 作者提供了多重独立论证：基于有效场论弦（EFT strings）的世界面理论、渐近无质量粒子塔（asymptotically massless tower of particles）的分析，以及将理论提升（uplift）至G₂流形上的M理论，从而统一处理在Type IIB/F理论框架中看似不同起源的量子阻碍（quantum obstructions）。

Result: 在固定的四维胀子（four-dimensional dilaton）下，经典Type IIA定向形的Kähler模扇区中的无限距离极限在量子层面上被消除。这一结论也适用于之前在Type IIB框架中未能检测到量子阻碍的无限距离极限。量子层面上，来自4d N=2矢量多重态扇区的定向形模空间中的无限距离极限，只有在其余部分模量也趋于无穷时才可能存在。

Conclusion: 量子修正有效地移除了Type IIA定向形Kähler模扇区中的经典无限距离方向，表明量子效应在超引力模空间几何中起着关键约束作用。该结果通过M理论在G₂流形上的统一描述得到了跨对偶框架的验证。

Abstract: Quantum corrections can severely modify or even remove classical infinite distance limits in four-dimensional gravity theories with minimal N=1 supersymmetry. In this note we study this effect for infinite distance directions in the classical Kähler moduli sector of Type IIA orientifolds at fixed four-dimensional dilaton. We present several independent arguments why such infinite distance directions are absent at the quantum level. These involve the worldsheet theory of EFT strings and the putative asymptotically massless tower of particles. Key insights are provided by the uplift to M-theory on G2 manifolds, which allows for a unified treatment of quantum obstructions of seemingly different origin in the dual Type IIB/F-theory frame. Our results apply also to the Type IIA dual of infinite distance limits for which no quantum obstruction could be detected in the Type IIB frame in previous work. In conclusion, infinite distance limits in the part of the orientifold moduli space descending from a 4d N=2 vector multiplet sector are only possible at the quantum level if also some of the remaining moduli are taken to infinity.

</details>


### [98] [Lattice Topological Defects in Non-Unitary Conformal Field Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25999)
*Madhav Sinha,Thiago Silva Tavares,Hubert Saleur,Ananda Roy*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用限制型固-固模型（restricted solid-on-solid models）的变体，在非幺正共形场论（non-unitary conformal field theories）中研究拓扑缺陷（topological defects）的构造与性质，通过数值计算与解析预测对比验证，并分析了重整化群流（renormalization group flows）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑缺陷在量子场论（quantum field theories）的对称性研究中具有基础性作用。已有方法可在二维共形场论（conformal field theories）中借助格点模型（lattice models）构造拓扑缺陷，但针对非幺正共形场论的情形尚缺乏系统的构造与分析。

Method: 采用限制型固-固模型（restricted solid-on-solid models）的适当变体，在格点系统中构造相应的杂质模型（impurity models）及缺陷算符（defect operators）；对能谱（energy spectrum）、缺陷算符本征值以及热力学量（thermodynamic characteristics）进行数值计算，并与解析预测进行比较；利用数值方法分析不同不动点（fixed points）之间的重整化群流（renormalization group flows）。

Result: 成功在非幺正共形场论中构造了拓扑缺陷对应的杂质模型与缺陷算符；数值计算的能谱、缺陷算符本征值及热力学量结果与解析预测相符。

Conclusion: 本文提出的格点构造方法可有效应用于非幺正共形场论中的拓扑缺陷研究，数值结果验证了相关解析理论的正确性。

Abstract: Topological defects play a fundamental role in the investigation of symmetries in quantum field theories. For conformal field theories in two space-time dimensions, it is possible to construct these defects using lattice models allowing ab-initio analytical and numerical computations of their characteristics. In this work, topological defects are investigated in non-unitary conformal field theories using appropriate variations of the restricted solid-on-solid models. The relevant impurity models and the corresponding defect operators are constructed for the lattice system. Numerical computations are performed for the energy spectrum, eigenvalues of the defect operators as well as thermodynamic characteristics and compared with analytical predictions. Finally, renormalization group flows between the different fixed points are analyzed using numerical methods.

</details>


### [99] [Quantum mechanical bootstrap without inequalities: SYK bilinear spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26007)
*Kok Hong Thong,David Vegh*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出一种“直接自举法”（direct bootstrap），通过考虑算符的分数幂（fractional powers of operators）导出约束方程，在不依赖正定性的条件下确定与SYK模型双线性算符谱一致的量子力学系统的本征值，且截断阶数增加时收敛到精确本征值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准基于正定性（positivity）的量子力学自举法（quantum mechanical bootstrap）无法区分决定Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev（SYK）谱的边界条件（boundary conditions），因而不足以为该系统确定本征值。

Method: 放弃正定性约束，转而利用算符的分数幂构建约束方程（constraint equations），通过增加截断阶数（truncation order）使解的根收敛到精确本征值。

Result: 随着截断阶数的提高，所得根（roots）逐步收敛到系统精确的本征值（exact eigenvalues）。

Conclusion: 这种不依赖正定性假设的“直接自举法”能够有效确定与SYK模型双线性算符谱相同的量子系统的本征值，为标准自举方法无法区分的边界条件问题提供了解决方案。

Abstract: We study a quantum mechanical system whose spectrum coincides with that of bilinear operators of the Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev model. The standard positivity-based quantum mechanical bootstrap is degenerate with respect to the boundary data: it does not distinguish the boundary conditions that select the SYK spectrum, and hence is insufficient to determine the eigenvalues. Instead, by considering fractional powers of operators, we obtain constraint equations that determine the spectrum without imposing positivity. The resulting roots converge to exact eigenvalues as the truncation order increases. We call this the direct bootstrap.

</details>


### [100] [The Schrodinger Equation as a Gauge Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26016)
*Dmitry S. Ageev,Vladimir A. Bykov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文从规范场论（gauge field theory）的角度重新表述薛定谔方程（Schrödinger equation），建立了薛定谔方程、量子流体动力学（quantum hydrodynamics）与规范表述之间的局部等价性，并展示了该对偶性如何组织电磁耦合、贝里联络（Berry connection）、任意子（anyon）激发以及边界自由度等结构，还在非线性区域通过双二形式描述将声学记忆、大规范变换（large gauge transformation）与软定理（soft theorem）组织为红外三角形（infrared triangle）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尝试将薛定谔方程重新表述为规范场论语言，从而揭示量子力学与规范理论之间的深层结构对应关系，并统一描述此前分散的物理现象。

Method: 从马德隆表示（Madelung representation）出发，利用规范场（gauge field）改写守恒的概率流（probability-current）：在(2+1)维理论中使用一形式规范场，在(3+1)维理论中使用二形式规范场，建立局部等价性；全局信息由波函数零点周围相位缠绕的量子化（quantization of phase winding）承载。

Result: 规范一侧，BF耦合描述了电磁耦合、贝里联络、旋量动力学、投影非阿贝尔绝热联络（projected non-abelian adiabatic connection）及内蕴和乐（intrinsic holonomy）；陈-西蒙斯项（Chern–Simons term）产生霍普夫泛函（Hopf functional）、电荷-通量附着（charge-flux attachment）及任意子扇区；边界存在时，拓扑项产生边缘自由度与边界电荷代数；非线性区中，双二形式描述将声学记忆、大规范变换与软定理组织为红外三角形。

Conclusion: 该规范对偶框架为量子力学提供了一个统一的几何-拓扑视角，能够自然地涵盖电磁耦合、拓扑相、边界效应及非线性声学现象，并揭示了这些结构之间的内在关联。

Abstract: In this paper, we reformulate the Schrodinger equation in gauge-theoretic terms. Starting from the Madelung representation, we rewrite the conserved probability-current using gauge fields, namely a one-form gauge field in the $(2+1)$-dimensional theory and a two-form gauge field in the $(3+1)$-dimensional theory. This gives a local equivalence between the Schrodinger equation, quantum hydrodynamics, and a gauge formulation, while the global information is carried by the quantization of phase winding around zeros of the wavefunction. We then explore how this correspondence organizes structures on both sides of the duality. On the gauge side, BF couplings to additional one-forms describe electromagnetic coupling, Berry connections, spinor dynamics, projected non-abelian adiabatic connections, and intrinsic holonomy, while Chern--Simons term generate Hopf functionals, charge-flux attachment, and anyonic sectors. In the presence of boundaries, the topological terms produce edge degrees of freedom and boundary charge algebras. Finally, in the nonlinear regime with a Bogoliubov sound mode, the dual two-form description relates acoustic memory, large gauge transformations and the corresponding soft theorem, organizing them into an infrared triangle.

### [101] [$\mathcal{H}$olographic $\mathcal{N}$aturalness and Pre-Geometric Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26032)
*Andrea Addazi,Salvatore Capozziello,Giuseppe Meluccio*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究表明：CC的大小直接由dS熵（亦即$v$）之大所决定，大熵态的衰变被指数级压制，从而使CC保持稳定且极小。此外，新的半经典量子引力效应会动态地产生"hairons"——一种质量与CC相关联的粒子。dS空间在凝聚体演化驱动下的不稳定性，暗示暗能量具有动力学起源。

Conclusion: 该框架将几何的涌现、尺度层级以及时空的量子信息结构三者不可分割地联系在一起，为解决CC问题提供了一条全新路径。

Abstract: The cosmological constant (CC, $Λ$) problem represents a remarkable discrepancy of about 120 orders of magnitude between the observed dark energy and its natural expectation from quantum field theory. This paper synthesizes two paradigms - holographic naturalness ($\mathcal{HN}$) and pre-geometric gravity (PGG) - to propose a unified resolution. The $\mathcal{HN}$ framework posits that CC stability is not a matter of radiative corrections but of quantum information and entropy. The large entropy $S_\text{dS}\sim M_\text{P}^2/Λ$ of the de Sitter (dS) vacuum acts as an entropic barrier, exponentially suppressing destabilizing quantum transitions. This explains why the universe remains in a high-entropy, low-CC state. We embed this within PGG, where spacetime geometry and the Einstein-Hilbert action emerge dynamically from the spontaneous symmetry breaking SO($1,4$)$\rightarrow$SO($1,3$), driven by a Higgs-like field $φ^A$. Both $M_\text{P}$ and $Λ$ are generated from more fundamental parameters. Crucially, we establish a direct correspondence between the VEV $v$ of the pre-geometric Higgs field and the de Sitter entropy: $S_\text{dS}\sim v$ (or $v^3$). Thus, the field generating spacetime also encodes its information content. The smallness of $Λ$ follows directly from the largeness of $S_\text{dS}$, a manifestation of a large $v$. The CC is stable because a large-entropy state's decay is exponentially suppressed. Our study shows new semi-classical quantum gravity effects dynamically generate "hairons", particles whose mass is tied to the CC. The instability of the dS space, driven by a condensate evolution, points to a dynamical origin for dark energy. This framework inextricably links the emergence of geometry, the hierarchy of scales and the quantum-information structure of spacetime, providing a novel path toward solving the CC problem.

### [102] [The Super Virasoro Minimal String from 3d Supergravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26038)
*Lorenz Eberhardt*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 超维拉宿最小弦（super Virasoro minimal string）通过在世界面上耦合类空和类时超刘维尔理论（super Liouville theories）定义，分为四种类型（0A± 和 0B±）。该理论自然地来源于三维超引力（3d supergravity）的量子化，且其振幅计算了满足交叉对称性（crossing symmetry）的 N=1 超共形块（superconformal blocks）空间的维数或超维数。0A+ 和 0B+ 与玻色子维拉宿最小弦具有相同的矩阵积分对偶，0B- 对偶于带反平方根奇点的矩阵积分，而 0A- 的所有非平凡微扰振幅均为零。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索超维拉宿最小弦理论的定义与分类，并揭示其与三维超引力量子化以及超共形块空间维数之间的深层联系。

Method: 通过在世界面上耦合类空和类时超刘维尔理论来定义该弦论，并依据世界面上的离散选择将其分为 0A± 和 0B± 四种类型。进而分析每种理论在微扰层面对偶的矩阵积分形式及其振幅行为。

Result: 0A+ 和 0B+ 在微扰层面对偶于与玻色子维拉宿最小弦相同的矩阵积分；0B- 对偶于一个具有反平方根奇点的矩阵积分；0A- 的所有非平凡微扰振幅均为零。

Conclusion: 超维拉宿最小弦是三维超引力量子化的自然产物，其振幅编码了 N=1 超共形块模交叉对称性空间的维数（+情形）或超维数（-情形），且不同离散选择导致显著不同的对偶矩阵模型行为。

Abstract: The super Virasoro minimal string is defined by coupling spacelike and timelike super Liouville theories on the worldsheet. There are four different theories 0A$^\pm$ and 0B$^\pm$ depending on discrete choices on the worldsheet. We show that these theories arise naturally from quantization of 3d supergravity, and the amplitudes compute the dimension ($+$) or superdimension ($-$) of the space of $\mathcal{N}=1$ superconformal blocks modulo crossing symmetry. Both 0A$^+$ and 0B$^+$ are perturbatively dual to the same matrix integral as the bosonic Virasoro minimal string, while 0B$^-$ is dual to a matrix integral with an inverse square root singularity. We show that all non-trivial perturbative amplitudes of the 0A$^-$ theory vanish.

### [103] [Euclidean volume fluctuations in de Sitter quantum gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26045)
*David Blanco,Guillem Pérez-Nadal,Bruno Sivilotti*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者将配分函数对宇宙学常数的依赖关系转化为宇宙体积的概率分布，并分别在多个近似层次下进行分析：鞍点近似（saddle point）、单圈近似（one loop）、全圈近似（all-loop）以及三维情况下的非微扰（non-perturbative）方案；在二维情况下，利用刘维尔理论（Liouville theory）给出了精确结果（exact result）。

Result: 在所有近似层次下，经典极限（classical limit）中概率分布集中于经典体积附近；随着量子效应的开启，分布逐渐展宽。一个普遍趋势是：量子效应越强，概率分布越倾向于支持更小的宇宙体积。

Conclusion: 该结果表明，量子引力效应倾向于使宇宙体积变小，这一趋势在不同维度（2D 和 3D）和不同近似层次下均一致出现，暗示其可能是一个普遍性质。

Abstract: The Euclidean formulation of quantum gravity can be interpreted in terms of a probability distribution over Riemannian manifolds. In the context of de Sitter gravity, the statistics of the total volume according to this distribution is encoded in the dependence of the partition function on the cosmological constant. We use this observation to obtain a probability distribution for the volume from known results and proposals for the de Sitter partition function, in several levels of approximation: saddle point, one loop, an all-loop and a non-perturbative proposal in 3 dimensions, and an exact result in 2 dimensions, in the context of Liouville theory. In all cases we find a reasonable behavior: in the classical limit the distribution concentrates around the classical volume, and it spreads as quantum effects are turned on. We also find as a common trend that, as quantum effects are increased, the probability distribution favors increasingly smaller universes.

Abstract: N=2 supyersymmetric Yang-Mills theories are described in terms of a Hitchin system over a Riemann surface C. For $sl_2$, the quantum connection takes values in $gl_2$(A) where A is an associative algebra which we explicitly describe for the cases of Painlevé I, II and IV. Moreover, we find that the quantum connection is equivalent to irregular versions of Knizhnik-Zamolodchikov (KZ) connections. Conclusion: FDR方案在$O(N)$普适类中的成功表现表明，其先前在Ising等普适类中的优异结果并非巧合，该方案是一种兼具效率与精度的可靠计算工具。

Abstract: The novel functional dimensional regularization (FDR) scheme has proven capable of yielding results that are competitive with the state-of-the-art in the computation of critical exponents in $d=3$, while also reproducing those from the $\varepsilon$-expansion for the Ising and other universality classes. Result: 获得了Y型结的超对称四分之一指标的精确闭式解；验证了对偶构型之间四分之一指标的相等性；在特殊 fugacity 极限下，指标可解释为BCD型W-代数（W-algebras of type BCD）和李超代数$\mathfrak{osp}(1|2N)$的真空特征标（vacuum characters）。

Conclusion: 所得结果为正交群和辛群下角落构型的S-对偶性提供了有力证据，并建立了与BCD型W-代数及$\mathfrak{osp}(1|2N)$李超代数作为角落顶点算子代数（corner vertex operator algebras）的联系。

Abstract: We study supersymmetric quarter-indices for corner configurations in 4d $\mathcal{N}=4$ super Yang-Mills theory with orthogonal and symplectic gauge groups. For the basic Y-junctions, we obtain exact closed-form expressions for the indices by making use of the Gustafson type integral formula and the Higgsing method. We demonstrate the equality of the quarter-indices between dual configurations, providing evidence for S-duality of the corner configurations. In the special fugacity limit, the indices admit an interpretation in terms of the vacuum characters of the W-algebras of type BCD, and the Lie superalgebra $\mathfrak{osp}(1|2N)$ as the corner vertex operator algebras.

### [107] [On the simplicity of de Sitter correlators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26421)
*Chandramouli Chowdhury,Song He,Yong-Xiang Su,Dongyu Yang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文通过时间积分表示法研究共形耦合φ³理论中的德西特（de Sitter）时空关联函数，证明关联函数比对应的波函数系数更简单，并提出关联函数优先（correlator-first）的研究视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期证据表明等时关联函数（equal-time correlators）比对应的波函数系数（wavefunction coefficients）更简单，这激发了直接研究德西特时空关联函数的动机，旨在探索其内在的简化结构。

Method: 通过反转动量空间装饰规则（dressing rules），推导出通用费曼图（Feynman graphs）的时间积分表示；该表示以平空关联函数（flat space correlators）及其共轭动量（conjugate momenta）为基本构建块，并导出两种递归结构：叶坍塌（collapsing leaves）和低点图融合（fusing lower-point graphs）。

Result: 奇数个共轭动量插入的图为零，解释了奇点关联函数权重下降；melonic插入收缩为更低复杂度图；总能量与部分能量奇点附近的领头阶行为（leading behavior）显式可见。在树图家族（链和星图）中，关联函数的符号字母表（symbol alphabet）小于对应波函数的字母表，缺失的字母可用管道数据（tubing data）自然解释。

Conclusion: 这些结果支持关联函数优先（correlator-first）的德西特观测量研究视角：关联函数的部分简单性是其自身固有的，而非间接继承自波函数。

Abstract: Motivated by recent evidence that equal-time correlators can be simpler than the corresponding wavefunction coefficients, we study de Sitter correlators in conformally coupled $φ^3$ theory directly. By inverting the momentum-space dressing rules, we derive a time integral representation for generic graphs and show that its natural building blocks are flat space correlators of fields and conjugate momenta. Among other things, this representation gives two useful recursive structures, one obtained by collapsing leaves and one by fusing lower-point graphs. In this representation several simplifications also become immediate. Graphs with an odd number of conjugate momentum insertions vanish, explaining the weight drop of odd-point correlators, melonic insertions collapse to lower complexity graphs and the leading behavior near total and partial-energy singularities is manifest, closely paralleling the flat space story. We then take a first step beyond the integrand and study integrated answers. For tree level families, in particular chains and stars, we find that the symbol alphabet of the correlator is smaller than that of the corresponding wavefunction, with the missing letters admitting a natural interpretation in terms of tubing data. These results support a correlator-first viewpoint for de Sitter observables: part of their simplicity appears to be intrinsic to the correlator itself, rather than inherited indirectly from the wavefunction.

### [109] [Monodromy, Logarithmic Sectors, and Two-Point Functions in Critical Topologically Massive Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26493)
*Yannick Mvondo-She*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文通过解析延拓（analytic continuation）和单值性（monodromy）方法，系统研究了临界拓扑质量引力（CTMG）在手征点处的对数模式（logarithmic modes）结构。结果表明，对数模式在径向坐标复化后具有天然的多值结构，诱导出非平凡的单值性作用，从而在线性化解空间中形成不可分解的若尔当块（Jordan block）表示，为对数共形场论（logarithmic conformal field theories）提供了体对应（bulk realization）。该单值性表示足以确定两点关联函数的对数形式和混合结构，无需预设对数共形场论数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在理解临界拓扑质量引力（CTMG）在手征点处对数模式的几何与代数结构，并探索其与对数共形场论（logCFT）及单值性理论之间的内在联系。

Method: 从有质量模式与左移动引力子的退化出发，构造参数空间中的导数形式的对数模式；通过对径向坐标进行复化（complexification）揭示其多值结构，并利用单值性（monodromy）作用分析线性化解空间的表示结构。

Result: 对数模式在复径向坐标下具有天然的多值性，诱导出单值性作用，使左移动模式与对数模式形成不可分解的若尔当块（Jordan block）表示；该单值性表示为幺幂的（unipotent），且仅凭此表示即可确定两点函数的对数形式与混合结构（不含归一化）。

Conclusion: 对数模式在体几何中可解释为产生分支结构（branchlike behavior）的源，类似于生成单值性的扭曲场（twist fields）；与分支覆盖、赫维茨理论（Hurwitz theory）和可积层次之间的精确对应关系尚待建立。

Abstract: We investigate the structure of logarithmic modes in critical topologically massive gravity (CTMG) at the chiral point $μ\ell=1$ from the perspective of analytic continuation and monodromy. Starting from the degeneration of massive and left-moving graviton modes, we construct the logarithmic mode as a derivative in parameter space and show that it acquires a natural multivalued structure upon complexification of the radial coordinate.
  We demonstrate that this multivaluedness induces a nontrivial monodromy action on the space of linearized solutions, under which the left-moving and logarithmic modes form an indecomposable (Jordan block) representation. This monodromy is unipotent and provides a bulk realization of the logarithmic structure typically associated with logarithmic conformal field theories.
  We further show that the monodromy representation alone is sufficiently constraining to determine the characteristic logarithmic form and mixing structure of two-point functions, up to normalization, without assuming logarithmic conformal field theory data a priori.
  These results suggest a geometric interpretation in which logarithmic modes act as sources of branchlike behavior in the bulk, analogous to twist fields that generate monodromy. While this perspective is compatible with proposed connections to branched coverings, Hurwitz theory, and integrable hierarchies, establishing a precise correspondence is left for future work.

Method: 在平坦FLRW度规中引入分数阶波利亚科夫作用量以纳入非局域记忆效应（nonlocal memory effects），允许环半径和极角同时演化，从而得到一个由弦张力、宇宙膨胀和离心力项耦合的非自治系统（non-autonomous system）。

Result: 角动力学（angular dynamics）在环演化中起关键作用；发现了不同于标准坍缩情景的持续膨胀解，其驱动力来自动态生成的角运动；系统表现出非线性行为并伴有混沌信号，混沌动力学的 onset 与膨胀解密切相关。

Conclusion: 分数阶记忆效应和角度自由度会定性改变宇宙弦环动力学，为宇宙学背景下的环稳定性提供了新的机制。

Abstract: We study the dynamics of circular cosmic string loops in a spatially flat Friedmann Lemaître Robertson Walker universe within a fractional Polyakov framework that incorporates nonlocal memory effects. Allowing both the loop radius and polar angle to evolve, we obtain a coupled non-autonomous system governed by string tension, cosmological expansion, and an emergent centrifugal contribution. We show that angular dynamics plays a crucial role in determining the loop evolution. In contrast to standard scenarios where loops collapse, we identify a class of solutions exhibiting sustained expansion driven by dynamically generated angular motion. The system also displays nonlinear behavior with signatures of chaos, with the onset of chaotic dynamics closely correlated with expanding solutions. Our results demonstrate that fractional memory effects and angular degrees of freedom qualitatively modify cosmic string loop dynamics, providing new mechanisms for stability in cosmological backgrounds.

### [111] [On the integrability of root-Kerr probe dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26544)
*Sungsoo Kim,Sangmin Lee*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 在Kerr-Newman黑洞背景下，标量粒子的运动由于Carter荷而可积；当粒子带有自旋时，Rüdiger电荷至少在低自旋阶维持可积性。本文在简化的root-Kerr模型中探究自旋粒子可积性范围：一阶探针电荷下可积性适用于所有自旋阶；二阶探针电荷下可积性可延展至自旋平方阶，但在自旋立方阶开始失效，且无法通过进一步变形探针作用量恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究指出Kerr-Newman黑洞背景中标量粒子运动因Carter荷可积，自旋粒子则依赖Rüdiger电荷维持低阶可积性。本文旨在更简单模型——root-Kerr粒子（Kerr-Newman黑洞的无引力极限）中，系统分析自旋粒子运动可积性在自旋高阶和探针电荷高阶条件下的保持范围与破坏机制。

Method: 采用root-Kerr粒子作为源和探针的非引力模型；在探针电荷的领头阶（leading order）和二阶（second order）分别分析可积性行为；利用Newman-Janis位移（Newman-Janis shift）约束探针相互作用顶点；通过渐近守恒（asymptotic conservation）论证判断进一步形变恢复守恒的可能性。

Result: 一阶探针电荷下，若相互作用顶点受Newman-Janis位移支配，可积性适用于所有自旋阶。二阶探针电荷下，可积性可延至自旋平方阶（spin-squared order）但在自旋立方阶（spin-cubic order）开始失效。渐近守恒分析表明，无法通过进一步变形探针作用量在此阶恢复守恒。

Conclusion: 自旋粒子在root-Kerr模型中的可积性在探针电荷和自旋阶数上存在明确的适用范围边界，且在高阶存在不可恢复的破坏。该结果与引力相互作用下Kerr黑洞相关观测进行了比较。

Abstract: In the background of a Kerr-Newman black hole, the motion of a scalar particle is integrable by virtue of an extra conserved charge known as Carter charge. When the particle is endowed with spin, it is known that another conserved charge, the Rüdiger charge, maintains the integrability at least at low orders in the spin magnitude. We explore the extent of this integrability in a simpler model where both the source and the probe are root-Kerr particles, the non-gravitating limit of the Kerr-Newman black hole. At the leading order in the probe charge, the integrability holds to all orders in the spin magnitude if the interaction vertices of the probe are dictated by the Newman-Janis shift. At the second order in the probe charge, the integrability can be extended to the spin-squared order but begins to fail at the spin-cubic order. An argument based on asymptotic conservation suggests that it is impossible to restore the conservation at the spin-cubic order by a further deformation of the probe action. We compare our results with related observations for Kerr black holes with gravitational interactions.

### [112] [Entanglement Revivals and Scrambling for Evaporating Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26600)

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究二维共形场论（CFT）在蒸发黑洞背景上的纠缠扩散与纠缠记忆效应，发现黑洞加扰（scrambling）会平滑并抑制晚期互信息尖峰，直至临界尺度下完全消失，并在单区间纠缠中观察到类似的纠缠凹陷现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用自由费米子CFT中的热场双态（thermofield double state）制备，分别在Jackiw-Teitelboim（JT）引力和Russo-Susskind-Thorlacius（RST）模型两种二维引力模型中，通过参数化调控黑洞加扰时间，研究其对晚期互信息尖峰的影响。

Result: 参数化增大黑洞加扰时间会平滑并抑制纠缠尖峰，直至其在临界尺度下完全消失，实现从自由准粒子图像到最大加扰图像之间的插值。临界点处区间长度与黑洞加扰时间呈指数关系。此外，在单边蒸发RST黑洞的单区间纠缠中发现了非常类似的纠缠凹陷效应。

Abstract: We investigate the spreading of entanglement, and entanglement memory effects, in two dimensional conformal field theory (CFT) propagating on evaporating black hole backgrounds. Memory effects leading to late-time spikes in mutual information for widely separated intervals are well known in CFTs admitting a quasiparticle description. In this work we examine the effect of black hole scrambling on late time mutual information spikes for disjoint intervals in free fermion CFT prepared in a thermofield double state. Late-time entanglement revival is driven by island-induced purification of modes in the union of the intervals. We show across two distinct 2d gravity models, Jackiw-Teitelboim (JT) gravity and the Russo-Susskind-Thorlacius (RST) model, that parametrically dialing up black hole scrambling time smooths out and suppresses entanglement spikes until they disappear at a critical scale, interpolating between free quasiparticle and maximal scrambling pictures. At the critical point, the interval lengths are exponential in black hole scrambling time. We further find a very closely related effect manifest as an entanglement dip for a single interval in a single-sided evaporating RST black hole.

Conclusion: Nariai几何中的重标量场两点关联函数需要通过复测地线求和来描述，其中相位的正确处理对避免虚假奇点至关重要。

Abstract: We study two-point correlation functions of heavy scalar fields in the Nariai geometry. Utilizing the heat kernel formalism, we obtain this result from a geodesic approximation to the two-point function on a product of spheres. By analytically continuing one of the spheres, we obtain the correlation function in the Nariai geometry. This result involves a sum over complex geodesics, extending previous results in pure de Sitter space. We emphasize the important role of the phase of each geodesic contribution, which needs to be taken into account to avoid spurious singularities in the correlator.

### [116] [A positive definite formulation of vacuum decay with reduced symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26795)
*José R. Espinosa,Ryusuke Jinno,Thomas Konstandin,Shogo Matake,Taiga Miyachi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文针对真空衰变（vacuum decay）中杂质（impurities）破坏O(4)对称性并催化衰变的问题，提出了一种明确正定的隧穿衰变作用量（tunneling decay action）计算方法，适用于杂质效应呈球对称从而将反弹对称性（bounce symmetry）降至O(3)的情形。该作用量可视为隐式假设O(4)对称性的隧穿势方法（tunneling potential method）的推广，并在O(4)对称情形下约化为原方法，同时给出了O(3)对称及任意壁厚（arbitrary wall thickness）的解析示例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真空衰变中的欧几里得反弹（Euclidean bounce）原本具有O(4)对称性，但杂质的存在会破坏该对称性并催化衰变，现有方法（如隧穿势方法）隐含了O(4)对称性假设，无法直接处理这些不对称场景。因此需要一种新的、明确正定的作用量计算公式，以处理对称性降低至O(3)的球对称杂质情形。

Method: 提出一种明确正定的隧穿衰变作用量构建方法，适用于杂质效应呈球对称、反弹对称性降至O(3)的情形；该作用量可视为隧穿势方法（tunneling potential method）的推广，并在O(4)对称情形下约化为后者；通过解析示例展示了O(3)对称及任意壁厚条件下的具体应用。

Result: 得到了一个明确正定的隧穿衰变作用量，在O(4)对称情形下可约化为隧穿势方法的结果；同时提供了具有O(3)对称性和任意壁厚的解析示例，验证了该公式的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文推广了隧穿势方法，使其能够处理对称性降低至O(3)的杂质催化真空衰变问题，为更一般情形下的衰变率计算提供了新工具。

Abstract: The Euclidean bounce for vacuum decay enjoys an $O(4)$ symmetry that is lost in the presence of impurities than can catalyze the decay. We present a formulation for the calculation of the tunneling decay action, that is explicitly positive definite, for impurities whose effects are spherically symmetric so that the bounce symmetry is reduced to $O(3)$. The action constructed can be regarded as a generalization of the tunneling potential method, which implicitly assumed $O(4)$ symmetry. We show that the action obtained reduces to the tunneling potential for $O(4)$-symmetric cases and provide analytic examples with $O(3)$ symmetry and arbitrary wall thickness.

### [117] [Deforming ${\rm AdS}_3\times S^3\times T^4$ in Type IIB Supergravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26854)

TL;DR: 本文讨论了IIB型超引力（Type IIB supergravity）中一类新的超对称（supersymmetric）解，即翘曲反德西特时空与翘曲三维球面加四维环面（WAdS₃ × WS³ × T⁴）的背景。这类解的核心特征是尽管保持超对称，两个几何因子的翘曲（warping）却由独立参数描述。部分解的光类翘曲（lightlike warping）反德西特因子源自渐近局部平直的D膜（D-brane）与通量（flux）正则构型在近视界极限下的结果，其构造依赖于两次独立的TsT变换。论文还给出了一类未发表过的新超对称解，其反德西特因子的翘曲包含光类、类空（spacelike）和类时（timelike）类型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索IIB型超引力中具有独立翘曲参数的超对称WAdS₃ × WS³ × T⁴背景，并揭示其与D膜和通量构型在近视界极限下的联系，以拓展超引力解的分类与弦理论（string theory）对偶构造。

Method: 采用两次独立的TsT变换来构造渐近局部平直的D膜与通量构型，从而在近视界极限下得到具有光类翘曲反德西特因子的超对称解；同时通过类似手法得到包含光类、类空和类时翘曲的新解类。

Result: 得到了具有独立翘曲参数的超对称WAdS₃ × WS³ × T⁴解，部分解可嵌入D膜和通量的渐近局部平直正则构型中。还获得了一类全新的超对称解，其反德西特因子的翘曲类型涵盖光类、类空和类时三种。

Conclusion: IIB型超引力中存在一类由独立参数描述翘曲的超对称WAdS₃ × WS³ × T⁴背景，其构造可由两次TsT变换和D膜构型实现，这些结果丰富了弦理论中翘曲时空超对称解的分类与构造方法。

Abstract: We discuss some new results on the construction of supersymmetric solutions of Type IIB supergravity of the form ${\rm WAdS}_3\times{\rm WS}^3\times T^4$, ${\rm WAdS}_3$ and ${\rm WS}^3$ denoting \emph{warped} anti-de Sitter spacetime and sphere, respectively. The distinctive feature of these backgrounds is that, in spite of them being supersymmetric, the warpings of the two factors are described by independent parameters. We illustrate how some of these geometries, characterised by a lightlike warping of the anti-de Sitter factor, arise in the near-horizon limit of a regular, asymptotically locally flat configuration of D-branes and fluxes. Central to the construction of the latter solutions is the use of two independent TsT transformations. We also give a new class of supersymmetric solutions of the general form ${\rm WAdS}_3\times{\rm WS}^3\times T^4$, which has not been published yet. They feature warpings of the anti-de Sitter factor of the lightlike, spacelike and timelike types. We discuss their properties.

### [118] [Schwinger-Keldysh Path Integral for Gauge theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26941)
*Greg Kaplanek,Maria Mylova,Andrew J. Tolley*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文为开放非阿贝尔规范理论建立了Schwinger-Keldysh路径积分形式，涵盖BRST规范固定、不定Hilbert空间处理、边界项以及开有效场论的BRST对称性结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非平衡过程中开放非阿贝尔规范理论缺乏完整且自洽的路径积分形式体系，尤其是在BRST（Becchi-Rouet-Stora-Tyutin）规范固定、不定Hilbert空间（indefinite Hilbert space）以及初始/终态边界条件的处理上存在困难。

Method: 采用Schwinger-Keldysh路径积分形式，结合BRST协变规范固定方法，引入Nakanishi-Lautrup场表示来处理初终条件，并构建了具有对角BRST对称性的路径积分；同时通过收缩原BRST对称性得到Keldysh BRST对称性。

Result: 得到了对角（延迟）BRST对称性下的Ward-Takahashi-Slavnov-Taylor恒等式；证明了超前BRST对称性因in-in边界条件而显式破缺；证明了Feynman-Vernon影响泛函在微扰论下保持BRST不变；并给出了在Higgs相中自发对称破缺时开有效场论的一般形式。

Conclusion: 所建立的形式为开放非阿贝尔规范理论在非平衡过程中的应用提供了自洽的路径积分框架，其对称性结构为开有效场论（Open EFT）的领头项行为提供了理论约束，Gribov歧义（Gribov ambiguity）被预期在非微扰层面会破坏或修改BRST对称性。

Abstract: We develop the Schwinger-Keldysh path-integral formalism for open non-Abelian gauge theories that are gauge-fixed via the BRST method in covariant gauges. We focus on generic initial states, pure and mixed, specified at finite times suitable for non-equilibrium processes. We pay particular attention to the handling of the indefinite Hilbert space, the construction of BRST-invariant Schrodinger picture wavefunctionals, density matrices and inner product, the implementation of the Hata-Kugo prescription, and the role of boundary terms at both the initial and final times. We highlight the advantages of the Nakanishi-Lautrup field representation in dealing with initial/final conditions. The resulting Schwinger-Keldysh path integral is manifestly invariant under a diagonal (retarded) BRST symmetry for arbitrary physical initial states, whether pure or mixed. From this, we obtain the corresponding Ward-Takahashi-Slavnov-Taylor identities, valid perturbatively. Non-perturbatively the Gribov ambiguity is expected to break or modify the BRST symmetry. The naive advanced BRST symmetry is shown to be explicitly violated by the in-in boundary conditions. We show that the Feynman-Vernon influence functional derived by integrating out charged matter and/or hard gluon modes remains (perturbatively) BRST invariant. When the Open EFT action is expanded to second order in advanced fields it exhibits an exact symmetry under a contraction of the original BRST symmetry. This Keldysh BRST symmetry is equivalent to the BRST associated with the retarded gauge transformations together with a linearly realized BRST transformation of the advanced fields. These govern the structure of the leading terms in an Open EFT. We illustrate this with the explicit example of Hard Thermal Loop Effective Theory, and construct the general form of the Open EFT in a Higgs phase when all gauge symmetries are spontaneously broken.

### [119] [Anomalous Transport and Explicit Symmetry Breaking in Holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26949)
*Ashis Tamang,Nishal Rai,Karl Landsteiner,Eugenio Megias*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本论文通过全息 Einstein-Maxwell 模型（带纯规范与混合规范-引力 Chern-Simons 项），在完整背景反作用下计算了显式对称性破缺情况下的反常输运系数，发现反常诱导的输运现象可延伸至非反常扇区，且输运系数依赖于对称性破缺质量参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在显式对称性破缺（explicit symmetry breaking）存在时，量子反常（quantum anomalies）如何影响反常输运（anomalous transport）现象，特别是反常效应是否会扩展到非反常扇区。

Method: 采用五维全息 Einstein-Maxwell 模型，引入纯规范（pure gauge）与混合规范-引力（mixed gauge-gravitational）Chern-Simons 项，包含标量场和规范场对度量的完整背景反作用（full backreaction），并利用 Kubo 公式（Kubo formulae）通过电荷流与能量流关联函数计算反常输运系数。

Result: 在显式对称性破缺存在时，反常诱导的输运现象不仅出现在反常扇区，还会影响非反常扇区。输运系数明显依赖于对称性破缺质量参数（symmetry-breaking mass parameter）。

Conclusion: 量子反常与显式对称性破缺在全息系统中存在相互耦合作用，这种耦合效应使得反常输运的影响范围超出传统预期。该结果为理解强耦合体系中反常输运与对称性破缺的关联提供了全息视角。

Abstract: We consider a holographic Einstein-Maxwell model in five dimensions with pure gauge and mixed gauge-gravitational Chern-Simons terms to study anomaly-induced transport in the presence of explicit symmetry breaking. We include the full backreaction of the scalar field and gauge fields on the metric and compute the anomalous transport coefficients using Kubo formulae involving charge and energy current correlators. Our findings reveal that, in the presence of explicit symmetry breaking, anomaly-induced transport phenomena can extend beyond anomalous currents and affect the non-anomalous sector as well. The transport coefficients exhibit a clear dependence on the symmetry-breaking mass parameter, highlighting the interplay between quantum anomalies and explicit symmetry breaking in holographic systems.

</details>

### [120] [Thermo-optic dynamics of effective epsilon-near-zero media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25656)
*Jiaye Wu,Xuanyi Liu,Marco Clementi,Shuang Qiu,Limin Lin,Zhang-Kai Zhou,Camille-Sophie Brès*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出将热光效应重新定义为有效介质的静态与动态重构（reconfiguration of effective media），并以此统一描述epsilon-near-zero（ENZ）体系中的稳态与瞬态热光现象，实验展示了在可见光波段CMOS兼容有效介质中异常大的热-光谱调制率与皮秒级热光非线性响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来研究发现，在ENZ条件下传统上被认为缓慢且次要的热光效应（thermo-optic effect）可以被强烈修饰，但缺乏统一的理论框架来同时描述其静态与瞬态行为。

Method: 建立了热光重构有效介质的统一物理框架；使用工作在可见光波段的CMOS兼容有效介质（effective medium），在热平衡与瞬态激发两种条件下进行实验，测量温度和超快激发对ENZ条件构成参数（constitutive parameters）的重新配置效应。

Result: 热平衡下观察到异常大的静态ENZ波长漂移，热-光谱调制率前所未有，有效热光系数（effective thermo-optic coefficient）量级为10^{-1} K^{-1}；超快激发下观察到皮秒（picosecond）量级热光非线性响应，对应光学参数的瞬态演化。

Conclusion: 热光效应可统一理解为有效介质的静态与动态重构过程，该视角弥合了热光物理、有效介质理论（effective-medium theory）与时变光子学（time-varying photonics）之间的概念鸿沟。

Abstract: Epsilon-near-zero (ENZ) photonic media exhibit extreme optical dispersion that enables unconventional light-matter interactions and enhanced optical nonlinearities. Recent studies suggested that thermo-optic effects, traditionally regarded as slow and secondary, can be strongly modified under the ENZ condition. Here we establish thermo-optic reconfiguration of effective media as a unified physical framework to describe both static and transient thermo-optic phenomena in ENZ systems. Using a CMOS-compatible effective medium operating in the visible spectral range, we experimentally demonstrate that temperature variation, whether under thermal equilibrium or transient excitation, reconfigures the constitutive parameters defining the ENZ condition, giving rise to pronounced linear and nonlinear optical responses. At thermal equilibrium, this reconfiguration manifests itself as static ENZ wavelength shift with an unprecedentedly large thermal-spectral modulation rate and an effective thermo-optic coefficient on the order of $10^{-1}$ K$^{-1}$. Under ultrafast excitation, we observe a picosecond-scale thermo-optic nonlinear response induced by transient heating. This response can be consistently interpreted as a time-dependent reconfiguration of the effective ENZ medium, corresponding to a transient evolution of its optical parameters. By reframing thermo-optic effects as a process of static and dynamic reconfiguration of effective media, this work provides a unified perspective that bridges thermo-optic physics, effective-medium theory, and time-varying photonics.

</details>

### [121] [EFT Pathways to $|ΔB| =2$: Chiral Constructions and Phenomenology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25989)
*Arnau Bas i Beneito,Ajdin Palavrić,Andrea Sainaghi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个系统的有效场论（effective field theory）框架，用于研究从紫外到低能标度下的 $|\Delta B|=2$ 相互作用。通过手征对称性（chiral symmetry）构建了完整且非冗余的低能算符集，并建立了与标准模型有效场论（Standard Model effective field theory, SMEFT）及重子手征微扰论（baryon chiral perturbation theory）的对应关系。将该框架应用于重子-反重子振荡（baryon-antibaryon oscillations）和双核子衰变（dinucleon decay）现象学，揭示了不同探针的互补性，并识别了此前未被探索的双核子衰变道。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重子数破坏（baryon number violation）是超出标准模型（Beyond Standard Model）的重要信号，但 $\Delta B=\pm 2$ 过程缺乏系统的理论框架来连接从紫外（ultraviolet）新物理到低能强子观测量的计算。现有研究对这类相互作用的算符结构和不同实验探针之间的互补性认识不完整。

Method: 基于有效场论（effective field theory）方法，利用手征对称性（chiral symmetry）构建低能标度下 $|\Delta B|=2$ 相互作用的完整、非冗余算符集。建立该算符集与标准模型有效场论（SMEFT）和高能标算符的匹配关系，并在重子手征微扰论（baryon $\chi$PT）框架下实现低能实现。

Result: 重子-反重子振荡（baryon-antibaryon oscillations）仅对有限的算符结构敏感；而双核子衰变（dinucleon decay）对更广泛的算符类敏感，包括振荡无法触及的跃迁。本文还识别了此前未被探索的双核子衰变道，可探测这些未受约束的参数空间区域。

Conclusion: 该形式化框架明确了不同实验探针之间的互补性，提供了一条从紫外（ultraviolet）起源到低能强子观测量的一致追踪路径，为系统研究产生 $|\Delta B|=2$ 相互作用的紫外模型奠定了基础。

Abstract: We develop a systematic effective field theory framework for studying $|ΔB|=2$ interactions across energy scales. Using chiral symmetry, we construct the complete and non-redundant set of operators governing these interactions at low energies and establish their connection to the corresponding operators in the Standard Model effective field theory, as well as to their realizations in baryon chiral perturbation theory. The framework is then applied to the phenomenology of baryon-antibaryon oscillations and dinucleon decay. While oscillations probe only a limited subset of operator structures, dinucleon decay is sensitive to a significantly broader class, including transitions that are otherwise inaccessible. In addition, we identify previously unexplored dinucleon decay channels, which can probe these unconstrained regions of parameter space. More generally, this formalism makes explicit the complementarity of different probes and provides a consistent way to trace baryon-number-violating effects from their ultraviolet origin to low-energy hadronic observables, thereby providing a basis for systematic studies of ultraviolet models generating such interactions.

</details>


### [122] [Revisiting Turner Window Axions: The Untapped Potential of NaI Dark Matter Detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26004)
*W. C. Haxton,Xing Liu,Anupam Ray,Evan Rule*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了“特纳窗口”（Turner window）中轴子（axion）的可行性，发现通过更完整的SN1987A轴子不透明度（opacity）处理后，原先被认为基本关闭的窗口对强子耦合轴子重新开放。并提出利用银河系碳燃烧恒星中²³Na的热泵（thermal pump）机制产生440 keV单能轴子，通过现有NaI探测器阵列（如DAMA/LIBRA）的共振吸收（resonant absorption）进行探测，可在两年数据内覆盖|g_app|~10^(-6.5)–10^(-2)的耦合范围，包括质量m_a≳10 eV的QCD轴子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 特纳窗口（Turner window）对应质量≳1 eV且与物质耦合足够强的轴子，该窗口因SN1987A冷却下限、神冈II探测器未观测到光子以及萨德伯里中微子观测站（Sudbury Neutrino Observatory）对太阳轴子产生中子的限制而被认为基本关闭。本文旨在重新评估该窗口的可行性，并寻找新的探测方法。

Method: 对SN1987A中轴子不透明度（axion opacity）进行更完整的处理，显著弱化了神冈II探测器的限制。提出利用银河系碳燃烧恒星（ONeMg白矮星前身及电子俘获超新星和核坍缩超新星的前身）中合成的大量²³Na在~10⁹K温度下作为热泵（thermal pump），将恒星能量转化为440 keV的轴子线。该轴子可通过NaI探测器的共振吸收（resonant absorption）探测，NaI同时作为靶和探测器。

Result: 对于具有强子耦合（hadronic couplings）的轴子或轴子类似粒子（axion-like particles），特纳窗口内的大片区域重新变得可行。利用现有NaI探测器阵列（DAMA/LIBRA等合作组已部署）的两年数据，可覆盖耦合范围|g_app|~10^(-6.5)–10^(-2)，包括质量m_a≳10 eV的QCD轴子。

Conclusion: 通过改进SN1987A轴子不透明度处理，特纳窗口对强子耦合轴子重新开放。银河系碳燃烧恒星产生的440 keV轴子可通过现有NaI探测器以共振吸收方式有效探测，为轴子搜索开辟了新的途径。

Abstract: The "Turner window" corresponds to axions with masses $\gtrsim$ 1 eV that have sufficiently strong couplings to matter to evade limits from the cooling of SN1987A. This window, through which the trajectories for the KSVZ and DFSZ QCD axions run, has been thought to be largely closed because of (1) the floor established by SN1987A cooling, (2) the absence of SN1987A-associated photons in the Kamioka II detector, and (3) the limit on neutrons produced by solar axions in the Sudbury Neutrino Observatory. We show that a more complete treatment of the axion opacity in SN1987A, significantly weakens (2). Consequently, for axion or axion-like particles with hadronic couplings, $g_{ann}$ and $g_{app}$, significant regions within the Turner window now become viable. We describe a new opportunity to constrain such hadronically coupled axions via their resonant absorption in NaI detectors. The source is the Milky Way's carbon-burning stars -- the progenitors of ONeMg white dwarfs as well as electron-capture and core-collapse supernovae -- which synthesize significant quantities of $^{23}$Na, keeping it at temperatures $\sim 10^9$K for periods up to tens of thousands of years. $^{23}$Na acts as a thermal pump to convert stellar energy into axions, which arrive at the Earth as a thermally broadened line at 440 keV. These axions can be detected via resonant absorption in NaI, with the needed detector arrays already in place, developed by DAMA/LIBRA and other collaborations to search for the elastic scattering of light WIMPs. In axion detection, NaI serves as both the target, producing $γ$'s following resonant absorption, and the detector for those $γ$'s. With current array masses and backgrounds, we find that the coupling range $|g_{app}| \sim 10^{-6.5}$--$10^{-2}$ can be covered after two years of data, including QCD axions with $m_a \gtrsim 10$ eV.

</details>


### [123] [Semileptonic $B_q$ decays to heavy tensor mesons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26406)
*Pietro Colangelo,Fulvia De Fazio,Carlo la Torre,Giuseppe Roselli*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用光锥QCD求和规则（light-cone QCD sum rules）系统研究了$B_q$介子（$q=u,d,s$）到$J^P=2^+$粲张量介子的半轻子衰变过程，计算了标准模型及其扩展中的形状因子，并给出了衰变率及轻子味普适性检验比率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究$B_q$介子到$J^P=2^+$粲介子的半轻子衰变，填补对$B$介子衰变到激发态张量介子（tensor meson）过程的形状因子和衰变率的理论计算空白。

Method: 采用光锥QCD求和规则（light-cone QCD sum rules），以外态$B_q$介子为背景，包含3粒子贡献（3-particle contributions），计算弱矢量流和轴矢流（weak vector and axial-vector quark currents）的强子矩阵元形状因子（form factors），并进一步确定标准模型扩展中赝标量和张量流（pseudoscalar and tensor quark currents）的形状因子。

Result: 检验了重夸克极限（heavy quark limit）下的预期关系，定量确定了各种形状因子因有限重夸克质量修正（finite heavy quark mass corrections）的大小；给出了标准模型中$B_q$到重张量介子的半轻子衰变率，以及用于检验轻子味普适性（Lepton Flavour Universality）的比率。

Conclusion: 所计算的形状因子和衰变率为理解$B$介子到激发态张量介子的半轻子衰变提供了重要理论参考，支持轻子味普适性的进一步检验。

Abstract: The semileptonic decays of $B_q$ mesons ($q=u,d,s$) to $J^P=2^+$ charmed mesons are investigated. The form factors parametrising the hadronic matrix elements of the weak vector and axial-vector quark currents are evaluated using light-cone QCD sum rules with external $B_q$ state, including the 3-particle contributions. The form factors of pseudoscalar and tensor quark currents occurring in extensions of the Standard Model are also determined. The relations expected in the heavy quark limit are tested and the size of finite heavy quark mass corrections are determined for the various form factors. Results are presented for the semileptonic $B_q$ to heavy tensor meson decay rates in the Standard Model, and for the ratios testing Lepton Flavour Universality.

</details>


### [124] [Gravitational Properties of the Monopole Bag](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26191)
*Yu Komiya,Fumihiro Takayama*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究轴子宇宙学中由单极子和轴子畴壁构成的混合缺陷（混合缺陷）的引力性质，发现引力坍缩后既可形成无视界残骸，也可形成一种规避奇点、保留非平凡轴子分布并具有奇特电磁性质的dyonic规则黑洞（dyonic regular black hole）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在轴子宇宙学（axionic cosmologies）中，早期宇宙存在丰富的对称性破缺现象；当宇宙中存在单极子（monopole）时，轴子场构型可能发生形变，形成由中心单极子与闭合轴子畴壁（axion domain wall）构成的“单极子袋（monopole bag）”态。该工作旨在研究这一混合缺陷（hybrid defect）的引力性质及其可能的引力坍缩终态。

Method: 考虑含单极子背景下轴子轮廓（axion profile）的形变，构建由中心单极子和闭合轴子畴壁组成的“单极子袋”混合缺陷。在此基础上，分析该系统的引力行为。

Result: 对于不同的输入参数，单极子-畴壁系统在引力坍缩后会产生两种类型的终态：一类是无视界（horizon-less）的残骸，另一类是类似黑洞（black hole-like）的终态。后者被证明是一种dyonic规则黑洞，能够规避常规的奇点引力坍缩（singular gravitational collapse），并通过轴子Chern-Simons项（axionic Chern-Simons term）的奇特电磁性质维持非平凡的轴子分布（non-trivial axionic profile）。

Conclusion: 单极子-畴壁混合缺陷的引力坍缩可以产生一种新型dyonic规则黑洞，它不出现奇点并保留轴子场结构，为研究轴子宇宙学中的缺陷结构及其引力物理提供了新的可能性。

Abstract: Axionic cosmologies constitute a class of models with phenomenologically rich symmetry breaking in the early universe. In the case where monopoles are present in such a background, the axion profile may be deformed; it is possible to construct a ``monopole bag" state composed of a central monopole within a closed axion domain wall. We consider the gravitational properties of this hybrid defect, and find a both horizon-less and a black hole-like final state can result as remnants of the monopole-domain wall system after gravitational collapse for different input parameters. We demonstrate that the latter classifies as dyonic regular black hole, evading the usual singular gravitational collapse and retaining a non-trivial axionic profile through exotic electromagnetic properties of an axionic Chern-Simons term.

</details>


### [125] [Dissipative Losses In Black Hole-Induced Vacuum Decay](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26009)
*Michael Geller,Ofri Telem*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本研究在薄壁（thin-wall）近似下，通过考虑辐射损失（radiative losses）机制，解决了黑洞催化的假真空衰变（false vacuum decay）问题，表明此类衰变过程始终存在指数抑制，尽管在某些参数空间中衰变率相对于真空隧穿（vacuum tunneling）有所增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期以来，黑洞催化假真空衰变是否是导致早期宇宙真空不稳定的机制一直存在争议——小质量黑洞的高霍金温度（Hawking temperature）似乎能产生高度增能的真真空泡（true vacuum bubbles）并触发无指数抑制的真空衰变，这一矛盾亟需理论澄清。

Method: 采用φ⁴和sine-Gordon模型，在薄壁（thin-wall） regime下进行分析，重点引入辐射损失（radiative losses）机制来研究真真空泡在宇宙演化中的减速行为。

Result: 辐射损失在阻止真真空泡加速和避免失控的真空衰变中起关键作用；尽管在参数空间的某些区域，黑洞催化的衰变率相比真空隧穿（vacuum tunneling）有所增强，但该过程始终受到指数抑制。

Conclusion: 黑洞催化不会导致假真空无指数抑制地衰变，辐射损失是确保真空泡减速并维持衰变过程指数抑制的核心物理机制。

Abstract: We address the long-standing puzzle of false vacuum decay catalyzed by black holes. Naively, small black holes with large Hawking temperatures can generate highly-boosted true vacuum bubbles in the early universe and trigger vacuum decay without any exponential suppression. Working in the thin-wall regime of the $φ^4$ and sine-Gordon models, we show that radiative losses play a crucial role in decelerating these bubbles and preventing runaway vacuum decay. We find that while the production rate is enhanced compared with vacuum tunneling in some parts of the parameter space, it is always exponentially suppressed.

</details>
