### [126] [Kinetics of segregation of topologically-modified ring polymers in cylindrical confinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26087)
*Harsh Doshi,Shreerang Pande,Sathish K. Sukumaran,Apratim Chatterji*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过朗之万动力学模拟（Langevin dynamics simulations），系统探究了拓扑修饰（在环形DNA上引入内部环）对圆柱约束下大肠杆菌（E. coli）子代环形聚合物分离速率的影响。结果表明，增加环的数量会缩短分离时间，其机制在于增强了链间的熵排斥（entropic repulsion）；环的轮廓长度及初始构型中各向异性链的相互取向也对分离时间有调节作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大肠杆菌中，圆柱约束下两个子代DNA环形聚合物之间的熵排斥被认为是调控染色体分离的重要因素，且这种排斥可通过拓扑修饰（引入内部环）进一步增强。然而，拓扑修饰对环形聚合物分离速率的具体影响尚不明确。

Method: 通过交联单体（crosslinking monomers）的方式，在选定位点沿环形DNA轮廓系统性地改变引入环的数量和轮廓长度；交联方案受启发于大肠杆菌染色体中挤出环（extruded loops）主要位于复制起点附近（ori-proximal region）的观察结果。随后对经过拓扑修饰的珠-弹簧聚合物（bead-spring polymers）进行朗之万动力学模拟，计算其在圆柱约束下的分离时间。

Result: 在一定条件下，增加环的数量导致分离时间缩短。环的轮廓长度以及初始构型中各向异性链的相互取向同样对分离时间有影响。

Conclusion: 拓扑修饰通过增强环形聚合物间的熵排斥来促进染色体分离；环的数量、轮廓长度及初始取向共同决定了分离时间。

Abstract: In Escherichia coli (E. coli), entropic repulsion between the two daughter DNA ring polymers under cylindrical confinement is believed to be an important factor governing chromosomal segregation. The repulsion can be enhanced by topological modifications, i.e., by the introduction of internal loops at certain locations along the contour of the circular DNA. However, the effect of topological modifications on the rate of segregation of ring polymers remains unclear. Therefore, we systematically varied the number and the contour length of loops introduced at selected locations by crosslinking monomers. The appropriate crosslinking was motivated by observations that extruded loops are located mainly near the origin of replication (ori-proximal) region of the E. coli chromosome. This resulted in the chains becoming intrinsically anisotropic. Using Langevin dynamics simulations of these topologically modified bead-spring polymers, we calculated the time required for segregation under cylinder confinement. With certain caveats, we found that increasing the number of loops resulted in a decrease in the time of segregation. In line with past work, we propose that this is due to the increase in the entropic repulsion between the polymers upon increasing the number of loops. In addition to the number of loops, the contour length of the loops and the mutual orientation of the (anisotropic) chains in the initial configurations played a role in determining the time of segregation.

</details>


### [127] [Viscous Settling of Bravais Unit-Cells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26189)
*Sebastian Bürger,Harshit Joshi,S Ganga Prasath,Rahul Chajwa,Rama Govindarajan*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过实验、理论和数值模拟研究了布拉维晶格（Bravais lattice）多孔结构在斯托克斯（Stokes）沉降中的速度与孔隙率关系，发现沉降速度U与固体分数φ满足幂律关系U ∝ φ^γ，其中实验指数γ=0.43，经容器壁效应校正后无界域指数γ=0.30。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解多孔物体在粘性流体中的沉降行为，为预测云层和海洋中复杂颗粒的沉积通量提供理论基础。

Method: 采用实验测量、解析分析、斯托克斯边界积分模拟（Stokesian boundary integral simulations）以及Faxén边界修正（Faxen's boundary correction）相结合的方法，系统研究多孔布拉维晶格单胞的沉降动力学。

Result: 实验发现沉降速度与固体分数满足幂律关系，指数γ=0.43且与形状无关；容器壁效应显著影响沉降行为；经壁效应校正后，无界域（unbounded domain）中的幂律指数降为γ=0.30。

Conclusion: 多孔物体沉降速度与孔隙率之间存在普适的幂律标度关系，但该标度性是否适用于自然界中不规则且生物结构复杂的聚集体仍有待进一步研究。

Abstract: We study experimentally and theoretically the Stokesian settling of a well-known class of porous shapes: Bravais lattice unit-cells, whose porosity we vary controllably by changing their lattice spacing. In our experiments, conducted in a square cuboidal container with its long-axis aligned along gravity, we find that the settling speed U and the solid fraction φ of these lattice units obey a power-law relationship U $\propto$ φ^γ , with an exponent γ = 0.43 independent of their shape. To understand the observed scaling exponent, we analytically and numerically investigate the settling of the simple cubic structure under different approximations. We find that the walls of the container, though far from the sinking object, have a defining effect. Our Stokesian boundary integral simulations show that the Faxen's boundary correction captures the wall-effects accurately and enables us to discount the wall-effect from the experimental data, yielding a power-law exponent γ = 0.30 for settling in an unbounded domain. The power-law relating sinking speed and porosity is a step towards predictively understanding the sedimentation fluxes of complex objects in the clouds and the oceans. However, the applicability of this universal scaling to irregular and biologically richer aggregates found in nature remains an open direction.

### [128] [A Thermodynamic Analysis of Enhanced Metastability in Isochoric Supercooled Liquids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26302)
*Boris Rubinsky*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文结合亥姆霍兹平衡热力学（Helmholtz equilibrium thermodynamics）与一阶微扰方法（first-order perturbation methodology），推导出一个关于等容条件下成核稳定性（nucleation stability）的不等式。该不等式从热力学上证明，对于固相密度低于液相的物质，等容系统中的凝固驱动力小于等压系统中的吉布斯驱动力，从而解释了等容条件下成核速率受到抑制的实验现象，并提出了一个可仅由体热力学数据计算的等容稳定性数（dimensionless isochoric stability number）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验观察到等容（isochoric，恒体积）条件相比等压（isobaric，恒压力）条件能增强过冷（supercooling）稳定性。本文旨在从热力学角度为这一现象提供普遍的理论证明，推导出等容条件下成核抑制作用的热力学基础。

Method: 将亥姆霍兹平衡热力学与一阶微扰方法相结合，推导出等容约束下的成核稳定性不等式。通过比较等容系统中凝固的亥姆霍兹驱动力（Helmholtz driving force）与等压系统中凝固的吉布斯驱动力（Gibbs driving force），建立热力学证明框架。

Result: 对于任何固相密度小于液相的相变物质，等容系统中的亥姆霍兹驱动力小于等压系统中的吉布斯驱动力。由于成核速率（nucleation rate）与驱动力的平方倒数呈指数依赖关系，驱动力的降低意味着核化受到抑制。此外，得到一个可仅由体热力学数据计算的等容稳定性数，该数为与几何结构无关的判据。

Conclusion: 该工作为等容条件下成核速率的抑制提供了热力学依据：驱动力减小削弱了预临界涨落（pre-critical fluctuation）的生长偏向，增加了其热溶解（thermal dissolution）的概率。提出的等容稳定性数可用于跨材料、跨条件比较过冷液体的稳定性。

Abstract: Experiments show that isochoric (constant-volume) conditions enhance supercooling stability relative to isobaric (constant-pressure) conditions. Here, combining Helmholtz equilibrium thermodynamics with a first-order perturbation methodology, we derive an inequality governing nucleation stability under volumetric constraint. The derivation provides a general thermodynamic proof that for any substance undergoing phase transformation in which the solid is less dense than the liquid, the Helmholtz driving force for solidification in isochoric systems is smaller than the Gibbs driving force in isobaric systems. Since nucleation rates depend exponentially on the inverse square of the driving force, this provides a thermodynamic basis for the observed suppression of nucleation rates. While a full stochastic treatment is beyond the scope of this work, the reduction in driving force implies a weakening of the bias toward growth of pre-critical fluctuations, increasing their probability of thermal dissolution. The analysis yields a dimensionless isochoric stability number. This number is computable from bulk thermodynamic data alone and provides a geometry-independent criterion for comparing metastable liquid stability across materials and conditions.

</details>


### [129] [Coexistence of patterned phases in chemically active multicomponent mixtures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26346)
*Chengjie Luo,Yicheng Qiang,Guido L. A. Kusters,David Zwicker*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本论文针对化学活性混合物（chemically active mixtures）中物理相互作用与化学反应耦合所导致的复杂图案（complex patterns），通过构造一类化学反应的Lyapunov泛函（Lyapunov functional），提出了广义吉布斯相律（generalized Gibbs phase rule），揭示了共存图案的数量规律，并展示了通过独立相（independent phases）的模块化组合可以构建复杂图案。该理论为分析更复杂的活性混合物系统提供了统一框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物理相互作用可导致相分离（phase separation），化学反应可形成反应-扩散图案（reaction-diffusion patterns），但二者耦合在化学活性混合物中产生的复杂图案尚未被充分理解。现有研究对单个过程已有较深入认识，但对两者组合的机制缺乏统一理论框架。

Method: 作者针对一类化学反应识别出了Lyapunov泛函（Lyapunov functional），通过最小化该泛函，推导出广义吉布斯相律（generalized Gibbs phase rule），该相律决定了共存图案（coexisting patterns）的数目，并表明复杂图案可以通过独立相（independent phases）的模块化组合来生成。

Result: 理论揭示了化学活性混合物中存在的复杂稳态图案（stationary patterns），并得出了一个控制共存图案数量的广义吉布斯相律。同时验证了通过独立相的模块化组合可以构造复杂图案。

Conclusion: 该工作为理解和分析化学活性混合物中的复杂图案提供了理论框架，并具有扩展至更复杂系统的潜力。

Abstract: Chemically active mixtures exhibit complex patterns that emerge from the interplay of physical interactions and reactions among components. Individually, these two processes are well-understood: Physical interactions can give rise to phase separation, whereas reactions can form reaction-diffusion patterns. To understand the combination of both processes, we identify a Lyapunov functional for a class of chemical reactions. By minimizing this functional, we identify a generalized Gibbs phase rule that governs the number of coexisting patterns, and we demonstrate that complex patterns can be created by the modular combination of independent phases. Our theory unveils complex stationary patterns in chemically active mixtures and provides a framework for analyzing more complex systems.

</details>


### [130] [A Category-Theoretic Framework from Biological Mechanics to Engineered Stimulus-Response Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26367)
*Lee Marom,Skylar Tibbits,Gioele Zardini,Markus J. Buehler*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于范畴论（category theory）的组成性框架，用于将生物设计逻辑形式化地转化为工程系统，并通过松果层级结构的水敏变形行为实例验证了该框架在生成、制造与实验验证中的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 天然材料通过层级组织和跨尺度耦合机制实现自适应行为，但将其转化为工程设计的方法目前仍高度依赖启发式经验，缺乏一个能在保持跨抽象层次物理一致性的同时、将生物设计逻辑系统性地转化为工程实现的形式化框架。

Method: 定义了一个刺激响应动力系统（stimulus response dynamical systems）的范畴，包含自然子范畴与人工子范畴；引入了一个保持结构的实现函子（implementation functor），将生物力学映射到工程系统；形式化了一个与机器无关的规约层（specification layer），将行为意图链接到可执行的制造程序。该框架在Grasshopper中实现，通过模块化参数化脚本保持模型的组成性结构。

Result: 以水敏松果层级结构为案例，通过熔丝制造（fused filament fabrication）完成制造并实验验证。生成了四类致动器（actuator），覆盖两种刺激类型和两种运动学响应，其中一类致动器完全通过先前验证组件的组合生成，无需额外手动推导。

Conclusion: 组成性不仅可作为描述性语言，还可作为机械材料设计的生成性且系统级可验证的方法。该工作为将形式化多尺度推理嵌入日益计算化、生成化与物理驱动的设计工作流提供了具体路径。

Abstract: Natural materials achieve adaptive behavior through hierarchical organization and coupled mechanisms across scales. Their translation into engineering, however, remains largely heuristic. What is missing is a formal translation framework that carries biological design logic into engineered realization while preserving physical consistency across levels of abstraction. Here we present a category theoretic compositional framework for verified nature-derived design. The framework defines a category of stimulus response dynamical systems with natural and artificial subcategories. It introduces a structure preserving implementation functor from biological mechanics to engineered systems. It also formalizes a machine agnostic specification layer that links behavioral intent to executable fabrication programs. We instantiate the framework on the hygromorphic pinecone hierarchy as a representative biological case. We implement the full pipeline in Grasshopper, where formal specifications are translated into modular parametric scripts that preserve the compositional structure of the model. The resulting designs are fabricated by fused filament fabrication, evaluated experimentally, and tested against model predictions derived from the pipeline. The current implementation generates four actuator classes spanning two stimulus types and two kinematic responses. One actuator arises purely through composition from previously validated components, without additional manual derivation. The results show that compositionality can function not just as a descriptive language, but as a generative and system level verifiable method for mechanical material design. More broadly, the work provides a concrete route for embedding formal multiscale reasoning within increasingly computational, generative, and physics-driven design workflows.

</details>


### [131] [Linear poroelastic response of thin permeable gel films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26464)
*Caroline Kopecz-Muller,Joshua D Mcgraw,Thomas Salez*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文推导了薄层多孔弹性凝胶在点力作用下的力学响应格林函数，发现表面变形仅局限于压痕点附近、范围约等于层厚，可直接用于预测凝胶表面的时空变形，对压痕实验、软物质及微流控润滑等问题具有重要应用价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 亲水性可变形多孔材料（如水凝胶）在溶剂中会大幅膨胀形成超软多孔凝胶，其表面受力时会发生变形并驱动溶剂在孔隙中流动，这种多孔弹性耦合（poroelastic coupling）现象对超薄涂层建模构成挑战，亟需建立其力学响应理论。

Method: 推导了薄层可渗透多孔弹性层（thin, permeable and poroelastic layer）在刚性基底上受点力作用时的力学响应格林函数（Green's function）。

Result: 凝胶表面变形仅局限于压痕点（indentation point）周围，变形范围半径约为层厚量级；所获得的格林函数可直接用于预测凝胶表面在空间和时间上的变形。

Conclusion: 该结果适用于膨胀凝胶的压痕实验、薄膜、软物质及生命体系，以及涉及软多孔壁的润滑问题（如微流控），具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: When a hydrophilic and deformable porous material is immersed in a bath, it may absorb the solvent and expand by several times its volume, thus forming a highly soft and porous hydrogel. A stress applied on the soft hydrogel surface deforms it and forces the absorbed solvent to move by flowing through the network of pores. This coupled phenomenon sets the framework of poroelasticity. Moreover, polymeric gels are often used in ultra-thin coatings to tune surface properties. Together with the characteristic poroelastic coupling, this thinness challenges the modelling of their response. In this article, we derive the point-force mechanical response of a thin, permeable and poroelastic layer bounded to a rigid substrate. We show that the gel surface is only deformed around the indentation point, within a radius on the order of the layer thickness. The obtained Green's function can be directly used to predict the space- and time-dependent surface deformation of the gel. Our findings are relevant for a broad range of applications, such as indentation experiments on swollen gels, thin membranes or soft and living systems, as well as lubrication problems involving a soft and porous wall, for instance in microfluidics.

</details>


### [132] [Programmable Persistent Random Walks in Active Brownian Particles Govern Emergent Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26825)
*Tarun Sunkesula Raghavendra,Yogesh Shelke,Stijn van der Ham,Anpuj Nair S,Hanumantha Rao Vutukuri*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出一种结合光调制推进强度与磁控推进方向的实验策略，在活性布朗粒子（ABPs）中编码多种持久随机游走模式（如列维游走、跑停-转向动力学等），实现了单实验内运动模式的按需切换，并展示了运动模式对团簇动力学的影响，为研究活性物质中的输运与自组织提供了通用平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的合成活性粒子系统大多局限于单一运动模式（即活性布朗粒子，ABPs），无法模拟微生物复杂的动态自组织行为。本研究旨在开发一种通用方法，使单个活性粒子能够执行多种可编程的持久随机游走模式。

Method: 通过将光调节的推进强度（light-modulated propulsion strength）与磁控的推进方向（magnetic control of propulsion direction）相结合，在活性布朗粒子中编码不同的持久随机游走（persistent random walks）。实验实现了列维游走（Levy walks）、跑停-转向动力学（run-and-tumble dynamics）、自规避随机游走（self-avoiding random walks）和高斯游走（Gaussian walks），并可沿复杂轨迹（如斐波那契螺旋线和嵌套多边形）引导粒子运动。

Result: 该系统实现了单实验内运动模式的按需切换，并能够引导粒子沿复杂轨迹（如斐波那契螺旋线和嵌套多边形）运动。通过比较ABPs与作圆周运动的手征活性粒子（chiral active particles）的团簇动力学，证明了推进模式影响团簇行为。

Conclusion: 这些结果建立了一个通用平台，用于研究单个粒子层次的编码运动如何调控活性物质系统的输运、搜索策略和涌现组织（emergent organization）。

Abstract: Self-propelled particles serve as minimal models for emulating the dynamic self-organization of microorganisms, yet most synthetic systems remain limited to a single mode of motion, namely active Brownian particles (ABPs). Here, we present an experimental strategy to encode various persistent random walks in ABPs by combining light-modulated propulsion strength with magnetic control of propulsion direction. Our system enables programmable Levy walks with tunable step-length distributions, run-and-tumble dynamics, self-avoiding random walks, and Gaussian walks, with on-demand switching between motion modes within a single experiment. In addition, particles are steered along complex trajectories such as Fibonacci spirals and nested polygons. Beyond single-particle behavior, we show that propulsion modes influence clustering dynamics by comparing ABPs with chiral active particles undergoing circular motion. These results establish a versatile platform for investigating how encoded motion at the level of individual particles governs transport, search strategies, and emergent organization in active matter systems.

### [133] [Two-Valued Groups, Chazy Equation, Dubrovin-Frobenius Structures, and QYBE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26641)

Abstract: We show that the associativity condition of the universal symmetric 2-algebraic 2-valued group defined by the Buchstaber polynomial admits several mutually equivalent interpretations from the viewpoints of the Chazy equation, Gauss-Manin connections, Dubrovin-Frobenius structures, and the quantum Yang-Baxter equation. These results place the universal 2-valued law in a unified framework linking geometry, algebraic topology, group theory, and mathematical physics.

### [134] [Can we teach generative artificial intelligence the design language of engineered living materials?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26872)
*Andrés Díaz Lantada,José A. Yáñez,William Solórzano-Requejo,Monsur Islam*

<details>

Method: 研究首先开发了一个包含类别（families）、工业应用（industrial applications）和合成/加工方法（synthesis/processing methods）三个维度的本体论，并设计了对应的编码方案。随后，将该本体论系统性地应用于100个ELMs实例，以验证其适用性。此外，研究还测试了生成式AI对本体的理解能力，通过自然语言与编码两种方式验证AI能否正确解析和运用该分类体系。

Result: 该本体论与编码方案成功适用于100种不同类型的ELMs，覆盖广泛的工业应用与合成方法。验证表明，生成式AI能够理解自然语言描述与编码，并能依据本体正确对ELMs示例进行编码，同时可协同生成新型ELMs的插图并支持概念设计。

Conclusion: 该本体论与编码方案可作为ELMs领域的综合性分类工具，为研究者提供通用语言；与生成式AI的协同有望加速ELMs领域的科学发现与技术革新。

Abstract: This study presents a versatile ontology and a useful codification scheme for describing all kinds of engineered living materials (ELMs). The different components of the ontology, namely: families according to the taxonomy for ELMs, industrial applications and synthesis or processing methods, are systematically organized, enumerated, classified, codified and explained. The methodic application of the ontology to a set of 100 relevant examples of ELMs helps to demonstrate its utility and adaptability to many different types of ELMs with a wide range of industrial applications and obtained through numerous synthesis and processing methods. This proves that the developed ontology and codification schemes, with the glossary provided to support its implementation and application, can serve as a comprehensive classification tool for the emergent field of ELMs. Furthermore, the usability of the ELMs ontology and codification by a generative artificial intelligence (AI) is explored and validated by different means, checking that both natural language and the codification are understandable for describing ELMs, verifying that the generative AI adequately codifies examples of ELMs according to the ontology, and validating the synergic applicability of the ontology and codification with generative AI tools for illustrating novel ELMs and supporting their conceptual design. This study is expected to provide a universal language to facilitate communication in the ELMs field and to foster the discovery of new ELMs and related innovations, hoping it may accelerate scientific and technological discoveries.

### [135] [Phases and dynamics of an impurity immersed in one-dimensional quantum droplets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26528)
*Dimitrios Diplaris,Ilias A. Englezos,Friethjof Theel,Peter Schmelcher,Simeon I. Mistakidis*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过从头算模拟研究了一维量子液滴介质（由双组分玻色混合物形成）中的单个杂质基态性质，发现调节杂质-液滴相互作用可重塑液滴密度分布和关联模式，并在释放陷阱后决定三组分体系的膨胀动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索杂质嵌入量子液滴这一新体系中的基态性质与关联效应，弥补现有研究对杂质-液滴混合系统中多体关联理解的不足。

Method: 采用从头算多体模拟（ab-initio simulations）研究一维双组分玻色混合物形成的量子液滴中的单个杂质；将多体结果与扩展Gross-Pitaevskii（extended Gross-Pitaevskii）有效场描述进行对比。

Result: 吸引性杂质-介质耦合会导致杂质局域化在液滴内并产生密度凸起，排斥性耦合则促进相分离；扩展Gross-Pitaevskii描述在密度轮廓上与多体结果基本一致，但系统性地高估了杂质局域化程度；释放陷阱后，杂质-液滴相互作用的符号和强度决定体系的膨胀行为，仅强吸引力耦合能抑制膨胀。

Conclusion: 结果证实了关联效应在杂质-液滴混合物中的关键作用，为未来利用杂质物理探测液滴构型的研究提供了启发。

Abstract: We explore the ground-state properties of a single impurity immersed in a one-dimensional quantum droplet medium formed by a two-component Bose mixture. Relying on ab-initio simulations, we demonstrate that tuning the impurity-droplet interactions allows to controllably reshape the droplets density profiles and associated correlation patterns. For attractive impurity-medium couplings, the impurity becomes localized within the droplet which exhibits a density hump at the vicinity of the impurity, while repulsive interactions facilitate their phase-separation. Comparing our many-body results to the appropriate extended Gross-Pitaevskii description, we find adequate agreement for the droplet density profiles, with the effective field approach systematically overestimating impurity localization. Following a release of the external trap, we unveil that the sign and magnitude of the interactions between the impurity and the droplet hosts dictate the response of the three-component setting which experiences expansion unless strongly attractive intercomponent couplings are present. These results corroborate the role and presence of correlations in impurity-droplet mixtures and inspire future investigations on impurity physics for probing droplet configurations.

### [136] [Quantum scattering of droplets by wells and barriers in one-dimensional Bose-Bose mixtures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26895)
*Sherzod R. Otajonov,Uktambek R. Eshimbetov,Bakhram A. Umarov,Fatkhulla Kh. Abdullaev*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过解析和数值方法研究了准一维量子液滴（quantum droplet）在Pöschl-Teller势阱和势垒上的散射行为，发现临界速度处存在完全反射与透射的突变转变，以及液滴大小不同导致的对称性破缺和相依赖的受限模式等丰富现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解准一维量子液滴在可调外部势（如Pöschl-Teller势）中的散射动力学，揭示其与孤子（soliton）不同的可压缩性、相干性和内部结构等特征。

Method: 采用解析分析与直接数值模拟（direct numerical simulation）相结合的方法，研究小（类孤子）和大（平顶型）量子液滴在吸引势阱与排斥势垒下的散射行为。

Result: 在吸引势阱中，临界速度处出现完全反射到完全透射的突变；小液滴形成空间对称的受限模式（trapped mode），大液滴则形成空间不对称的受限态；临界速度随原子数非单调变化，先升后降，转折点对应可压缩与不可压缩液滴之间的交叉区域。反射无能势阱（reflectionless well）会引入π相位移动，强烈改变液滴-液滴碰撞；碰撞后受限模式是否持续取决于相对相位。排斥势垒存在完全反射、部分返回和完全透射三种行为，取决于入射速度、势垒高度和粒子数。

Conclusion: 量子液滴在Pöschl-Teller势中的散射呈现丰富的动力学现象，包括临界速度转变、对称性破缺、相位依赖的碰撞行为等，所有理论预测均与直接数值模拟一致。

Abstract: We investigate, both analytically and numerically, the scattering of quasi-one-dimensional quantum droplets from Pöschl-Teller potential wells and barriers. For attractive wells, we find a sharp transition between complete reflection and transmission at a critical incident velocity for both small and large flat-top droplets. The scattering interactions differ: small, soliton-like droplets form a spatially symmetric trapped mode at the critical velocity, showing their compressibility and coherence characteristics, while large droplets develop a spatially asymmetric trapped state, revealing incompressibility and internal structure. The critical velocity depends non-monotonically on atom number: it rises in the small, compressible-droplet regime, falls in the incompressible, flat-top regime, and turns at the crossover point. We also show that the reflectionless well generates a $π$-phase shift, strongly altering droplet-droplet collisions relative to free space. The persistence of a confined mode after collisions between trapped and incident droplets depends sensitively on their relative phase. For the repulsive barrier, we identify regimes of complete reflection, partial return, and full transmission, depending on incident velocity, barrier height, and particle number. Our predictions match direct numerical simulations in all cases.

</details>

### [137] [Constitutive Modelling of Korteweg Fluids Using Liu's Method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26846)
*Zagorka Matić,Srboljub Simić,Peter Ván*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文运用刘氏乘子法（Liu's method of multipliers）对Korteweg流体进行本构建模（constitutive modelling），在满足热力学一致性（thermodynamic consistency）的条件下将毛细效应（capillary effects）纳入比熵，推导出Korteweg应力并建立了含毛细效应的广义Gibbs关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为Korteweg流体的本构建模提供热力学一致的理论框架，确保模型与熵平衡律（entropy balance law）相容，并纳入毛细效应及热-力耦合。

Method: 采用刘氏乘子法实现热力学一致性；通过适当本构假设将毛细效应引入比熵；从熵产生（entropy production）消失及其在平衡态最小化条件推导Korteweg应力。

Result: Korteweg应力中的材料参数可依赖温度，与动理论（kinetic-theory）结果一致，并导致热-力交叉耦合；推导出继承毛细效应的广义Gibbs关系（generalized Gibbs' relation）。

Conclusion: 刘氏乘子法能够自洽地处理Korteweg流体的本构模型，广义Gibbs关系的出现是该方法的独特特征。

Abstract: The paper studies constitutive modelling of Korteweg fluids. Thermodynamic consistency, i.e. compatibility with entropy balance law, is achieved using Liu's method of multipliers. Appropriate constitutive assumptions facilitated inclusion of the capillary effects in the specific entropy. Korteweg stresses are derived from the equilibrium conditions -- vanishing of the entropy production and its minimization in equilibrium. Material parameter in Korteweg stresses is allowed to depend on temperature, which turns out to be consistent with kinetic-theory results and leads to cross-coupling of mechanical and thermal effects. The generalized Gibbs' relation, which inherits the capillary effects, is derived as consequence, which is a peculiar feature of the Liu's method.

### [138] [Physics-based modeling of cyclic and calendar aging of LIBs with Si-Gr composite anodes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26545)
*Micha C. J. Philipp,Lukas Köbbing,Alexander Karger,Andreas Jossen,Arnulf Latz,Birger Horstmann*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个基于物理的模型，用于描述含硅负极锂离子电池在循环与存储过程中的退化机制，并揭示了检查频率（check-up frequency）对退化表现的影响，为电池使用与设计优化提供了理论依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 下一代锂离子电池需要更高的能量密度和更长的寿命。硅（silicon）作为有前景的负极材料，虽具有高比容量，但其在嵌锂/脱锂过程中的巨大体积变化会显著缩短电池寿命。因此，理解导致电池退化的物理过程是缓解该问题、推动领域发展的关键。

Method: 开发了一个基于物理的模型（physics-based model），用于描述不同循环协议、存储条件以及不同检查频率（check-up, CU）下的电池退化过程。该模型能够区分基本退化机制（如固体电解质界面（Solid-Electrolyte Interphase, SEI）的生长）与硅相关机制（如颗粒开裂、裂纹处SEI生长以及活性材料损失（loss of active material, LAM））。

Result: 分析了检查频率（CU）对观测到的存储退化的影响，阐明了含硅负极电池退化加剧的原因；并将观测到的退化与运行条件关联起来。

Conclusion: 该模型为未来电池使用与设计的优化提供了理论依据，有助于通过理解退化机制来延长含硅负极锂离子电池的寿命。

Abstract: Higher energy density and longer lifetime are the requirements for next-generation lithium-ion batteries. A promising anode material is silicon, which offers high specific capacity, but its significant volume change during lithiation and delithiation enormously reduces battery lifetime. A physical understanding of the processes degrading the battery is key to mitigate this effect and advance in the field. We develop a physics-based model to describe degradation during battery cycling under various protocols and storage conditions, with varying check-up (CU) frequencies. The model can disentangle basic degradation mechanisms, such as the growth of the Solid-Electrolyte Interphase (SEI), from silicon mechanisms, such as particle cracking, SEI growth on cracks, and loss of active material (LAM). We investigate the impact of CUs on the observed storage degradation and the reason behind the increased degradation in batteries, including silicon in the anode. Additionally, we relate the observed degradation to operating conditions, enabling future optimization of battery use and design.

### [139] [Quantum Hall Liquids Coupled to Dynamical Electromagnetism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26014)
*T. H. Hansson,Qing-Dong Jiang,S. A. Kivelson,Thomas Klein Kvorning*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了量子霍尔（Quantum Hall, QH）液体与三维动态电磁场耦合所产生的效应，该耦合导致系统无能隙。在热力学极限下，霍尔电阻（Hall resistance, ρ_H）保持量子化，纵向电阻（longitudinal resistance, ρ_L）趋近于与精细结构常数（fine structure constant, α）和克利青常数（Klitzing constant, R_K）成正比的非零极限；同时，霍尔电导（Hall conductance, σ_H）相比量子化值有约为α²/R_K的修正，准粒子电荷与统计也受到α²量级的修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究量子霍尔液体与三维动态电磁场耦合后，系统呈现无能隙（gapless）行为时，其霍尔电阻、纵向电阻以及电导的量子化性质是否会受到破坏或修正。

Method: 构建了一个最小化的电磁环境模型，其中包含一个允许反向流动电流（counter-flow current）的小三维电导率（conductivity, \tilde{σ}），以此计算霍尔电阻ρ_H、纵向电阻ρ_L以及霍尔电导σ_H；同时利用规范不变性（gauge invariance）论证了准粒子电荷与统计的修正，并给出与复合玻色子（composite boson）表象中通量附着（flux attachment）相关的直观论证。

Result: 在热力学极限下，ρ_H保持量子化；ρ_L趋近于非零极限ρ_L ∼ α R_K；σ_H相比预期量子化值存在∼α²/R_K的修正；准粒子电荷与统计均受到α²量级的修正。

Conclusion: 电磁相互作用对量子霍尔液体的输运性质及准粒子属性产生可计算的修正，但霍尔电阻的量子化在热力学极限下得以维持；这些结果与基于规范不变性的一般论证及复合玻色子通量附着的直观图像自洽。

Abstract: We investigate the effect on a Quantum Hall (QH) liquid of its coupling to 3+1 dimensional dynamical electromagnetism, which renders the system gapless. We calculate both the Hall and longitudinal resistances, $ρ_H$ and $ρ_L$, in the context of a minimal model of the electromagnetic environment, with a small three dimensional conductivity ${\tildeσ}$, that allows for a counter-flow current. In the thermodynamic limit, we show that $ρ_H$ is quantized, while $ρ_L$ approaches a non-zero limit, $ρ_L \sim α\, R_K$, where $α$ and $R_K=2π/e^2$ are the fine structure and the Klitzing constant. In contrast, the QH conductance, $σ_H$, is smaller than the expected quantized value by a correction $\sim α^2/R_K$. The electromagnetic interaction also generates corrections of order $α^2$ to the quasiparticle charges and statistics, in a way that is consistent with general arguments based on gauge invariance. In addition, we present an intuitive argument that relates the flux attachment associated with the composite boson representation of the electron liquid to the empirically observed %persistence of approximate quantization of $ρ_H$, even in circumstances in which $ρ_L$, and the deviation of $σ_H$ from its quantized value, are substantial.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文揭示了由非阿贝尔多能带带拓扑（non-Abelian multigap band topology）中非平凡欧拉类不变量（Euler class invariant）所引发的可观测磁非线性霍尔输运现象（magnetononlinear Hall transport），并在二维kagome氮杂环卡宾（NHC）金属有机框架中展示了这些效应及其调控性。

Method: 以最近合成的二维kagome氮杂环卡宾（NHC）金属有机框架为模型体系，通过外加电压、温度变化和化学取代等可控手段，研究在保持体相拓扑（bulk topology）及相应边缘态（edge states）不变的条件下，非线性输运效应的变化规律。

Conclusion: 金属有机材料中存在此前未知的欧拉类拓扑（Euler class topology），其可通过可测量的磁输运实验加以检测，为拓扑材料与非线性输运研究开辟了新方向。

Abstract: We unveil that non-Abelian multigap band topology characterized by nontrivial Euler class invariants induces observable magnetononlinear Hall transport phenomena. We demonstrate these effects in a highly-tunable class of recently synthesized two-dimensional kagome N-heterocyclic carbene (NHC) metal-organic frameworks. We showcase the controllability of the nonlinear effect upon applying external voltage, changing temperature, and chemical substitutions that preserve the bulk topology and associated edge states. Our findings therefore reveal an uncharted presence of Euler class topology in metal-organic materials that can be experimentally deduced through measurable magnetotransport.

### [141] [Strain and Twist Engineering of Interfacial Thermal Transport in Homo- and Hetero-Interfaces of Graphene and Hexagonal Boron Nitride](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26300)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 预测并理解同质与异质二维材料界面（如石墨烯（graphene）/六方氮化硼（h-BN））在外部力学扰动（面内应变和界面扭转）下垂直热导率（vertical thermal conductance）的差异行为及其物理机制。

Method: 采用原子尺度模拟（atomistic simulations）计算界面热导率；利用费米黄金定则（Fermi's golden rule）和声子态密度（density of phonon modes）分析解释模拟结果；提出一个基于局部层间距（local interlayer distance）和局部堆叠构型（local stacking）的简单唯象模型（phenomenological model）来拟合热导率对应变和扭转的依赖关系。

Result: 同质石墨烯和氮化硼界面的垂直热导率对面内应变和界面扭转均表现出显著的降低；而异质石墨烯/氮化硼界面的垂直热导率对扭转形变不敏感，但在压缩应变下显著升高、拉伸应变下显著降低。声子分析表明垂直方向的声子（vertical phonons）和局部堆叠构型在层间热输运中起核心作用。

Conclusion: 垂直声子和局部堆叠构型是决定层间热输运行为的关键因素；基于层间距和堆叠的简单唯象模型能够有效描述垂直热导率对应变和扭转形变的依赖关系，为理解二维异质界面热管理提供了理论基础。

Abstract: A dramatic difference between the vertical thermal conductance response of homogeneous and heterogeneous graphene/h-BN interfaces to external mechanical perturbations, is predicted. Homogeneous graphene and h-BN interfaces exhibit strong conductance reduction for both in-plane strain and interfacial twist. Conversely, the vertical thermal conductance of the heterogeneous graphene/h-BN junction is insensitive to twist deformations but shows significant increase or decrease under compressive or tensile strains, respectively. Our atomistic simulations predictions are rationalized by Fermi's golden rule and density of phonon modes analyses, indicating that vertical phonons and local stacking configurations have a central role in the interlayer heat transport behavior. A simple phenomenological model, based on local interlayer distance and stacking, captures well the dependence of vertical heat conductance on strain and twist deformations.

### [144] [Flux-Mediated Correspondence Between Real- and Momentum-Space Nonsymmorphicity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26575)
*Z. Y. Chen,Y. X. Zhao*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个关于动量空间晶体学群（momentum-space crystallographic groups）的一般理论，该理论源于在规范通量（gauge flux）存在下实空间晶体学群的投影表示（projective representations）。核心结果是发现了一种由规范通量介导的“双非对称性（bi-nonsymmorphicity）”关系，揭示了实空间与动量空间非对称性之间的结构对应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管实空间非对称性（real-space nonsymmorphic symmetries）在晶体拓扑相（crystalline topological phases）研究中早已发挥重要作用，而动量空间非对称性（momentum-space nonsymmorphic symmetries）近期也在人工晶体和凝聚态晶体中引起广泛关注，但二者之间在规范通量存在下的系统性联系尚缺乏一般理论框架。

Method: 作者从实空间晶体学群的投影表示出发，系统构建了动量空间晶体学群的一般理论，特别适用于实空间非对称群。通过引入规范通量作为关键中介，推导出“双非对称性”关系，从而建立实空间与动量空间非对称性之间的结构对应。

Result: 该“双非对称性”关系表明：在对称规范通量（symmetric gauge flux）下，实空间非对称性可以强制产生动量空间非对称性；在某些情形下，对称规范通量要求实空间和动量空间同时具备非对称性。

Conclusion: 这项工作不仅揭示了投影晶体对称性（projective crystal symmetries）中的一个基本结构，还为设计同时具有实空间和动量空间非对称性的人工晶体与凝聚态平台提供了指导原则。

Abstract: Momentum-space nonsymmorphic symmetries have recently attracted significant interest in both artificial and condensed-matter crystals, whereas real-space nonsymmorphic symmetries have long played an important role in the study of crystalline topological phases. Here, we establish a general theory of momentum-space crystallographic groups that emerge from projective representations of real-space crystallographic groups in the presence of gauge flux, applicable in particular to real-space nonsymmorphic groups. A central result is a flux-mediated ``bi-nonsymmorphicity'' relation that reveals a structural correspondence between real-space and momentum-space nonsymmorphicity mediated by gauge flux. This relation implies that, under a symmetric gauge flux, real-space nonsymmorphicity can enforce momentum-space nonsymmorphicity, and that in some cases a symmetric gauge flux requires nonsymmorphicity in both real and momentum space. Our work not only identifies a fundamental structure in projective crystal symmetries, but also provides guiding principles for designing artificial crystals and condensed-matter platforms that exhibit both real-space and momentum-space nonsymmorphic symmetries.

Abstract: Moiré superlattices based on rhombohedral multilayer graphene have emerged as a highly tunable platform for engineering correlated topological phases. ### [146] [Beyond conventional skyrmions in synthetic antiferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26680)

Conclusion: 该有效场方法（effective-field method）为实现多层膜中选定层内极性可控的可编程三维自旋织构（three-dimensional spin textures）提供了一条稳健路径，在基于斯格明子的计算和自旋逻辑架构（spin-logic architectures）中具有应用潜力。

Abstract: Magnetic skyrmions are topologically protected spin textures that can act as reconfigurable nanoscale information carriers. In synthetic antiferromagnets (SAFs), interlayer exchange coupling offers an additional control parameter beyond the interfacial Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction (DMI) and magnetic anisotropy. Here, we engineer a SAF composed of two chemically distinct ferromagnets (CoB and CoFeB), in which the external magnetic field and interlayer exchange act asymmetrically on the sublattices. The competition of these effects, acting as a resultant effective-field, gives rise to two distinct skyrmion families in different field regimes. In large fields, conventional-polarity skyrmions nucleate, with core antiparallel to the external field, whereas in smaller fields an inverse-polarity skyrmion state emerges as the effective-field reverses sign and almost saturates the CoFeB layers. Return-point memory measurements confirm independent nucleation pathways for the two families. Using element-resolved x-ray magnetometry, correlative magnetic force and Lorentz transmission electron microscopies, and parameter-matched micromagnetic modelling, we show that all textures reside only in the CoFeB layers, which experience a Ruderman-Kittel-Kasuya-Yosida (RKKY) exchange field originating from the CoB layers. This effective-field method provides a robust route to programmable three-dimensional spin textures with controlled polarity in selected layers of a multilayer with potential for applications in skyrmion-based computing and spin-logic architectures.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统凝聚态理论通过费米面附近是否存在带电准粒子（quasiparticle）来区分金属与绝缘体，但该判据在贝里曲率（Berry curvature）主导的系统中失效。本文旨在揭示这类系统中的非常规输运机制，并探索超越德鲁德（Drude）模型的电导起源。

Method: 本文发展了一套针对体拓扑绝缘体（bulk topological insulators）的量子输运微观理论，该系统在费米能级处态密度（density of states）为零，传统德鲁德贡献缺失。研究通过分析杂质散射引起的相干性衰减（coherence decay），探讨其在拓扑平庸区域产生的纵向输运通道，并严格排除边缘态贡献。

Result: 即使在费米能级处无载流子时，系统仍表现出有限纵向电导率（longitudinal conductivity）。该电导在稀释极限下与杂质密度（impurity density）呈线性关系，与德鲁德行为截然不同。此外，该退相干诱导的电导与温度成反比，呈现出类似奇异金属（strange-metal）行为的特征。

Conclusion: 量子退相干（quantum decoherence）是超越德鲁德范式的纵向输运的基本起源，这一发现挑战了金属与绝缘体之间的传统区分标准。

Abstract: In modern condensed matter theory, phases of electronic matter--such as metals and insulators-are fundamentally distinguished by the presence or absence of charge-carrying quasiparticles or excitations near the Fermi surface at low temperatures. Here, we show that this criterion breaks down in Berry-curvature-dominated systems, where transport is governed by interband coherence across the entire Fermi sea. We develop a microscopic theory of quantum transport in bulk topological insulators with a vanishing density of states at the Fermi energy, for which the conventional Drude contribution is absent. We demonstrate that impurity-scattering-induced coherence decay generates a distinct longitudinal transport channel even in the topologically trivial regime, with edge contributions rigorously excluded. This mechanism yields a finite longitudinal conductivity even in the absence of carriers at the Fermi level and exhibits an unconventional scaling linear in impurity density in the dilute limit, in stark contrast to Drude behaviour. Importantly, this decoherence-induced conductance is inversely proportional to temperature, reminiscent of strange-metal behaviour, most prominently observed in cuprate superconductors above their critical temperature. Our findings reveal quantum decoherence as a fundamental origin of longitudinal transport beyond the Drude paradigm, challenging the traditional distinction between metals and insulators.

</details>


### [148] [Non-Equilibrium Orbital Transport in Terahertz Optorbitronics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26717)
*Sobhan Subhra Mishra,Ranjan Singh*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文介绍了“太赫兹轨道电子学”（terahertz optorbitronics）这一新兴领域，利用超快飞秒激光脉冲和太赫兹辐射实时追踪纳米薄膜材料中轨道角动量（OAM）电流的生成、传播与转换过程，揭示了当前关于轨道电流传播机制（弹道波式传播 vs. 数原子层内衰减）的根本性争议，并探讨了通过材料设计、光场、电门控等手段主动控制轨道输运的可能性，为超越传统自旋电子学（spintronics）极限的更快、更高效纳米器件开辟了新方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代信息技术依赖电子的电荷（charge）和自旋（spin）控制，但轨道角动量（OAM）作为新兴的信息载体有望实现更节能的器件并减少对稀缺重元素的依赖；然而轨道电流（orbital current）的产生与输运机制，尤其在超快时间尺度上，仍基本未知，这是当前领域面临的核心挑战。

Method: 本文采用综述方法，系统介绍了太赫兹轨道电子学（terahertz optorbitronics），即利用超快飞秒激光脉冲和太赫兹辐射，在四分之一皮秒（quadrillionth of a second）时间尺度上实时追踪纳米薄膜材料中轨道电流的发射、传播及其向电信号的转换过程。

Result: 近期实验揭示了两个相互矛盾的图景：轨道电流可能像弹道波（ballistic wave）一样传播数十纳米，也可能在仅数原子层内迅速衰减；该技术能够将轨道运动与传统的自旋输运（spin transport）区分开来；同时，从工程化石墨烯到交变磁体（altermagnets）等新材料可作为可调谐的轨道电流源。

Conclusion: 太赫兹轨道电子学将轨道输运揭示为一个动态的非平衡过程（non-equilibrium process），为纳米科学开辟了新的方向，有望催生比传统自旋电子学更快、更高效的技术。

Abstract: Modern information technologies rely on controlling the flow of electrons through their charge and spin. A rapidly emerging alternative is to use the orbital motion of electrons, the way they circulate around atomic sites as a new carrier of information. This orbital angular momentum (OAM) could enable more energy-efficient devices and reduce reliance on scarce heavy elements, but how orbital currents are generated and transported, especially on ultrafast timescales, remains largely unknown. In this review, we introduce terahertz optorbitronics, an approach that uses ultrafast femtosecond laser pulses and terahertz radiation to observe orbital transport in real time. On timescales of quadrillionth of a second, this technique allows us to track how orbital currents are launched, propagate, and convert into electrical signals in nanoscale thin-film materials. Surprisingly, recent experiments have revealed conflicting pictures such as orbital currents may travel over tens of nanometres like ballistic waves or instead decay within just a few atomic layers, highlighting a fundamental unresolved question in the field. We explain how these ultrafast measurements can disentangle orbital motion from conventional spin transport, and we highlight new materials from engineered graphene to altermagnets, that could act as tunable sources of orbital currents. We also discuss how light, electrical gating, strain, and interface design can be used to actively control orbital transport and improve its conversion into usable electronic signals. By revealing orbital transport as a dynamic, non-equilibrium process, terahertz optorbitronics opens a new direction for nanoscale science, the one that could lead to faster, more efficient technologies operating beyond the limits of conventional spin-based electronics.

### [149] [Universal magnetotunnel conductance at a Weyl semimetal-layered Chern insulator junction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26739)
*Nirnoy Basak,Sumathi Rao,Faruk Abdulla*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究外尔半金属（Weyl semimetal, WSM）与层状陈绝缘体（layered Chern insulator, LCI）在垂直磁场下的结区电子输运，发现界面费米弧（Fermi arc）态因拓扑失配（topological mismatch）产生独特连接方式，且磁隧穿电导在低场下线性增长并在临界场后饱和到一个与微观细节无关的普适常数，揭示该普适性源于拓扑电荷泵浦（topological charge pumping）机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索拓扑失配体系（外尔半金属与层状陈绝缘体）界面处电子输运的新物理行为，特别是磁隧穿电导的普适饱和现象及其拓扑起源。

Method: 构建外尔半金属-层状陈绝缘体结区模型，在垂直界面磁场下分析界面谱（spectrum），并计算由界面局域态介导的磁隧穿电导（magneto tunnel conductance）。

Result: 界面费米弧具有与WSM-WSM结不同的连接方式（通过布里渊区边界重新连接而非终止于外尔节点投影）；电导在低磁场下随磁场线性增加，超过临界场后饱和至与界面耦合、弧几何及晶格尺度参数无关的普适常数值；在特定条件下，两种不同外尔半金属之间的结区也呈现类似饱和行为。

Conclusion: 该普适饱和现象并非源于费米弧间的磁击穿（magnetic breakdown），而是由陈层（Chern layers）的拓扑电荷泵浦所主导，澄清了该普适性的拓扑起源。

Abstract: We investigate electronic transport across a junction between a Weyl semimetal (WSM) and a layered Chern insulator (LCI) in the presence of a magnetic field perpendicular to the interface. The topological mismatch between the gapless Weyl semimetal and the momentum-resolved chiral edge modes of the layered Chern insulator leads to interface Fermi-arc states with a qualitatively distinct connectivity: unlike WSM-WSM junctions, the interface Fermi arcs are forced to reconnect through the Brillouin-zone boundary rather than terminating at the projections of the Weyl nodes. We analyze the spectrum and compute the magneto tunnel conductance mediated by the interface-localized states. We find that the conductance increases linearly with magnetic field at low fields and saturates beyond a critical field to a constant value that is independent of microscopic details such as interface coupling, arc geometry, and lattice-scale parameters. This universal saturation reflects a transport mechanism governed by the topological charge pumping associated with the Chern layers, rather than magnetic breakdown between Fermi arcs. We further show that, under specific conditions, a junction between two distinct Weyl semimetals can exhibit a similar saturation behavior, thereby clarifying the topological origin of the observed universality.

Abstract: Ultrafast scintillators are indispensable for precise timing in high-energy physics and medical diagnostics. Fundamentally constrained by the trade-off between emission rate and light yield, conventional scintillators remain kinetically trapped in the sub-nanosecond regime, failing to break 50-picosecond limit. Here, we demonstrate a strategy to bypass this limitation by harnessing the coherent radiative acceleration in weakly confined CsPbCl3 perovskite nanocrystals to generate an ultrafast photon burst. This effect originates from the giant oscillator strength, which we unlock by suppressing exciton-phonon scattering at mild cryogenic temperatures. Consequently, our scintillator achieves an unprecedented dominant lifetime of 13.11 ps alongside a high light yield of 21,851 ph/MeV. The resulting prompt photon emission rate more than 100 times higher than that of state-of-the-art ultrafast scintillators. We validate this breakthrough in realistic detection scenarios, achieving a coincidence time resolution of 30.8 ps and accurately resolving 13.5 ps electron bunches and 16.6 ps single-shot gamma-ray pulses. Our findings establish a robust coherent framework for next-generation ultrafast scintillators, pushing extreme radiation diagnostics into the picosecond frontier.

Method: 通过研究非对角Aubry–André–Harper链中的量子输运，分析边缘态（edge states）、带内体态（in-band bulk states）和带边体态（band-edge bulk states）的输运特征，并考察链-电极耦合强度（chain–electrode coupling strength）和退相干（dephasing）对输运行为的影响。

Result: 带边体态表现出类似边缘态的行为，对系统尺寸依赖性弱；带内体态则呈现明显的尺寸依赖性振荡。链-电极耦合控制透射共振展宽，驱动从隧穿主导到近弹道输运的交叉。退相干对不同态类产生不同的敏感性，取决于其空间局域化程度。

Conclusion: 内部边界和量子相干性（quantum coherence）在调控调制一维系统（modulated one-dimensional systems）的输运中起关键作用。

Abstract: We investigate quantum transport in an off-diagonal Aubry--André--Harper chain. The periodic hopping modulation generates effective internal boundaries that strongly influence the transmission characteristics. We show that edge, in-band bulk, and band-edge bulk states can be clearly distinguished through their transport signatures. In particular, bulk states near the band edges exhibit behavior similar to edge states, with weak dependence on system size, whereas in-band bulk states display pronounced size-dependent oscillations. We further demonstrate that the chain--electrode coupling strength controls the broadening of transmission resonances and drives a crossover from tunneling-dominated to nearly ballistic transport. In addition, dephasing introduces distinct sensitivity across different state classes, depending on their degree of spatial localization. These results highlight the key role of internal boundaries and quantum coherence in governing transport in modulated one-dimensional systems.

### [152] [Large quantum dot energy level shifts in anomalous photon-assisted tunneling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26947)
*Jared Benson,C. E. Sturner,A. R. Huffman,Sanghyeok Park,Valentin John,Brighton X. Coe,Tyler J. Kovach,Stefan D. Oosterhout,Lucas E. A. Stehouwer,Francesco Borsoi,Giordano Scappucci,Menno Veldhorst,Benjamin D. Woods,Mark Friesen,M. A. Eriksson*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 实验发现ST劈裂对顶栅电压存在显著的强依赖性，导致反常的PAT测量结果。所建立的模型能很好地描述ST劈裂随门电压的线性变化。此外，当器件被重新调谐后，两个量子点的ST劈裂表现出类似的线性门电压依赖关系，但两者的比例显著不同。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了顶栅电压对ST劈裂的强线性依赖效应，推翻了此前认为该依赖可忽略的普遍假设，为理解量子点空穴自旋量子比特的控制机制提供了新的实验依据和理论模型。

Abstract: Orbital energy splittings are important quantum dot parameters for the operation of hole spin qubits. They are known to depend on the lateral confinement of the quantum dots. However, when changing top, plunger gate voltages, which are the typical control parameter for qubit applications, such energy splitting changes are typically negligible, both as measured in experiment and as assumed in effective theories. Here, we study the singlet-triplet (ST) splittings, which depend on the orbital splittings, of a double quantum dot (DQD) in a Ge/SiGe heterostructure using photon-assisted tunneling (PAT) and pulsed-gate spectroscopy. We find that the ST splittings have a surprising, strong dependence on the top gate voltages, leading to anomalous PAT measurements. We combine data from both measurements in a model that well describes the linear gate-voltage dependence of the ST splittings. Finally, we show that the ST splittings of the two dots exhibit similar linear gate-voltage dependences when the device is retuned such that their ratio is significantly different.

### [153] [Turing patterns on non-fluctuating surfaces under mechanical stresses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26309)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用反应-扩散方程（reaction-diffusion equation）对激活因子$u$和抑制因子$v$在二维和三维晶格上进行数值研究；通过芬斯勒几何建模技术实现力学特性，引入对应于机械应力方向的内部自由度$\vecτ$；利用基于高斯键势的应力公式在非涨落晶格上计算熵，以捕捉应力松弛现象。

Consequently, $u$ and $v$ have values at spatially discrete points, such as the pigment cells in zebrafish and sea shells. Furthermore, the mechanical property is implemented through the Finsler geometry modeling technique. This technique incorporates the internal degree of freedom $\vecτ$, corresponding to the direction of mechanical stress. Additionally, a stress formula based on Gaussian bond potential is shown to be well-defined on the non-fluctuating lattices, and therefore, it enables the calculation of entropy for capturing the stress relaxation phenomenon in a manner analogous to that on fluctuating surfaces. The results of the study indicate that these biological patterns also exhibit responses to external mechanical forces similar to TPs on fluctuating membranes.

### [154] [The dynamical algebra of the generic superintegrable model on the two-sphere](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26122)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将二阶Jacobi代数（rank two Jacobi algebra）$\mathfrak{J}_2$嵌入到$\mathfrak{su}(1,1)^{\otimes 3}$中，利用该嵌入关系构建物理表示（physical representation），并在此表示框架下进行代数推导。

Abstract: The rank two Jacobi algebra $\mathfrak{J}_2$ is identified as the dynamical algebra of the generic quadratic superintegrable model on the two-sphere. The physical representation of this algebra is obtained from its embedding in $\mathfrak{su}(1,1)^{\otimes 3}$. The exact solution of the model is derived algebraically from this representation. *Shousuke Ohmori,Junichi Takahashi*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在赋范希尔伯特空间（rigged Hilbert spaces, RHS）框架下，为拟厄米刘维尔算符（quasi-Hermitian Liouvillian operators）建立了一个超bra-ket形式体系。通过利用希尔伯特-施密特算符空间（Hilbert-Schmidt operators）与张量积希尔伯特空间的酉等价性，重构了刘维尔空间中的RHS（即赋范刘维尔空间，RLS）。该RLS为超bra-ket的构造以及厄米与非厄米刘维尔算符（Liouville operators）的谱分解提供了严格基础，并以调和振子为例阐明了两种谱分解形式的差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的刘维尔空间框架在严格处理拟厄米刘维尔算符的超bra-ket形式及其谱分解时缺乏严格的数学基础，需要一种更严谨的数学结构来支撑相关构造。

Method: 基于希尔伯特-施密特算符空间与张量积希尔伯特空间之间的酉等价性，将RHS框架推广到刘维尔空间，构建了赋范刘维尔空间（RLS）。利用RLS中的广义本征向量（generalized eigenvectors）来统一刻画厄米与非厄米刘维尔算符的超bra-ket构造和谱分解，并保持非厄米刘维尔算符及其伴随算符之间的对称结构。

Result: 建立了RLS框架，为超bra-ket构造以及厄米和拟厄米刘维尔算符的谱分解提供了严格数学基础；实现了非厄米刘维尔算符与其伴随算符的对称构造。以厄米和非厄米调和振子为例，展示了两种刘维尔算符谱分解形式的差异。

Conclusion: 所提出的RLS方法为拟厄米刘维尔算符的超bra-ket形式提供了严格的数学基础，能够对称地构造非厄米刘维尔算符及其伴随算符，并揭示了厄米与非厄米情形下谱分解形式之间的本质区别。

Abstract: We discuss a super bra-ket formalism for quasi-Hermitian Liouvillian operators within the framework of rigged Hilbert spaces (RHS). An RHS in terms of the Liouville space, referred to as a rigged Liouville space (RLS), is reconstructed by exploiting the mathematical fact that the space of Hilbert-Schmidt operators is unitarily equivalent to the tensor product of Hilbert spaces. The obtained RLS endows a rigorous foundation of the construction for the super bra-ket and for the spectral decompositions of both Hermitian and quasi-Hermitian Liouville operators, which are characterized by the generalized eigenvectors in the dual spaces. Furthermore, within this framework, the non-Hermitian Liouvillian operator and its adjoint can be constructed symmetrically, with their symmetric structure preserved. As an application of our RLS methodology, we examine the Liouville operators corresponding to Hermitian and non-Hermitian harmonic oscillators and elucidate the differences between their spectral decomposition forms.

</details>


### [156] [Combinatorics and asymptotic behavior for double Hurwitz numbers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26323)
*Xiang Li*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文从2-Toda hierarchy出发推导了双Hurwitz数的Pandharipande型方程，并基于这些方程和[4]中的方法，研究了双Hurwitz数的大亏格（large genus）和大度数（large degree）渐近行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典Hurwitz数已有基于Pandharipande方程的多项式时间算法[4]，且双Hurwitz数的配分函数已被证明满足2-Toda hierarchy[21]。本文旨在进一步建立双Hurwitz数与2-Toda hierarchy之间的深层联系，并利用这种代数结构研究其渐近性质。

Method: 类似[21]的做法，从2-Toda hierarchy导出双Hurwitz数的Pandharipande型方程；再结合[4]中发展出的计算方法，将这些代数方程应用于大亏格和大度数情形下的渐近分析。

Result: 得到了双Hurwitz数在大亏格以及大度数下的渐近行为。

Conclusion: 2-Toda hierarchy导出的Pandharipande型方程不仅能够用于构造多项式时间算法，还能有效地推导双Hurwitz数的渐近公式，拓展了[4]和[21]方法的适用范围。

Abstract: Polynomial-in-time algorithms for computing classical Hurwitz numbers were given in [4] based on the Pandharipande equation. The paritition function of double Hurwitz numbers was proved [21] to satisfy the 2-Toda hierarchy. In this paper, similar to [21] we derive Pandharipande-type equations for double Hurwitz numbers from 2-Toda hierarchy. Based on these equations and a method from [4], we study large genus as well as large degree asymptotics of double Hurwitz numbers.

</details>


### [157] [On enumeration of $b$-angulations of surfaces from an integrability perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26354)
*Elba Garcia-Failde,Jianghao Xu,Di Yang,Don Zagier*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于Toda可积性（Toda integrability）和Hodge-GUE对应（Hodge-GUE correspondence），系统研究了封闭有向曲面上固定亏格（genus）的多边形剖分计数级数，在b=3和b=4情形下证明了新的结构结果，并在b=2ν（ν≥2）情形下推导出精细结构，证实了Gharakhloo–Latimer的一个猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在建立封闭有向曲面上多边形剖分（polygonal angulation）的生成级数（generating series）的结构性结果，特别是针对b=3和b=4这两种情形，并验证Gharakhloo–Latimer提出的猜想性论断。

Method: 研究采用Toda可积性（Toda integrability）框架处理b=3和b=4的情形；对于b=2ν（ν≥2）的情形，则利用Hodge–GUE对应（Hodge–GUE correspondence）进行分析。

Result: 在b=3和b=4情形下获得了新的结构结果；在b=2ν情形下推导出精细结构（fine structure），从而证实了Gharakhloo–Latimer的猜想性论断。

Conclusion: 本文借助可积系统与Hodge–GUE对应，为固定亏格曲面上b-边形剖分的枚举计数问题提供了新的结构性刻画，并完成了对相关猜想的证明。

Abstract: In this paper, we study generating series enumerating polygonal angulations of closed oriented surfaces of fixed genus, focusing on $b$-angulations with $b = 3$ or $b = 2ν$, $ν\geq 2$. Based on Toda integrability, we establish new structural results in the cases $b = 3$ and $b = 4$. Furthermore, via the Hodge--GUE correspondence, we derive a fine structure in the $b = 2ν$ case, which implies a conjectural statement of Gharakhloo--Latimer.

</details>

### [158] [Dispersion Splitting of Phonon Polaritons in van der Waals Heterostructure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26260)
*Daeho Noh,Jaehyeong Ock,Sergey G. Menabde,Min Seok Jang*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文实验展示了α相三氧化钼（α-MoO3）在Type-I Reststrahlen波段（RB-I）中双曲声子极化激元（hyperbolic phonon-polaritons）的杂化模式分裂，并通过引入六方氮化硼（hBN）间隔层和石墨烯调控，提出了一种新的色散工程（dispersion engineering）平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管α-MoO3在RB-I中支持低损耗、长寿命的双曲声子极化激元，但该波段的色散工程尚未得到充分探索，亟需发展有效的调控手段。

Method: 将两片α-MoO3薄片紧密放置，利用其本征模杂化导致色散分裂为具有不同动量和场对称性的两支；以六方氮化硼（hBN）为间隔层构建异质结构，通过散射型扫描近场光学显微镜（s-SNOM）探测；并提出引入石墨烯并通过调控其费米能级（Fermi energy）实现主动模式选择性色散调控的设计框架。

Result: 实验证实了α-MoO3在RB-I中的声子极化激元模式分裂，并验证了该异质结构可用于色散操控。

Conclusion: 该工作证明了RB-I中声子极化激元模式分裂的可行性，并为双曲声子极化激元的色散工程提供了新的通用平台。

Abstract: The biaxial van der Waals crystal α-phase molybdenum trioxide (α-MoO3) supports hyperbolic phonon-polaritons with anomalous dispersion in the Type-I Reststrahlen band (RB-I). Despite the low loss and long lifetime of these polaritons, dispersion engineering in this regime has remained largely unexplored. In this work, we show that when two α-MoO3 slabs are placed in close proximity, their eigenmodes hybridize and the dispersion splits into two branches with different momenta and field symmetry, providing a powerful platform for dispersion manipulation. We experimentally demonstrate the polaritonic mode splitting in α-MoO3 within a heterostructure with hexagonal boron nitride (hBN) employed as a spacer, probed by a scattering-type scanning near-field optical microscope. Furthermore, we propose a design framework for active and mode-selective tailoring of the polaritonic dispersion in the heterostructure incorporating graphene, achieved through tuning its Fermi energy. Our work experimentally demonstrates the feasibility of phonon-polariton mode splitting in the RB-I and suggests a new platform for dispersion engineering of hyperbolic phonon-polaritons in general.

</details>
